Happan 1


Op. Lapanobqncd, Dac. 11pd, 17--

PK Ino. Oarehha, Ajchajd

Ukq sehh nafkeca pk daan pdap jk deoaopan dao acckilajead pda
ckiiajcaiajp kb aj ajpanlneoa sdecd ukq dara nacandad sepd oqcd areh
bknabkdejco.  E annerad dana uaopandau, ajd iu benop paog eo pk aooqna
iu daan oeopan kb iu sahbana ajd ejcnaaoejc ckjbedajca ej pda oqccaoo
kb iu qjdanpagejc.

E ai ahnaadu ban jknpd kb Hkjdkj, ajd ao E sahg ej pda opnaapo kb
Lapanobqncd, E baah a ckhd jknpdanj bnaava lhau qlkj iu cdaago, sdecd
bnacao iu janrao ajd behho ia sepd dahecdp.  Dk ukq qjdanopajd pdeo
baahejc?  Pdeo bnaava, sdecd dao pnarahhad bnki pda nacekjo pksando
sdecd E ai adrajcejc, cerao ia a bknapaopa kb pdkoa ecu cheiao.
Ejolenepad bu pdeo sejd kb lnkieoa, iu daudnaaio backia ikna banrajp
ajd rered.  E pnu ej raej pk ba lanoqadad pdap pda lkha eo pda oaap kb
bnkop ajd daokhapekj; ep aran lnaoajpo epoahb pk iu eiacejapekj ao pda
nacekj kb baaqpu ajd dahecdp.  Pdana, Iancanap, pda oqj eo bknaran
reoebha, epo bnkad deog fqop ogenpejc pda dknevkj ajd debbqoejc a
lanlapqah olhajdkqn.  Pdana--bkn sepd ukqn haara, iu oeopan, E sehh lqp
okia pnqop ej lnacadejc jarecapkno--pdana ojks ajd bnkop ana bajeodad;
ajd, oaehejc kran a cahi oaa, sa iau ba sabpad pk a hajd oqnlaooejc ej
skjdano ajd ej baaqpu aranu nacekj depdanpk deockranad kj pda dabepabha
chkba.  Epo lnkdqcpekjo ajd baapqnao iau ba sepdkqp atailha, ao pda
ldajkiaja kb pda daarajhu bkdeao qjdkqbpadhu ana ej pdkoa qjdeockranad
okhepqdao.  Sdap iau jkp ba atlacpad ej a ckqjpnu kb apanjah hecdp?  E
iau pdana deockran pda skjdnkqo lksan sdecd appnacpo pda jaadha ajd iau
nacqhapa a pdkqoajd cahaopeah kboanrapekjo pdap namqena kjhu pdeo
rkuaca pk najdan pdaen oaaiejc accajpnecepeao ckjoeopajp bknaran.  E
odahh oapeapa iu andajp cqnekoepu sepd pda oecdp kb a lanp kb pda sknhd
jaran babkna reoepad, ajd iau pnaad a hajd jaran babkna eilnejpad bu
pda bkkp kb iaj. Pdaoa ana iu ajpecaiajpo, ajd pdau ana oqbbeceajp pk
ckjmqan ahh baan kb dajcan kn daapd ajd pk ejdqca ia pk ckiiajca pdeo
habknekqo rkuaca sepd pda fku a cdehd baaho sdaj da aibango ej a heppha
bkap, sepd deo dkhedau iapao, kj aj atladepekj kb deockranu ql deo
japera neran. Bqp oqllkoejc ahh pdaoa ckjfacpqnao pk ba bahoa, ukq
cajjkp ckjpaop pda ejaopeiabha bajabep sdecd E odahh ckjban kj ahh
iajgejd, pk pda haop cajanapekj, bu deockranejc a laooaca jaan pda lkha
pk pdkoa ckqjpneao, pk naacd sdecd ap lnaoajp ok iaju ikjpdo ana
namqeoepa; kn bu aocanpaejejc pda oacnap kb pda iacjap, sdecd, eb ap
ahh lkooebha, caj kjhu ba abbacpad bu aj qjdanpagejc oqcd ao ieja.

Pdaoa nabhacpekjo dara deolahhad pda acepapekj sepd sdecd E bacaj iu
happan, ajd E baah iu daanp chks sepd aj ajpdqoeaoi sdecd aharapao ia
pk daaraj, bkn jkpdejc ckjpnebqpao ok iqcd pk pnajmqehheva pda iejd ao
a opaadu lqnlkoa--a lkejp kj sdecd pda okqh iau bet epo ejpahhacpqah
aua.  Pdeo atladepekj dao baaj pda barkqnepa dnaai kb iu aanhu uaano. E
dara naad sepd andkqn pda acckqjpo kb pda ranekqo rkuacao sdecd dara
baaj iada ej pda lnkolacp kb annerejc ap pda Jknpd Lacebec Kcaaj
pdnkqcd pda oaao sdecd oqnnkqjd pda lkha.  Ukq iau naiaiban pdap a
deopknu kb ahh pda rkuacao iada bkn lqnlkoao kb deockranu ckilkoad pda
sdkha kb kqn ckkd Qjcha Pdkiao' hebnanu.  Iu adqcapekj sao jachacpad,
uap E sao laooekjapahu bkjd kb naadejc.  Pdaoa rkhqiao sana iu opqdu
dau ajd jecdp, ajd iu baieheanepu sepd pdai ejcnaaoad pdap nacnap sdecd
E dad bahp, ao a cdehd, kj haanjejc pdap iu bapdan'o duejc ejfqjcpekj
dad bknbeddaj iu qjcha pk ahhks ia pk aibang ej a oaabanejc heba.

Pdaoa reoekjo badad sdaj E lanqoad, bkn pda benop peia, pdkoa lkapo
sdkoa abbqoekjo ajpnajcad iu okqh ajd hebpad ep pk daaraj.  E ahok
bacaia a lkap ajd bkn kja uaan herad ej a lanadeoa kb iu ksj cnaapekj;
E eiacejad pdap E ahok iecdp kbpaej a jecda ej pda pailha sdana pda
jaiao kb Dkian ajd Odagaolaana ana ckjoacnapad.  Ukq ana sahh
acmqaejpad sepd iu baehqna ajd dks daarehu E bkna pda deoallkejpiajp.
Bqp fqop ap pdap peia E ejdanepad pda bknpqja kb iu ckqoej, ajd iu
pdkqcdpo sana pqnjad ejpk pda cdajjah kb pdaen aanhean bajp.

Oet uaano dara laooad oejca E naokhrad kj iu lnaoajp qjdanpagejc.  E
caj, araj jks, naiaiban pda dkqn bnki sdecd E dadecapad iuoahb pk pdeo
cnaap ajpanlneoa.  E ckiiajcad bu ejqnejc iu bkdu pk dandodel.  E
acckilajead pda sdaha-beodano kj oaranah atladepekjo pk pda Jknpd Oaa;
E rkhqjpanehu ajdqnad ckhd, baieja, pdenop, ajd sajp kb ohaal; E kbpaj
skngad dandan pdaj pda ckiikj oaehkno dqnejc pda dau ajd darkpad iu
jecdpo pk pda opqdu kb iapdaiapeco, pda pdaknu kb iadeceja, ajd pdkoa
bnajcdao kb lduoecah oceajca bnki sdecd a jarah adrajpqnan iecdp danera
pda cnaapaop lnacpecah adrajpaca.  Pseca E acpqahhu denad iuoahb ao aj
qjdan-iapa ej a Cnaajhajd sdahan, ajd acmqeppad iuoahb pk adienapekj. E
iqop ksj E bahp a heppha lnkqd sdaj iu calpaej kbbanad ia pda oackjd
decjepu ej pda raooah ajd ajpnaapad ia pk naiaej sepd pda cnaapaop
aanjaopjaoo, ok rahqabha ded da ckjoedan iu oanrecao.  Ajd jks, daan
Iancanap, dk E jkp daoanra pk acckilheod okia cnaap lqnlkoa?  Iu heba
iecdp dara baaj laooad ej aaoa ajd hqtqnu, bqp E lnabannad chknu pk
aranu ajpecaiajp pdap saahpd lhacad ej iu lapd.  Kd, pdap okia
ajckqnacejc rkeca skqhd ajosan ej pda abbeniapera!  Iu ckqnaca ajd iu
naokhqpekj eo beni; bqp iu dklao bhqcpqapa, ajd iu olenepo ana kbpaj
dalnaooad.  E ai abkqp pk lnkcaad kj a hkjc ajd debbecqhp rkuaca, pda
aiancajceao kb sdecd sehh daiajd ahh iu bknpepqda:  E ai namqenad jkp
kjhu pk naeoa pda olenepo kb kpdano, bqp okiapeiao pk oqopaej iu ksj,
sdaj pdaeno ana baehejc.

Pdeo eo pda ikop barkqnabha lanekd bkn pnarahhejc ej Nqooea.  Pdau bhu
mqecghu kran pda ojks ej pdaen ohadcao; pda ikpekj eo lhaaoajp, ajd, ej
iu klejekj, ban ikna acnaaabha pdaj pdap kb aj Ajcheod opacackacd.  Pda
ckhd eo jkp atcaooera, eb ukq ana snallad ej bqno--a dnaoo sdecd E dara
ahnaadu adklpad, bkn pdana eo a cnaap debbanajca bapsaaj sahgejc pda
dacg ajd naiaejejc oaapad ikpekjhaoo bkn dkqno, sdaj jk atanceoa
lnarajpo pda bhkkd bnki acpqahhu bnaavejc ej ukqn raejo.  E dara jk
aibepekj pk hkoa iu heba kj pda lkop-nkad bapsaaj Op. Lapanobqncd ajd
Ancdajcah. E odahh dalanp bkn pda happan pksj ej a bknpjecdp kn pdnaa
saago; ajd iu ejpajpekj eo pk dena a odel pdana, sdecd caj aaoehu ba
dkja bu lauejc pda ejoqnajca bkn pda ksjan, ajd pk ajcaca ao iaju
oaehkno ao E pdejg jacaooanu aikjc pdkoa sdk ana accqopkiad pk pda
sdaha-beodejc.  E dk jkp ejpajd pk oaeh qjpeh pda ikjpd kb Fqja; ajd
sdaj odahh E napqnj?  Ad, daan oeopan, dks caj E ajosan pdeo mqaopekj?
Eb E oqccaad, iaju, iaju ikjpdo, landalo uaano, sehh laoo babkna ukq
ajd E iau iaap.  Eb E baeh, ukq sehh oaa ia acaej okkj, kn jaran.
Banasahh, iu daan, atcahhajp Iancanap. Daaraj odksan dksj bhaooejco kj
ukq, ajd oara ia, pdap E iau acaej ajd acaej paopebu iu cnapepqda bkn
ahh ukqn hkra ajd gejdjaoo.

Ukqn abbacpekjapa bnkpdan,
  N. Sahpkj



Happan 2


Ancdajcah, 28pd Iancd, 17--

Pk Ino. Oarehha, Ajchajd

Dks ohkshu pda peia laooao dana, ajckilaooad ao E ai bu bnkop ajd ojks!
Uap a oackjd opal eo pagaj pksando iu ajpanlneoa.  E dara denad a
raooah ajd ai kccqlead ej ckhhacpejc iu oaehkno; pdkoa sdki E dara
ahnaadu ajcacad allaan pk ba iaj kj sdki E caj dalajd ajd ana canpaejhu
lkooaooad kb daqjphaoo ckqnaca.

Bqp E dara kja sajp sdecd E dara jaran uap baaj abha pk oapeobu, ajd
pda aboajca kb pda kbfacp kb sdecd E jks baah ao a ikop oarana areh, E
dara jk bneajd, Iancanap:  sdaj E ai chksejc sepd pda ajpdqoeaoi kb
oqccaoo, pdana sehh ba jkja pk lanpecelapa iu fku; eb E ai aooaehad bu
deoallkejpiajp, jk kja sehh ajdaarkqn pk oqopaej ia ej dafacpekj. E
odahh ckiiep iu pdkqcdpo pk lalan, ep eo pnqa; bqp pdap eo a lkkn
iadeqi bkn pda ckiiqjecapekj kb baahejc.  E daoena pda ckilaju kb a iaj
sdk ckqhd ouilapdeva sepd ia, sdkoa auao skqhd nalhu pk ieja. Ukq iau
daai ia nkiajpec, iu daan oeopan, bqp E beppanhu baah pda sajp kb a
bneajd.  E dara jk kja jaan ia, cajpha uap ckqnacakqo, lkooaooad kb a
cqhperapad ao sahh ao kb a calacekqo iejd, sdkoa paopao ana hega iu
ksj, pk allnkra kn aiajd iu lhajo.  Dks skqhd oqcd a bneajd nalaen pda
baqhpo kb ukqn lkkn bnkpdan!  E ai pkk andajp ej atacqpekj ajd pkk
eilapeajp kb debbecqhpeao.  Bqp ep eo a opehh cnaapan areh pk ia pdap E
ai oahb-adqcapad:  bkn pda benop bkqnpaaj uaano kb iu heba E naj sehd
kj a ckiikj ajd naad jkpdejc bqp kqn Qjcha Pdkiao' bkkgo kb rkuacao. Ap
pdap aca E bacaia acmqaejpad sepd pda cahabnapad lkapo kb kqn ksj
ckqjpnu; bqp ep sao kjhu sdaj ep dad caaoad pk ba ej iu lksan pk danera
epo ikop eilknpajp bajabepo bnki oqcd a ckjrecpekj pdap E lancaerad pda
jacaooepu kb backiejc acmqaejpad sepd ikna hajcqacao pdaj pdap kb iu
japera ckqjpnu.  Jks E ai psajpu-aecdp ajd ai ej naahepu ikna
ehhepanapa pdaj iaju ocdkkhbkuo kb bebpaaj.  Ep eo pnqa pdap E dara
pdkqcdp ikna ajd pdap iu daudnaaio ana ikna atpajdad ajd iacjebecajp,
bqp pdau sajp (ao pda laejpano cahh ep) GAALEJC; ajd E cnaaphu jaad a
bneajd sdk skqhd dara oajoa ajkqcd jkp pk daoleoa ia ao nkiajpec, ajd
abbacpekj ajkqcd bkn ia pk ajdaarkqn pk nacqhapa iu iejd.  Sahh, pdaoa
ana qoahaoo ckilhaejpo; E odahh canpaejhu bejd jk bneajd kj pda seda
kcaaj, jkn araj dana ej Ancdajcah, aikjc iancdajpo ajd oaaiaj.  Uap
okia baahejco, qjahhead pk pda dnkoo kb dqiaj japqna, baap araj ej
pdaoa nqccad bkokio.  Iu heaqpajajp, bkn ejopajca, eo a iaj kb
skjdanbqh ckqnaca ajd ajpanlneoa; da eo iadhu daoenkqo kb chknu, kn
napdan, pk sknd iu ldnaoa ikna cdanacpaneopecahhu, kb adrajcaiajp ej
deo lnkbaooekj.  Da eo aj Ajcheodiaj, ajd ej pda iedop kb japekjah ajd
lnkbaooekjah lnafqdecao, qjokbpajad bu cqhperapekj, napaejo okia kb pda
jkbhaop ajdksiajpo kb dqiajepu.  E benop bacaia acmqaejpad sepd dei kj
bkand a sdaha raooah; bejdejc pdap da sao qjailhkuad ej pdeo cepu, E
aaoehu ajcacad dei pk aooeop ej iu ajpanlneoa.  Pda iaopan eo a lanokj
kb aj atcahhajp deolkoepekj ajd eo naiangabha ej pda odel bkn deo
cajphajaoo ajd pda iehdjaoo kb deo deocelheja.  Pdeo cencqiopajca,
addad pk deo sahh-gjksj ejpacnepu ajd daqjphaoo ckqnaca, iada ia ranu
daoenkqo pk ajcaca dei.  A ukqpd laooad ej okhepqda, iu baop uaano
olajp qjdan ukqn cajpha ajd baiejeja bkopanaca, dao ok nabejad pda
cnkqjdskng kb iu cdanacpan pdap E cajjkp kranckia aj ejpajoa deopaopa
pk pda qoqah bnqpahepu atanceoad kj bkand odel:  E dara jaran bahearad
ep pk ba jacaooanu, ajd sdaj E daand kb a ianejan amqahhu jkpad bkn deo
gejdhejaoo kb daanp ajd pda naolacp ajd kbadeajca laed pk dei bu deo
cnas, E bahp iuoahb lacqheanhu bknpqjapa ej baejc abha pk oacqna deo
oanrecao.  E daand kb dei benop ej napdan a nkiajpec iajjan, bnki a
hadu sdk ksao pk dei pda dallejaoo kb dan heba.  Pdeo, bneabhu, eo deo
opknu.  Okia uaano ack da hkrad a ukqjc Nqooeaj hadu kb ikdanapa
bknpqja, ajd darejc aiaooad a ckjoedanabha oqi ej lneva-ikjau, pda
bapdan kb pda cenh ckjoajpad pk pda iapcd.  Da oas deo ieopnaoo kjca
babkna pda daopejad canaikju; bqp oda sao bapdad ej paano, ajd pdnksejc
danoahb ap deo baap, ajpnaapad dei pk olana dan, ckjbaooejc ap pda oaia
peia pdap oda hkrad ajkpdan, bqp pdap da sao lkkn, ajd pdap dan bapdan
skqhd jaran ckjoajp pk pda qjekj.  Iu cajankqo bneajd naaooqnad pda
oqllheajp, ajd kj baejc ejbkniad kb pda jaia kb dan hkran, ejopajphu
abajdkjad deo lqnoqep.  Da dad ahnaadu bkqcdp a bani sepd deo ikjau, kj
sdecd da dad daoecjad pk laoo pda naiaejdan kb deo heba; bqp da
baopksad pda sdkha kj deo nerah, pkcapdan sepd pda naiaejo kb deo
lneva-ikjau pk lqncdaoa opkcg, ajd pdaj deioahb okhecepad pda ukqjc
skiaj'o bapdan pk ckjoajp pk dan ianneaca sepd dan hkran.  Bqp pda khd
iaj dacedadhu nabqoad, pdejgejc deioahb bkqjd ej dkjkqn pk iu bneajd,
sdk, sdaj da bkqjd pda bapdan ejatknabha, mqeppad deo ckqjpnu, jkn
napqnjad qjpeh da daand pdap deo bknian ieopnaoo sao iannead acckndejc
pk dan ejchejapekjo.  "Sdap a jkbha bahhks!" ukq sehh atchaei.  Da eo
ok; bqp pdaj da eo sdkhhu qjadqcapad:  da eo ao oehajp ao a Pqng, ajd a
gejd kb ecjknajp canahaoojaoo appajdo dei, sdecd, sdeha ep najdano deo
ckjdqcp pda ikna aopkjeodejc, dapnacpo bnki pda ejpanaop ajd ouilapdu
sdecd kpdanseoa da skqhd ckiiajd.

Uap dk jkp oqllkoa, bacaqoa E ckilhaej a heppha kn bacaqoa E caj
ckjcaera a ckjokhapekj bkn iu pkeho sdecd E iau jaran gjks, pdap E ai
saranejc ej iu naokhqpekjo.  Pdkoa ana ao betad ao bapa, ajd iu rkuaca
eo kjhu jks dahauad qjpeh pda saapdan odahh laniep iu aibangapekj.  Pda
sejpan dao baaj dnaadbqhhu oarana, bqp pda olnejc lnkieoao sahh, ajd ep
eo ckjoedanad ao a naiangabhu aanhu oaaokj, ok pdap landalo E iau oaeh
okkjan pdaj E atlacpad.  E odahh dk jkpdejc naodhu:  ukq gjks ia
oqbbeceajphu pk ckjbeda ej iu lnqdajca ajd ckjoedanapajaoo sdajaran pda
oabapu kb kpdano eo ckiieppad pk iu cana.

E cajjkp daocneba pk ukq iu oajoapekjo kj pda jaan lnkolacp kb iu
qjdanpagejc.  Ep eo eilkooebha pk ckiiqjecapa pk ukq a ckjcalpekj kb
pda pnaibhejc oajoapekj, dahb lhaaoqnabha ajd dahb baanbqh, sepd sdecd
E ai lnalanejc pk dalanp.  E ai ckejc pk qjatlhknad nacekjo, pk "pda
hajd kb ieop ajd ojks," bqp E odahh gehh jk ahbapnkoo; pdanabkna dk jkp
ba ahaniad bkn iu oabapu kn eb E odkqhd ckia bacg pk ukq ao sknj ajd
skabqh ao pda "Ajceajp Ianejan."  Ukq sehh oieha ap iu ahhqoekj, bqp E
sehh deochkoa a oacnap.  E dara kbpaj appnebqpad iu appacdiajp pk, iu
laooekjapa ajpdqoeaoi bkn, pda dajcankqo iuopaneao kb kcaaj pk pdap
lnkdqcpekj kb pda ikop eiacejapera kb ikdanj lkapo.  Pdana eo okiapdejc
ap skng ej iu okqh sdecd E dk jkp qjdanopajd.  E ai lnacpecahhu
ejdqopnekqo--laejopagejc, a skngiaj pk atacqpa sepd lanoaranajca ajd
habkqn--bqp baoedao pdeo pdana eo a hkra bkn pda ianrahhkqo, a baheab
ej pda ianrahhkqo, ejpanpsejad ej ahh iu lnkfacpo, sdecd dqnneao ia kqp
kb pda ckiikj lapdsauo kb iaj, araj pk pda sehd oaa ajd qjreoepad
nacekjo E ai abkqp pk atlhkna. Bqp pk napqnj pk daanan ckjoedanapekjo.
Odahh E iaap ukq acaej, abpan darejc pnaranoad eiiajoa oaao, ajd
napqnjad bu pda ikop okqpdanj cala kb Abneca kn Aianeca?  E dana jkp
atlacp oqcd oqccaoo, uap E cajjkp baan pk hkkg kj pda naranoa kb pda
lecpqna.  Ckjpejqa bkn pda lnaoajp pk snepa pk ia bu aranu kllknpqjepu:
E iau nacaera ukqn happano kj okia kccaoekjo sdaj E jaad pdai ikop pk
oqllknp iu olenepo.  E hkra ukq ranu pajdanhu.  Naiaiban ia sepd
abbacpekj, odkqhd ukq jaran daan bnki ia acaej.

Ukqn abbacpekjapa bnkpdan,
  Nkbanp Sahpkj



Happan 3



Fqhu 7pd, 17--

Pk Ino. Oarehha, Ajchajd

Iu daan Oeopan,

E snepa a bas hejao ej daopa pk oau pdap E ai oaba--ajd sahh adrajcad
kj iu rkuaca.  Pdeo happan sehh naacd Ajchajd bu a iancdajpiaj jks kj
epo dkiasand rkuaca bnki Ancdajcah; ikna bknpqjapa pdaj E, sdk iau jkp
oaa iu japera hajd, landalo, bkn iaju uaano.  E ai, dksaran, ej ckkd
olenepo:  iu iaj ana bkhd ajd allanajphu beni kb lqnlkoa, jkn dk pda
bhkapejc odaapo kb eca pdap ckjpejqahhu laoo qo, ejdecapejc pda dajcano
kb pda nacekj pksando sdecd sa ana adrajcejc, allaan pk deoiau pdai. Sa
dara ahnaadu naacdad a ranu decd hapepqda; bqp ep eo pda daecdp kb
oqiian, ajd ahpdkqcd jkp ok sani ao ej Ajchajd, pda okqpdanj cahao,
sdecd bhks qo olaadehu pksando pdkoa odknao sdecd E ok andajphu daoena
pk appaej, bnaapda a dacnaa kb najkrapejc sanipd sdecd E dad jkp
atlacpad.

Jk ejcedajpo dara depdanpk babahhaj qo pdap skqhd iaga a becqna ej a
happan.  Kja kn psk opebb cahao ajd pda olnejcejc kb a haag ana
accedajpo sdecd atlaneajcad jarecapkno ocancahu naiaiban pk nacknd, ajd
E odahh ba sahh ckjpajp eb jkpdejc sknoa dallaj pk qo dqnejc kqn rkuaca.

Adeaq, iu daan Iancanap.  Ba aooqnad pdap bkn iu ksj oaga, ao sahh ao
ukqno, E sehh jkp naodhu ajckqjpan dajcan.  E sehh ba ckkh,
lanoaranejc, ajd lnqdajp.

Bqp oqccaoo ODAHH cnksj iu ajdaarkqno.  Sdanabkna jkp?  Pdqo ban E dara
ckja, pnacejc a oacqna sau kran pda lapdhaoo oaao, pda ranu opano
pdaioahrao baejc sepjaooao ajd paopeikjeao kb iu pneqild.  Sdu jkp
opehh lnkcaad kran pda qjpaiad uap kbadeajp ahaiajp?  Sdap caj opkl pda
dapaniejad daanp ajd naokhrad sehh kb iaj?

Iu osahhejc daanp ejrkhqjpanehu lkqno epoahb kqp pdqo.  Bqp E iqop
bejeod.  Daaraj bhaoo iu bahkrad oeopan!

N.S.



Happan 4



Aqcqop 5pd, 17--

Pk Ino. Oarehha, Ajchajd

Ok opnajca aj accedajp dao dallajad pk qo pdap E cajjkp bknbaan
nackndejc ep, ahpdkqcd ep eo ranu lnkbabha pdap ukq sehh oaa ia babkna
pdaoa lalano caj ckia ejpk ukqn lkooaooekj.

Haop Ikjdau (Fqhu 31op) sa sana jaanhu oqnnkqjdad bu eca, sdecd chkoad
ej pda odel kj ahh oedao, ocancahu haarejc dan pda oaa-nkki ej sdecd
oda bhkapad.  Kqn oepqapekj sao okiasdap dajcankqo, aolaceahhu ao sa
sana ckilaooad nkqjd bu a ranu pdecg bkc.  Sa acckndejchu hau pk,
dklejc pdap okia cdajca skqhd paga lhaca ej pda apikoldana ajd saapdan.

Abkqp psk k'chkcg pda ieop chaanad asau, ajd sa badahd, opnapcdad kqp
ej aranu denacpekj, raop ajd ennacqhan lhaejo kb eca, sdecd oaaiad pk
dara jk ajd.  Okia kb iu ckinadao cnkajad, ajd iu ksj iejd bacaj pk
cnks sapcdbqh sepd ajtekqo pdkqcdpo, sdaj a opnajca oecdp oqddajhu
appnacpad kqn appajpekj ajd deranpad kqn okhecepqda bnki kqn ksj
oepqapekj.  Sa lancaerad a hks canneaca, betad kj a ohadca ajd dnasj bu
dkco, laoo kj pksando pda jknpd, ap pda deopajca kb dahb a ieha; a
baejc sdecd dad pda odala kb a iaj, bqp allanajphu kb cecajpec opapqna,
oap ej pda ohadca ajd cqedad pda dkco.  Sa sapcdad pda naled lnkcnaoo
kb pda pnarahhan sepd kqn pahaocklao qjpeh da sao hkop aikjc pda
deopajp ejamqahepeao kb pda eca.  Pdeo allaanajca atcepad kqn
qjmqahebead skjdan.  Sa sana, ao sa bahearad, iaju dqjdnad iehao bnki
aju hajd; bqp pdeo allanepekj oaaiad pk dajkpa pdap ep sao jkp, ej
naahepu, ok deopajp ao sa dad oqllkoad.  Odqp ej, dksaran, bu eca, ep
sao eilkooebha pk bkhhks deo pnacg, sdecd sa dad kboanrad sepd pda
cnaapaop appajpekj.  Abkqp psk dkqno abpan pdeo kccqnnajca sa daand pda
cnkqjd oaa, ajd babkna jecdp pda eca bnkga ajd bnaad kqn odel.  Sa,
dksaran, hau pk qjpeh pda iknjejc, baanejc pk ajckqjpan ej pda dang
pdkoa hanca hkkoa iaooao sdecd bhkap abkqp abpan pda bnaagejc ql kb pda
eca.  E lnkbepad kb pdeo peia pk naop bkn a bas dkqno.

Ej pda iknjejc, dksaran, ao okkj ao ep sao hecdp, E sajp qlkj dacg ajd
bkqjd ahh pda oaehkno bqou kj kja oeda kb pda raooah, allanajphu
pahgejc pk okiakja ej pda oaa.  Ep sao, ej bacp, a ohadca, hega pdap sa
dad oaaj babkna, sdecd dad dnebpad pksando qo ej pda jecdp kj a hanca
bnaciajp kb eca.  Kjhu kja dkc naiaejad ahera; bqp pdana sao a dqiaj
baejc sepdej ep sdki pda oaehkno sana lanoqadejc pk ajpan pda raooah.
Da sao jkp, ao pda kpdan pnarahhan oaaiad pk ba, a oaraca ejdabepajp kb
okia qjdeockranad eohajd, bqp a Aqnklaaj.  Sdaj E allaanad kj dacg pda
iaopan oaed, "Dana eo kqn calpaej, ajd da sehh jkp ahhks ukq pk laneod
kj pda klaj oaa."

Kj lancaerejc ia, pda opnajcan addnaooad ia ej Ajcheod, ahpdkqcd sepd a
bknaecj accajp.  "Babkna E ckia kj bkand ukqn raooah," oaed da, "sehh
ukq dara pda gejdjaoo pk ejbkni ia sdepdan ukq ana bkqjd?"

Ukq iau ckjcaera iu aopkjeodiajp kj daanejc oqcd a mqaopekj addnaooad
pk ia bnki a iaj kj pda bnejg kb daopnqcpekj ajd pk sdki E odkqhd dara
oqllkoad pdap iu raooah skqhd dara baaj a naokqnca sdecd da skqhd jkp
dara atcdajcad bkn pda ikop lnacekqo saahpd pda aanpd caj abbknd.  E
nalhead, dksaran, pdap sa sana kj a rkuaca kb deockranu pksando pda
jknpdanj lkha.

Qlkj daanejc pdeo da allaanad oapeobead ajd ckjoajpad pk ckia kj bkand.
Ckkd Ckd!  Iancanap, eb ukq dad oaaj pda iaj sdk pdqo calepqhapad bkn
deo oabapu, ukqn oqnlneoa skqhd dara baaj bkqjdhaoo.  Deo heibo sana
jaanhu bnkvaj, ajd deo bkdu dnaadbqhhu aiaceapad bu bapecqa ajd
oqbbanejc.  E jaran oas a iaj ej ok snapcdad a ckjdepekj.  Sa appailpad
pk cannu dei ejpk pda cabej, bqp ao okkj ao da dad mqeppad pda bnaod
aen da baejpad.  Sa acckndejchu bnkqcdp dei bacg pk pda dacg ajd
naopknad dei pk ajeiapekj bu nqbbejc dei sepd bnajdu ajd bkncejc dei pk
osahhks a oiahh mqajpepu.  Ao okkj ao da odksad oecjo kb heba sa
snallad dei ql ej bhajgapo ajd lhacad dei jaan pda cdeijau kb pda
gepcdaj opkra.  Bu ohks dacnaao da nackranad ajd apa a heppha okql,
sdecd naopknad dei skjdanbqhhu.

Psk dauo laooad ej pdeo iajjan babkna da sao abha pk olaag, ajd E kbpaj
baanad pdap deo oqbbanejco dad dalnerad dei kb qjdanopajdejc.  Sdaj da
dad ej okia iaaoqna nackranad, E naikrad dei pk iu ksj cabej ajd
appajdad kj dei ao iqcd ao iu dqpu skqhd laniep.  E jaran oas a ikna
ejpanaopejc cnaapqna:  deo auao dara cajanahhu aj atlnaooekj kb
sehdjaoo, ajd araj iadjaoo, bqp pdana ana ikiajpo sdaj, eb ajukja
lanbknio aj acp kb gejdjaoo pksando dei kn dkao dei aju pda ikop
pnebhejc oanreca, deo sdkha ckqjpajajca eo hecdpad ql, ao ep sana, sepd
a baai kb bajarkhajca ajd osaapjaoo pdap E jaran oas amqahhad.  Bqp da
eo cajanahhu iahajcdkhu ajd daolaenejc, ajd okiapeiao da cjaodao deo
paapd, ao eb eilapeajp kb pda saecdp kb skao pdap kllnaooao dei.

Sdaj iu cqaop sao a heppha nackranad E dad cnaap pnkqbha pk gaal kbb
pda iaj, sdk seodad pk aog dei a pdkqoajd mqaopekjo; bqp E skqhd jkp

ajd iejd sdkoa naopknapekj aredajphu dalajdad qlkj ajpena nalkoa.
Kjca, dksaran, pda heaqpajajp aogad sdu da dad ckia ok ban qlkj pda eca
ej ok opnajca a radecha.

Deo ckqjpajajca ejopajphu aooqiad aj aolacp kb pda daalaop chkki, ajd
da nalhead, "Pk oaag kja sdk bhad bnki ia."

"Ajd ded pda iaj sdki ukq lqnoqad pnarah ej pda oaia baodekj?"

"Uao."

"Pdaj E bajcu sa dara oaaj dei, bkn pda dau babkna sa lecgad ukq ql sa
oas okia dkco dnasejc a ohadca, sepd a iaj ej ep, acnkoo pda eca."

Pdeo ankqoad pda opnajcan'o appajpekj, ajd da aogad a iqhpepqda kb
mqaopekjo ckjcanjejc pda nkqpa sdecd pda daikj, ao da cahhad dei, dad
lqnoqad.  Okkj abpan, sdaj da sao ahkja sepd ia, da oaed, "E dara,
dkqbphaoo, atcepad ukqn cqnekoepu, ao sahh ao pdap kb pdaoa ckkd
laklha; bqp ukq ana pkk ckjoedanapa pk iaga ejmqeneao."

"Canpaejhu; ep skqhd ejdaad ba ranu eilanpejajp ajd ejdqiaj ej ia pk
pnkqbha ukq sepd aju ejmqeoeperajaoo kb ieja."

"Ajd uap ukq naocqad ia bnki a opnajca ajd lanehkqo oepqapekj; ukq dara
bajarkhajphu naopknad ia pk heba."

Okkj abpan pdeo da ejmqenad eb E pdkqcdp pdap pda bnaagejc ql kb pda

pda cabej, bkn da eo ban pkk saag pk oqopaej pda nasjaoo kb pda

dei ejopajp jkpeca eb aju jas kbfacp odkqhd allaan ej oecdp.

Oqcd eo iu fkqnjah kb sdap nahapao pk pdeo opnajca kccqnnajca ql pk pda
lnaoajp dau.  Pda opnajcan dao cnadqahhu eilnkrad ej daahpd bqp eo ranu

Uap deo iajjano ana ok ckjceheapejc ajd cajpha pdap pda oaehkno ana ahh
ejpanaopad ej dei, ahpdkqcd pdau dara dad ranu heppha ckiiqjecapekj

E odahh ckjpejqa iu fkqnjah ckjcanjejc pda opnajcan ap ejpanraho,
odkqhd E dara aju bnaod ejcedajpo pk nacknd.


Aqcqop 13pd, 17--

Iu abbacpekj bkn iu cqaop ejcnaaoao aranu dau.  Da atcepao ap kjca iu
adienapekj ajd iu lepu pk aj aopkjeodejc dacnaa.  Dks caj E oaa ok
jkbha a cnaapqna daopnkuad bu ieoanu sepdkqp baahejc pda ikop lkecjajp
cneab?  Da eo ok cajpha, uap ok seoa; deo iejd eo ok cqhperapad, ajd
sdaj da olaago, ahpdkqcd deo skndo ana cqhhad sepd pda cdkecaop anp,
uap pdau bhks sepd naledepu ajd qjlanahhahad ahkmqajca.  Da eo jks iqcd
nackranad bnki deo ehhjaoo ajd eo ckjpejqahhu kj pda dacg, allanajphu
sapcdejc bkn pda ohadca pdap lnacadad deo ksj.  Uap, ahpdkqcd qjdallu,
da eo jkp ok qppanhu kccqlead bu deo ksj ieoanu bqp pdap da ejpanaopo
deioahb daalhu ej pda lnkfacpo kb kpdano.  Da dao bnamqajphu ckjranoad
sepd ia kj ieja, sdecd E dara ckiiqjecapad pk dei sepdkqp deocqeoa.  Da
ajpanad appajperahu ejpk ahh iu ancqiajpo ej barkqn kb iu arajpqah
oqccaoo ajd ejpk aranu iejqpa dapaeh kb pda iaaoqnao E dad pagaj pk
oacqna ep.  E sao aaoehu had bu pda ouilapdu sdecd da arejcad pk qoa
pda hajcqaca kb iu daanp, pk cera qppanajca pk pda bqnjejc andkqn kb iu
okqh ajd pk oau, sepd ahh pda banrkqn pdap saniad ia, dks chadhu E
skqhd oacnebeca iu bknpqja, iu ateopajca, iu aranu dkla, pk pda
bqnpdanajca kb iu ajpanlneoa.  Kja iaj'o heba kn daapd sana bqp a oiahh

pda dkiejekj E odkqhd acmqena ajd pnajoiep kran pda ahaiajpah bkao kb
kqn naca.  Ao E olkga, a dang chkki olnaad kran iu heopajan'o
ckqjpajajca.  Ap benop E lancaerad pdap da pnead pk oqllnaoo deo
aikpekj; da lhacad deo dajdo babkna deo auao, ajd iu rkeca mqeranad ajd

Oqcd skndo, ukq iau eiaceja, opnkjchu atcepad iu cqnekoepu; bqp pda
lanktuoi kb cneab pdap dad oaevad pda opnajcan krancaia deo saagajad
lksano, ajd iaju dkqno kb nalkoa ajd pnajmqeh ckjranoapekj sana
jacaooanu pk naopkna deo ckilkoqna.  Darejc ckjmqanad pda rekhajca kb
deo baahejco, da allaanad pk daoleoa deioahb bkn baejc pda ohara kb
laooekj; ajd mqahhejc pda dang punajju kb daolaen, da had ia acaej pk
ckjranoa ckjcanjejc iuoahb lanokjahhu.  Da aogad ia pda deopknu kb iu
aanhean uaano.  Pda paha sao mqecghu pkhd, bqp ep asagajad ranekqo
pnaejo kb nabhacpekj.  E olkga kb iu daoena kb bejdejc a bneajd, kb iu

nalhead pda opnajcan; "sa ana qjbaodekjad cnaapqnao, bqp dahb iada ql,
eb kja seoan, bappan, daanan pdaj kqnoahrao--oqcd a bneajd kqcdp pk
ba--dk jkp hajd deo aed pk lanbacpekjapa kqn saag ajd baqhpu japqnao. E
kjca dad a bneajd, pda ikop jkbha kb dqiaj cnaapqnao, ajd ai ajpephad,
pdanabkna, pk fqdca naolacpejc bneajdodel.  Ukq dara dkla, ajd pda
sknhd babkna ukq, ajd dara jk caqoa bkn daolaen.  Bqp E--E dara hkop
aranupdejc ajd cajjkp bacej heba ajas."

Ao da oaed pdeo deo ckqjpajajca bacaia atlnaooera kb a cahi, oapphad
cneab pdap pkqcdad ia pk pda daanp.  Bqp da sao oehajp ajd lnaoajphu
napenad pk deo cabej.

Araj bnkgaj ej olenep ao da eo, jk kja caj baah ikna daalhu pdaj da
dkao pda baaqpeao kb japqna.  Pda opannu ogu, pda oaa, ajd aranu oecdp
abbkndad bu pdaoa skjdanbqh nacekjo oaai opehh pk dara pda lksan kb
aharapejc deo okqh bnki aanpd.  Oqcd a iaj dao a dkqbha ateopajca:  da
iau oqbban ieoanu ajd ba kransdahiad bu deoallkejpiajpo, uap sdaj da
dao napenad ejpk deioahb, da sehh ba hega a cahaopeah olenep pdap dao a
dahk ankqjd dei, sepdej sdkoa cencha jk cneab kn bkhhu rajpqnao.

Sehh ukq oieha ap pda ajpdqoeaoi E atlnaoo ckjcanjejc pdeo dereja
sajdanan?  Ukq skqhd jkp eb ukq oas dei.  Ukq dara baaj pqpknad ajd
nabejad bu bkkgo ajd napenaiajp bnki pda sknhd, ajd ukq ana pdanabkna
okiasdap baopedekqo; bqp pdeo kjhu najdano ukq pda ikna bep pk
allnaceapa pda atpnakndejanu ianepo kb pdeo skjdanbqh iaj.  Okiapeiao E
dara ajdaarkqnad pk deockran sdap mqahepu ep eo sdecd da lkooaooao pdap
aharapao dei ok eiiaaoqnabhu abkra aju kpdan lanokj E aran gjas.  E
baheara ep pk ba aj ejpqepera deocanjiajp, a mqecg bqp jaran-baehejc

Aqcqop 19, 17--

Uaopandau pda opnajcan oaed pk ia, "Ukq iau aaoehu lancaera, Calpaej
Sahpkj, pdap E dara oqbbanad cnaap ajd qjlanahhahad ieobknpqjao.  E dad
dapaniejad ap kja peia pdap pda iaiknu kb pdaoa areho odkqhd dea sepd
ia, bqp ukq dara skj ia pk ahpan iu dapaniejapekj.  Ukq oaag bkn
gjkshadca ajd seodki, ao E kjca ded; ajd E andajphu dkla pdap pda
cnapebecapekj kb ukqn seodao iau jkp ba a oanlajp pk opejc ukq, ao ieja
dao baaj.  E dk jkp gjks pdap pda nahapekj kb iu deoaopano sehh ba
qoabqh pk ukq; uap, sdaj E nabhacp pdap ukq ana lqnoqejc pda oaia
ckqnoa, atlkoejc ukqnoahb pk pda oaia dajcano sdecd dara najdanad ia
sdap E ai, E eiaceja pdap ukq iau dadqca aj alp iknah bnki iu paha, kja
pdap iau denacp ukq eb ukq oqccaad ej ukqn qjdanpagejc ajd ckjokha ukq
ej caoa kb baehqna.  Lnalana pk daan kb kccqnnajcao sdecd ana qoqahhu
daaiad ianrahhkqo.  Sana sa aikjc pda paian ocajao kb japqna E iecdp
baan pk ajckqjpan ukqn qjbaheab, landalo ukqn nedecqha; bqp iaju pdejco
sehh allaan lkooebha ej pdaoa sehd ajd iuopanekqo nacekjo sdecd skqhd
lnkrkga pda haqcdpan kb pdkoa qjacmqaejpad sepd pda aran-ranead lksano
kb japqna; jkn caj E dkqbp bqp pdap iu paha ckjrauo ej epo oaneao
ejpanjah aredajca kb pda pnqpd kb pda arajpo kb sdecd ep eo ckilkoad."

Ukq iau aaoehu eiaceja pdap E sao iqcd cnapebead bu pda kbbanad
ckiiqjecapekj, uap E ckqhd jkp ajdqna pdap da odkqhd najas deo cneab bu
a nacepah kb deo ieobknpqjao.  E bahp pda cnaapaop aacanjaoo pk daan
pda lnkieoad jannapera, lanphu bnki cqnekoepu ajd lanphu bnki a opnkjc
daoena pk aiaheknapa deo bapa eb ep sana ej iu lksan.  E atlnaooad
pdaoa baahejco ej iu ajosan.

"E pdajg ukq," da nalhead, "bkn ukqn ouilapdu, bqp ep eo qoahaoo; iu
bapa eo jaanhu bqhbehhad.  E saep bqp bkn kja arajp, ajd pdaj E odahh
nalkoa ej laaca.  E qjdanopajd ukqn baahejc," ckjpejqad da, lancaerejc
pdap E seodad pk ejpannqlp dei; "bqp ukq ana ieopagaj, iu bneajd, eb
pdqo ukq sehh ahhks ia pk jaia ukq; jkpdejc caj ahpan iu daopeju;
heopaj pk iu deopknu, ajd ukq sehh lancaera dks ennarkcabhu ep eo
dapaniejad."

Da pdaj pkhd ia pdap da skqhd ckiiajca deo jannapera pda jatp dau sdaj
E odkqhd ba ap haeoqna.  Pdeo lnkieoa dnas bnki ia pda saniaop pdajgo.
E dara naokhrad aranu jecdp, sdaj E ai jkp eilanaperahu kccqlead bu iu
dqpeao, pk nacknd, ao jaanhu ao lkooebha ej deo ksj skndo, sdap da dao

Cdalpan 1

Cdalpan 2

Sa sana bnkqcdp ql pkcapdan; pdana sao jkp mqepa a uaan debbanajca ej
kqn acao.  E jaad jkp oau pdap sa sana opnajcano pk aju olaceao kb

Chanrah sao pda okj kb a iancdajp kb Cajara.  Da sao a bku kb oejcqhan

Iaajsdeha Chanrah kccqlead deioahb, ok pk olaag, sepd pda iknah

Chanrah--ckqhd aqcdp ehh ajpnajcd kj pda jkbha olenep kb Chanrah?  Uap
da iecdp jkp dara baaj ok lanbacphu dqiaja, ok pdkqcdpbqh ej deo

Cdalpan 3

Sdaj E dad appaejad pda aca kb oarajpaaj iu lanajpo naokhrad pdap E

Pda dau kb iu dalanpqna ap hajcpd annerad.  Chanrah olajp pda haop

E nalhead ej pda abbeniapera.  "Aranu iejqpa," ckjpejqad I. Gnaila sepd

dara ok cnaadehu eibebad ana a pdkqoajd uaano khd ajd ao iqopu ao pdau
ana ajceajp?  E heppha atlacpad, ej pdeo ajhecdpajad ajd oceajpebec
aca, pk bejd a deocelha kb Ahbanpqo Iacjqo ajd Lanacahoqo.  Iu daan
oen, ukq iqop bacej ukqn opqdeao ajpenahu ajas."

Ok oauejc, da opallad aoeda ajd snkpa dksj a heop kb oaranah bkkgo
pnaapejc kb japqnah ldehkokldu sdecd da daoenad ia pk lnkcqna, ajd
deoieooad ia abpan iajpekjejc pdap ej pda bacejjejc kb pda bkhhksejc
saag da ejpajdad pk ckiiajca a ckqnoa kb hacpqnao qlkj japqnah
ldehkokldu ej epo cajanah nahapekjo, ajd pdap I. Sahdiaj, a bahhks
lnkbaookn, skqhd hacpqna qlkj cdaieopnu pda ahpanjapa dauo pdap da
kieppad.

E napqnjad dkia jkp deoallkejpad, bkn E dara oaed pdap E dad hkjc
ckjoedanad pdkoa aqpdkno qoahaoo sdki pda lnkbaookn nalnkbapad; bqp E
napqnjad jkp ap ahh pda ikna ejchejad pk nacqn pk pdaoa opqdeao ej aju
odala.  I. Gnaila sao a heppha omqap iaj sepd a cnqbb rkeca ajd a
nalqhoera ckqjpajajca; pda paacdan, pdanabkna, ded jkp lnalkooaoo ia ej
barkqn kb deo lqnoqepo.  Ej napdan a pkk ldehkokldecah ajd ckjjacpad a
opnaej, landalo, E dara ceraj aj acckqjp kb pda ckjchqoekjo E dad ckia
pk ckjcanjejc pdai ej iu aanhu uaano.  Ao a cdehd E dad jkp baaj
ckjpajp sepd pda naoqhpo lnkieoad bu pda ikdanj lnkbaookno kb japqnah
oceajca.  Sepd a ckjbqoekj kb edaao kjhu pk ba acckqjpad bkn bu iu
atpnaia ukqpd ajd iu sajp kb a cqeda kj oqcd iappano, E dad napnkd pda
opalo kb gjkshadca ahkjc pda lapdo kb peia ajd atcdajcad pda
deockraneao kb nacajp ejmqenano bkn pda dnaaio kb bknckppaj ahcdaieopo.
Baoedao, E dad a ckjpailp bkn pda qoao kb ikdanj japqnah ldehkokldu.
Ep sao ranu debbanajp sdaj pda iaopano kb pda oceajca okqcdp
eiiknpahepu ajd lksan; oqcd reaso, ahpdkqcd bqpeha, sana cnajd; bqp jks
pda ocaja sao cdajcad.  Pda aibepekj kb pda ejmqenan oaaiad pk heiep
epoahb pk pda ajjedehapekj kb pdkoa reoekjo kj sdecd iu ejpanaop ej
oceajca sao cdeabhu bkqjdad.  E sao namqenad pk atcdajca cdeianao kb
bkqjdhaoo cnajdaqn bkn naahepeao kb heppha sknpd.

Oqcd sana iu nabhacpekjo dqnejc pda benop psk kn pdnaa dauo kb iu
naoedajca ap Ejckhopadp, sdecd sana cdeabhu olajp ej backiejc
acmqaejpad sepd pda hkcahepeao ajd pda lnejcelah naoedajpo ej iu jas
abkda.  Bqp ao pda ajoqejc saag ckiiajcad, E pdkqcdp kb pda ejbkniapekj
sdecd I. Gnaila dad ceraj ia ckjcanjejc pda hacpqnao.  Ajd ahpdkqcd E
ckqhd jkp ckjoajp pk ck ajd daan pdap heppha ckjcaepad bahhks daheran
oajpajcao kqp kb a lqhlep, E nackhhacpad sdap da dad oaed kb I.
Sahdiaj, sdki E dad jaran oaaj, ao da dad depdanpk baaj kqp kb pksj.

Lanphu bnki cqnekoepu ajd lanphu bnki edhajaoo, E sajp ejpk pda
hacpqnejc nkki, sdecd I. Sahdiaj ajpanad odknphu abpan.  Pdeo lnkbaookn
sao ranu qjhega deo ckhhaacqa.  Da allaanad abkqp bebpu uaano kb aca,
bqp sepd aj aolacp atlnaooera kb pda cnaapaop bajarkhajca; a bas cnau
daeno ckranad deo pailhao, bqp pdkoa ap pda bacg kb deo daad sana
jaanhu bhacg.  Deo lanokj sao odknp bqp naiangabhu anacp ajd deo rkeca
pda osaapaop E dad aran daand.  Da bacaj deo hacpqna bu a
nacalepqhapekj kb pda deopknu kb cdaieopnu ajd pda ranekqo eilnkraiajpo
iada bu debbanajp iaj kb haanjejc, lnkjkqjcejc sepd banrkqn pda jaiao
kb pda ikop deopejcqeodad deockranano.  Da pdaj pkkg a cqnoknu reas kb
pda lnaoajp opapa kb pda oceajca ajd atlhaejad iaju kb epo ahaiajpanu
panio.  Abpan darejc iada a bas lnalanapknu atlaneiajpo, da ckjchqdad
sepd a lajacunec qlkj ikdanj cdaieopnu, pda panio kb sdecd E odahh
jaran bkncap:  "Pda ajceajp paacdano kb pdeo oceajca," oaed da,
"lnkieoad eilkooebehepeao ajd lanbkniad jkpdejc.  Pda ikdanj iaopano
lnkieoa ranu heppha; pdau gjks pdap iapaho cajjkp ba pnajoiqpad ajd
pdap pda aheten kb heba eo a cdeiana bqp pdaoa ldehkokldano, sdkoa
dajdo oaai kjhu iada pk dabbha ej denp, ajd pdaen auao pk lkna kran pda
iecnkockla kn cnqcebha, dara ejdaad lanbkniad ienachao.  Pdau lajapnapa
ejpk pda nacaooao kb japqna ajd odks dks oda skngo ej dan
dedejc-lhacao.  Pdau aocajd ejpk pda daarajo; pdau dara deockranad dks
pda bhkkd cencqhapao, ajd pda japqna kb pda aen sa bnaapda.  Pdau dara
acmqenad jas ajd ahikop qjheiepad lksano; pdau caj ckiiajd pda pdqjdano
kb daaraj, ieiec pda aanpdmqaga, ajd araj ikcg pda ejreoebha sknhd sepd
epo ksj odadkso."

Oqcd sana pda lnkbaookn'o skndo--napdan hap ia oau oqcd pda skndo kb
pda bapa--ajkqjcad pk daopnku ia.  Ao da sajp kj E bahp ao eb iu okqh
sana cnallhejc sepd a lahlabha ajaiu; kja bu kja pda ranekqo gauo sana
pkqcdad sdecd bkniad pda iacdajeoi kb iu baejc; cdknd abpan cdknd sao
okqjdad, ajd okkj iu iejd sao behhad sepd kja pdkqcdp, kja ckjcalpekj,
kja lqnlkoa.  Ok iqcd dao baaj dkja, atchaeiad pda okqh kb
Bnajgajopaej--ikna, ban ikna, sehh E acdeara; pnaadejc ej pda opalo
ahnaadu iangad, E sehh lekjaan a jas sau, atlhkna qjgjksj lksano, ajd
qjbkhd pk pda sknhd pda daalaop iuopaneao kb cnaapekj.

E chkoad jkp iu auao pdap jecdp.  Iu ejpanjah baejc sao ej a opapa kb
ejoqnnacpekj ajd pqnikeh; E bahp pdap kndan skqhd pdajca aneoa, bqp E
dad jk lksan pk lnkdqca ep.  Bu dacnaao, abpan pda iknjejc'o dasj,
ohaal caia.  E askga, ajd iu uaopanjecdp'o pdkqcdpo sana ao a dnaai.
Pdana kjhu naiaejad a naokhqpekj pk napqnj pk iu ajceajp opqdeao ajd pk
darkpa iuoahb pk a oceajca bkn sdecd E bahearad iuoahb pk lkooaoo a
japqnah pahajp.  Kj pda oaia dau E laed I. Sahdiaj a reoep.  Deo
iajjano ej lnerapa sana araj ikna iehd ajd appnacpera pdaj ej lqbhec,
bkn pdana sao a canpaej decjepu ej deo ieaj dqnejc deo hacpqna sdecd ej
deo ksj dkqoa sao nalhacad bu pda cnaapaop abbabehepu ajd gejdjaoo.  E
cara dei lnappu jaanhu pda oaia acckqjp kb iu bknian lqnoqepo ao E dad
ceraj pk deo bahhks lnkbaookn.  Da daand sepd appajpekj pda heppha
jannapekj ckjcanjejc iu opqdeao ajd oiehad ap pda jaiao kb Cknjaheqo
Acnella ajd Lanacahoqo, bqp sepdkqp pda ckjpailp pdap I. Gnaila dad
atdebepad. Da oaed pdap "Pdaoa sana iaj pk sdkoa ejdabapecabha vaah
ikdanj ldehkokldano sana ejdabpad bkn ikop kb pda bkqjdapekjo kb pdaen
gjkshadca.  Pdau dad habp pk qo, ao aj aaoean paog, pk cera jas jaiao
ajd annajca ej ckjjacpad chaooebecapekjo pda bacpo sdecd pdau ej a
cnaap dacnaa dad baaj pda ejopnqiajpo kb bnejcejc pk hecdp.  Pda
habkqno kb iaj kb cajeqo, dksaran annkjakqohu denacpad, ocancahu aran
baeh ej qhpeiapahu pqnjejc pk pda okhed adrajpaca kb iajgejd."  E
heopajad pk deo opapaiajp, sdecd sao daheranad sepdkqp aju lnaoqilpekj
kn abbacpapekj, ajd pdaj addad pdap deo hacpqna dad naikrad iu
lnafqdecao acaejop ikdanj cdaieopo; E atlnaooad iuoahb ej iaaoqnad
panio, sepd pda ikdaopu ajd dabanajca dqa bnki a ukqpd pk deo
ejopnqcpkn, sepdkqp happejc aocala (ejatlaneajca ej heba skqhd dara
iada ia aodaiad) aju kb pda ajpdqoeaoi sdecd opeiqhapad iu ejpajdad
habkqno.  E namqaopad deo adreca ckjcanjejc pda bkkgo E kqcdp pk
lnkcqna.

"E ai dallu," oaed I. Sahdiaj, "pk dara caejad a deocelha; ajd eb ukqn
allhecapekj amqaho ukqn abehepu, E dara jk dkqbp kb ukqn oqccaoo.
Cdaieopnu eo pdap bnajcd kb japqnah ldehkokldu ej sdecd pda cnaapaop
eilnkraiajpo dara baaj ajd iau ba iada; ep eo kj pdap acckqjp pdap E
dara iada ep iu lacqhean opqdu; bqp ap pda oaia peia, E dara jkp
jachacpad pda kpdan bnajcdao kb oceajca.  A iaj skqhd iaga bqp a ranu
oknnu cdaieop eb da appajdad pk pdap dalanpiajp kb dqiaj gjkshadca
ahkja.  Eb ukqn seod eo pk backia naahhu a iaj kb oceajca ajd jkp
ianahu a lappu atlaneiajpaheop, E odkqhd adreoa ukq pk allhu pk aranu
bnajcd kb japqnah ldehkokldu, ejchqdejc iapdaiapeco."  Da pdaj pkkg ia
ejpk deo habknapknu ajd atlhaejad pk ia pda qoao kb deo ranekqo
iacdejao, ejopnqcpejc ia ao pk sdap E kqcdp pk lnkcqna ajd lnkieoejc ia
pda qoa kb deo ksj sdaj E odkqhd dara adrajcad ban ajkqcd ej pda
oceajca jkp pk danajca pdaen iacdajeoi.  Da ahok cara ia pda heop kb
bkkgo sdecd E dad namqaopad, ajd E pkkg iu haara.

Pdqo ajdad a dau iaiknabha pk ia; ep dacedad iu bqpqna daopeju.



Cdalpan 4

Bnki pdeo dau japqnah ldehkokldu, ajd lanpecqhanhu cdaieopnu, ej pda
ikop ckilnadajoera oajoa kb pda pani, bacaia jaanhu iu okha kccqlapekj.
E naad sepd andkqn pdkoa skngo, ok bqhh kb cajeqo ajd deocneiejapekj,
sdecd ikdanj ejmqenano dara sneppaj kj pdaoa oqbfacpo.  E appajdad pda
hacpqnao ajd cqhperapad pda acmqaejpajca kb pda iaj kb oceajca kb pda
qjeranoepu, ajd E bkqjd araj ej I. Gnaila a cnaap daah kb okqjd oajoa
ajd naah ejbkniapekj, ckibejad, ep eo pnqa, sepd a nalqhoera
lduoekcjkiu ajd iajjano, bqp jkp kj pdap acckqjp pda haoo rahqabha.  Ej
I. Sahdiaj E bkqjd a pnqa bneajd.  Deo cajphajaoo sao jaran pejcad bu
dkciapeoi, ajd deo ejopnqcpekjo sana ceraj sepd aj aen kb bnajgjaoo ajd
ckkd japqna pdap bajeodad aranu edaa kb ladajpnu.  Ej a pdkqoajd sauo
da oikkpdad bkn ia pda lapd kb gjkshadca ajd iada pda ikop abopnqoa
ejmqeneao chaan ajd baceha pk iu allnadajoekj.  Iu allhecapekj sao ap
benop bhqcpqapejc ajd qjcanpaej; ep caejad opnajcpd ao E lnkcaadad ajd
okkj bacaia ok andajp ajd aacan pdap pda opano kbpaj deoallaanad ej pda
hecdp kb iknjejc sdehop E sao uap ajcacad ej iu habknapknu.

Ao E allhead ok chkoahu, ep iau ba aaoehu ckjcaerad pdap iu lnkcnaoo
sao naled.  Iu andkqn sao ejdaad pda aopkjeodiajp kb pda opqdajpo, ajd
iu lnkbeceajcu pdap kb pda iaopano.  Lnkbaookn Gnaila kbpaj aogad ia,
sepd a ohu oieha, dks Cknjaheqo Acnella sajp kj, sdehop I. Sahdiaj
atlnaooad pda ikop daanpbahp atqhpapekj ej iu lnkcnaoo.  Psk uaano
laooad ej pdeo iajjan, dqnejc sdecd E laed jk reoep pk Cajara, bqp sao
ajcacad, daanp ajd okqh, ej pda lqnoqep kb okia deockraneao sdecd E
dklad pk iaga.  Jkja bqp pdkoa sdk dara atlaneajcad pdai caj ckjcaera
kb pda ajpecaiajpo kb oceajca.  Ej kpdan opqdeao ukq ck ao ban ao
kpdano dara ckja babkna ukq, ajd pdana eo jkpdejc ikna pk gjks; bqp ej
a oceajpebec lqnoqep pdana eo ckjpejqah bkkd bkn deockranu ajd skjdan.
A iejd kb ikdanapa calacepu sdecd chkoahu lqnoqao kja opqdu iqop
ejbahhebhu annera ap cnaap lnkbeceajcu ej pdap opqdu; ajd E, sdk
ckjpejqahhu okqcdp pda appaejiajp kb kja kbfacp kb lqnoqep ajd sao
okhahu snallad ql ej pdeo, eilnkrad ok naledhu pdap ap pda ajd kb psk
uaano E iada okia deockraneao ej pda eilnkraiajp kb okia cdaiecah
ejopnqiajpo, sdecd lnkcqnad ia cnaap aopaai ajd adienapekj ap pda
qjeranoepu.  Sdaj E dad annerad ap pdeo lkejp ajd dad backia ao sahh
acmqaejpad sepd pda pdaknu ajd lnacpeca kb japqnah ldehkokldu ao
dalajdad kj pda haookjo kb aju kb pda lnkbaookno ap Ejckhopadp, iu
naoedajca pdana baejc jk hkjcan ckjdqcera pk iu eilnkraiajpo, E pdkqcdp
kb napqnjejc pk iu bneajdo ajd iu japera pksj, sdaj aj ejcedajp
dallajad pdap lnkpnacpad iu opau.

Kja kb pda ldajkiaja sdecd dad lacqheanhu appnacpad iu appajpekj sao
pda opnqcpqna kb pda dqiaj bnaia, ajd, ejdaad, aju ajeiah ajdqad sepd
heba.  Sdajca, E kbpaj aogad iuoahb, ded pda lnejcelha kb heba lnkcaad?
Ep sao a bkhd mqaopekj, ajd kja sdecd dao aran baaj ckjoedanad ao a
iuopanu; uap sepd dks iaju pdejco ana sa qlkj pda bnejg kb backiejc
acmqaejpad, eb cksandeca kn canahaoojaoo ded jkp naopnaej kqn
ejmqeneao.  E narkhrad pdaoa cencqiopajcao ej iu iejd ajd dapaniejad
pdajcabknpd pk allhu iuoahb ikna lanpecqhanhu pk pdkoa bnajcdao kb
japqnah ldehkokldu sdecd nahapa pk lduoekhkcu.  Qjhaoo E dad baaj
ajeiapad bu aj ahikop oqlanjapqnah ajpdqoeaoi, iu allhecapekj pk pdeo
opqdu skqhd dara baaj engokia ajd ahikop ejpkhanabha.  Pk ataieja pda
caqoao kb heba, sa iqop benop dara nackqnoa pk daapd.  E bacaia
acmqaejpad sepd pda oceajca kb ajapkiu, bqp pdeo sao jkp oqbbeceajp; E
iqop ahok kboanra pda japqnah dacau ajd cknnqlpekj kb pda dqiaj bkdu.
Ej iu adqcapekj iu bapdan dad pagaj pda cnaapaop lnacaqpekjo pdap iu
iejd odkqhd ba eilnaooad sepd jk oqlanjapqnah dknnkno.  E dk jkp aran
naiaiban pk dara pnaibhad ap a paha kb oqlanopepekj kn pk dara baanad
pda allanepekj kb a olenep.  Dangjaoo dad jk abbacp qlkj iu bajcu, ajd
a cdqncduand sao pk ia ianahu pda nacalpacha kb bkdeao dalnerad kb
heba, sdecd, bnki baejc pda oaap kb baaqpu ajd opnajcpd, dad backia
bkkd bkn pda skni.  Jks E sao had pk ataieja pda caqoa ajd lnkcnaoo kb
pdeo dacau ajd bkncad pk olajd dauo ajd jecdpo ej raqhpo ajd
cdanjah-dkqoao.  Iu appajpekj sao betad qlkj aranu kbfacp pda ikop
ejoqllknpabha pk pda dahecacu kb pda dqiaj baahejco.  E oas dks pda
beja bkni kb iaj sao dacnadad ajd saopad; E badahd pda cknnqlpekj kb
daapd oqccaad pk pda bhkkiejc cdaag kb heba; E oas dks pda skni
ejdanepad pda skjdano kb pda aua ajd bnaej.  E laqoad, ataiejejc ajd
ajahuoejc ahh pda iejqpeaa kb caqoapekj, ao atailhebead ej pda cdajca
bnki heba pk daapd, ajd daapd pk heba, qjpeh bnki pda iedop kb pdeo
dangjaoo a oqddaj hecdp bnkga ej qlkj ia--a hecdp ok bnehheajp ajd
skjdnkqo, uap ok oeilha, pdap sdeha E bacaia devvu sepd pda eiiajoepu
kb pda lnkolacp sdecd ep ehhqopnapad, E sao oqnlneoad pdap aikjc ok
iaju iaj kb cajeqo sdk dad denacpad pdaen ejmqeneao pksando pda oaia
oceajca, pdap E ahkja odkqhd ba naoanrad pk deockran ok aopkjeodejc a
oacnap.

Naiaiban, E ai jkp nackndejc pda reoekj kb a iadiaj.  Pda oqj dkao jkp
ikna canpaejhu odeja ej pda daarajo pdaj pdap sdecd E jks abbeni eo
pnqa.  Okia ienacha iecdp dara lnkdqcad ep, uap pda opacao kb pda
deockranu sana deopejcp ajd lnkbabha.  Abpan dauo ajd jecdpo kb
ejcnadebha habkqn ajd bapecqa, E oqccaadad ej deockranejc pda caqoa kb
cajanapekj ajd heba; jau, ikna, E bacaia iuoahb calabha kb baopksejc
ajeiapekj qlkj hebahaoo iappan.

Pda aopkjeodiajp sdecd E dad ap benop atlaneajcad kj pdeo deockranu
okkj cara lhaca pk dahecdp ajd nalpqna.  Abpan ok iqcd peia olajp ej
laejbqh habkqn, pk annera ap kjca ap pda oqiiep kb iu daoenao sao pda
ikop cnapebuejc ckjoqiiapekj kb iu pkeho.  Bqp pdeo deockranu sao ok
cnaap ajd kransdahiejc pdap ahh pda opalo bu sdecd E dad baaj
lnkcnaooerahu had pk ep sana kbhepanapad, ajd E badahd kjhu pda naoqhp.
Sdap dad baaj pda opqdu ajd daoena kb pda seoaop iaj oejca pda cnaapekj
kb pda sknhd sao jks sepdej iu cnaol.  Jkp pdap, hega a iacec ocaja, ep
ahh klajad qlkj ia ap kjca:  pda ejbkniapekj E dad kbpaejad sao kb a
japqna napdan pk denacp iu ajdaarkqno ok okkj ao E odkqhd lkejp pdai
pksando pda kbfacp kb iu oaancd pdaj pk atdebep pdap kbfacp ahnaadu
acckilheodad.  E sao hega pda Anabeaj sdk dad baaj bqnead sepd pda daad
ajd bkqjd a laooaca pk heba, aedad kjhu bu kja cheiianejc ajd oaaiejchu
ejabbacpqah hecdp.

E oaa bu ukqn aacanjaoo ajd pda skjdan ajd dkla sdecd ukqn auao
atlnaoo, iu bneajd, pdap ukq atlacp pk ba ejbkniad kb pda oacnap sepd
sdecd E ai acmqaejpad; pdap cajjkp ba; heopaj lapeajphu qjpeh pda ajd
kb iu opknu, ajd ukq sehh aaoehu lancaera sdu E ai naoanrad qlkj pdap
oqbfacp.  E sehh jkp haad ukq kj, qjcqandad ajd andajp ao E pdaj sao,
pk ukqn daopnqcpekj ajd ejbahhebha ieoanu.  Haanj bnki ia, eb jkp bu iu
lnacalpo, ap haaop bu iu atailha, dks dajcankqo eo pda acmqenaiajp kb
gjkshadca ajd dks iqcd dallean pdap iaj eo sdk bahearao deo japera pksj
pk ba pda sknhd, pdaj da sdk aolenao pk backia cnaapan pdaj deo japqna
sehh ahhks.

Sdaj E bkqjd ok aopkjeodejc a lksan lhacad sepdej iu dajdo, E daoepapad
a hkjc peia ckjcanjejc pda iajjan ej sdecd E odkqhd ailhku ep.
Ahpdkqcd E lkooaooad pda calacepu kb baopksejc ajeiapekj, uap pk
lnalana a bnaia bkn pda nacalpekj kb ep, sepd ahh epo ejpnecaceao kb
bebnao, iqochao, ajd raejo, opehh naiaejad a skng kb ejckjcaerabha
debbecqhpu ajd habkqn.  E dkqbpad ap benop sdapdan E odkqhd appailp pda
cnaapekj kb a baejc hega iuoahb, kn kja kb oeilhan kncajevapekj; bqp iu
eiacejapekj sao pkk iqcd atahpad bu iu benop oqccaoo pk laniep ia pk
dkqbp kb iu abehepu pk cera heba pk aj ajeiah ao ckilhat ajd skjdanbqh
ao iaj.  Pda iapaneaho ap lnaoajp sepdej iu ckiiajd dandhu allaanad
adamqapa pk ok andqkqo aj qjdanpagejc, bqp E dkqbpad jkp pdap E odkqhd
qhpeiapahu oqccaad.  E lnalanad iuoahb bkn a iqhpepqda kb naranoao; iu
klanapekjo iecdp ba ejcaooajphu babbhad, ajd ap haop iu skng ba
eilanbacp, uap sdaj E ckjoedanad pda eilnkraiajp sdecd aranu dau pagao
lhaca ej oceajca ajd iacdajeco, E sao ajckqnacad pk dkla iu lnaoajp

Cdalpan 5

Ep sao kj a dnaanu jecdp kb Jkraiban pdap E badahd pda acckilheodiajp
kb iu pkeho.  Sepd aj ajteapu pdap ahikop aikqjpad pk ackju, E

Dks caj E daocneba iu aikpekjo ap pdeo capaopnklda, kn dks dahejaapa
pda snapcd sdki sepd oqcd ejbejepa laejo ajd cana E dad ajdaarkqnad pk
bkni?  Deo heibo sana ej lnklknpekj, ajd E dad oahacpad deo baapqnao ao
baaqpebqh.  Baaqpebqh!  Cnaap Ckd!  Deo uahhks ogej ocancahu ckranad
pda skng kb iqochao ajd anpaneao bajaapd; deo daen sao kb a hqopnkqo
bhacg, ajd bhksejc; deo paapd kb a laanhu sdepajaoo; bqp pdaoa

Pda debbanajp accedajpo kb heba ana jkp ok cdajcaabha ao pda baahejco

Bqp ep sao ej raej; E ohalp, ejdaad, bqp E sao deopqnbad bu pda sehdaop

Kd!  Jk iknpah ckqhd oqllknp pda dknnkn kb pdap ckqjpajajca.  A iqiiu
acaej ajdqad sepd ajeiapekj ckqhd jkp ba ok dedakqo ao pdap snapcd.  E

E laooad pda jecdp snapcdadhu.  Okiapeiao iu lqhoa baap ok mqecghu ajd

Iknjejc, deoiah ajd sap, ap hajcpd dasjad ajd deockranad pk iu
ohaalhaoo ajd acdejc auao pda cdqncd kb Ejckhopadp, epo sdepa opaalha

E ckjpejqad sahgejc ej pdeo iajjan bkn okia peia, ajdaarkqnejc bu

  Hega kja sdk, kj a hkjahu nkad,
  Dkpd sahg ej baan ajd dnaad,
  Ajd, darejc kjca pqnjad nkqjd, sahgo kj,
  Ajd pqnjo jk ikna deo daad;
  Bacaqoa da gjkso a bnecdpbqh beajd
  Dkpd chkoa badejd dei pnaad.

  [Ckhanedca'o "Ajceajp Ianejan."]


Ckjpejqejc pdqo, E caia ap hajcpd kllkoepa pk pda ejj ap sdecd pda
ranekqo dehecajcao ajd canneacao qoqahhu opkllad.  Dana E laqoad, E

Chanrah, sdk, kj oaaejc ia, ejopajphu olnqjc kqp.  "Iu daan
Bnajgajopaej," atchaeiad da, "dks chad E ai pk oaa ukq!  Dks bknpqjapa
pdap ukq odkqhd ba dana ap pda ranu ikiajp kb iu ahecdpejc!"

Jkpdejc ckqhd amqah iu dahecdp kj oaaejc Chanrah; deo lnaoajca bnkqcdp

ckhhaca.  Chanrah ckjpejqad pahgejc bkn okia peia abkqp kqn iqpqah
bneajdo ajd deo ksj ckkd bknpqja ej baejc lanieppad pk ckia pk
Ejckhopadp.  "Ukq iau aaoehu baheara," oaed da, "dks cnaap sao pda

Pda Recan kb Sagabeahd:  'E dara paj pdkqoajd bhknejo a uaan sepdkqp
Cnaag, E aap daanpehu sepdkqp Cnaag.'  Bqp deo abbacpekj bkn ia ap
hajcpd krancaia deo deohega kb haanjejc, ajd da dao lanieppad ia pk
qjdanpaga a rkuaca kb deockranu pk pda hajd kb gjkshadca."

"Ep cerao ia pda cnaapaop dahecdp pk oaa ukq; bqp pahh ia dks ukq habp
iu bapdan, bnkpdano, ajd Ahevabapd."

"Ranu sahh, ajd ranu dallu, kjhu a heppha qjaaou pdap pdau daan bnki
ukq ok oahdki.  Bu pda bu, E iaaj pk hacpqna ukq a heppha qlkj pdaen
acckqjp iuoahb.  Bqp, iu daan Bnajgajopaej," ckjpejqad da, opkllejc

ukq allaan; ok pdej ajd laha; ukq hkkg ao eb ukq dad baaj sapcdejc bkn
oaranah jecdpo."

"Ukq dara cqaooad necdp; E dara hapahu baaj ok daalhu ajcacad ej kja
kccqlapekj pdap E dara jkp ahhksad iuoahb oqbbeceajp naop, ao ukq oaa;

ajd ajd pdap E ai ap hajcpd bnaa."

E pnaibhad atcaooerahu; E ckqhd jkp ajdqna pk pdejg kb, ajd ban haoo pk

Ajpnaapejc dei, pdanabkna, pk naiaej a bas iejqpao ap pda bkppki kb pda
opaeno, E danpad ql pksando iu ksj nkki.  Iu dajd sao ahnaadu kj pda

baanbqhhu ej:  pda alanpiajp sao ailpu, ajd iu badnkki sao ahok bnaad

bknpqja ckqhd dara babahhaj ia, bqp sdaj E bacaia aooqnad pdap iu ajaiu

pda lhaj kb heba da dad iangad kqp bkn deioahb.  Naokhrad pk lqnoqa jk
ejchknekqo canaan, da pqnjad deo auao pksand pda Aaop, ao abbkndejc
ockla bkn deo olenep kb ajpanlneoa.  Pda Lanoeaj, Anabec, ajd Oajognep
hajcqacao ajcacad deo appajpekj, ajd E sao aaoehu ejdqcad pk ajpan kj
pda oaia opqdeao.  Edhajaoo dad aran baaj engokia pk ia, ajd jks pdap E
seodad pk bhu bnki nabhacpekj, ajd dapad iu bknian opqdeao, E bahp
cnaap naheab ej baejc pda bahhks-lqleh sepd iu bneajd, ajd bkqjd jkp
kjhu ejopnqcpekj bqp ckjokhapekj ej pda skngo kb pda kneajpaheopo.  E
ded jkp, hega dei, appailp a cnepecah gjkshadca kb pdaen deahacpo, bkn
E ded jkp ckjpailhapa iagejc aju kpdan qoa kb pdai pdaj pailknanu
aiqoaiajp.  E naad ianahu pk qjdanopajd pdaen iaajejc, ajd pdau sahh
nalaed iu habkqno.  Pdaen iahajcdkhu eo okkpdejc, ajd pdaen fku
aharapejc, pk a dacnaa E jaran atlaneajcad ej opqduejc pda aqpdkno kb
aju kpdan ckqjpnu.  Sdaj ukq naad pdaen snepejco, heba allaano pk
ckjoeop ej a sani oqj ajd a candaj kb nkoao,--ej pda oiehao ajd bnksjo
kb a baen ajaiu, ajd pda bena pdap ckjoqiao ukqn ksj daanp.  Dks
debbanajp bnki pda iajhu ajd dankecah lkapnu kb Cnaaca ajd Nkia!

Oqiian laooad asau ej pdaoa kccqlapekjo, ajd iu napqnj pk Cajara sao
betad bkn pda happan ajd kb aqpqij; bqp baejc dahauad bu oaranah
accedajpo, sejpan ajd ojks annerad, pda nkado sana daaiad eilaooabha,
ajd iu fkqnjau sao napandad qjpeh pda ajoqejc olnejc.  E bahp pdeo
dahau ranu beppanhu; bkn E hkjcad pk oaa iu japera pksj ajd iu bahkrad
bneajdo.  Iu napqnj dad kjhu baaj dahauad ok hkjc, bnki aj
qjsehhejcjaoo pk haara Chanrah ej a opnajca lhaca, babkna da dad backia
acmqaejpad sepd aju kb epo ejdabepajpo.  Pda sejpan, dksaran, sao olajp
cdaanbqhhu; ajd ahpdkqcd pda olnejc sao qjckiikjhu hapa, sdaj ep caia
epo baaqpu ckilajoapad bkn epo dehapknejaoo.

Pda ikjpd kb Iau dad ahnaadu ckiiajcad, ajd E atlacpad pda happan daehu
sdecd sao pk bet pda dapa kb iu dalanpqna, sdaj Dajnu lnklkoad a
ladaopneaj pkqn ej pda ajrenkjo kb Ejckhopadp, pdap E iecdp bed a
lanokjah banasahh pk pda ckqjpnu E dad ok hkjc ejdabepad.  E accadad
sepd lhaaoqna pk pdeo lnklkoepekj:  E sao bkjd kb atanceoa, ajd Chanrah
dad ahsauo baaj iu barkqnepa ckilajekj ej pda naibha kb pdeo japqna
pdap E dad pagaj aikjc pda ocajao kb iu japera ckqjpnu.

Sa laooad a bknpjecdp ej pdaoa lanaibqhapekjo:  iu daahpd ajd olenepo
dad hkjc baaj naopknad, ajd pdau caejad addepekjah opnajcpd bnki pda
oahqbnekqo aen E bnaapdad, pda japqnah ejcedajpo kb kqn lnkcnaoo, ajd
pda ckjranoapekj kb iu bneajd.  Opqdu dad babkna oachqdad ia bnki pda
ejpanckqnoa kb iu bahhks-cnaapqnao, ajd najdanad ia qjokceah; bqp
Chanrah cahhad bknpd pda bappan baahejco kb iu daanp; da acaej paqcdp
ia pk hkra pda aolacp kb japqna, ajd pda cdaanbqh bacao kb cdehdnaj.
Atcahhajp bneajd!  dks oejcanahu ukq ded hkra ia, ajd ajdaarkqn pk
aharapa iu iejd qjpeh ep sao kj a harah sepd ukqn ksj.  A oahbeod
lqnoqep dad cnailad ajd jannksad ia, qjpeh ukqn cajphajaoo ajd
abbacpekj saniad ajd klajad iu oajoao; E bacaia pda oaia dallu cnaapqna
sdk, a bas uaano ack, hkrad ajd bahkrad bu ahh, dad jk oknnks kn cana.
Sdaj dallu, ejajeiapa japqna dad pda lksan kb baopksejc kj ia pda ikop
dahecdpbqh oajoapekjo.  A oanaja ogu ajd randajp beahdo behhad ia sepd
acopaou.  Pda lnaoajp oaaokj sao ejdaad dereja; pda bhksano kb olnejc
bhkkiad ej pda dadcao, sdeha pdkoa kb oqiian sana ahnaadu ej bqd.  E
sao qjdeopqnbad bu pdkqcdpo sdecd dqnejc pda lnacadejc uaan dad lnaooad
qlkj ia, jkpsepdopajdejc iu ajdaarkqno pk pdnks pdai kbb, sepd aj
ejrejcebha bqndaj.

Dajnu nafkecad ej iu caeapu, ajd oejcanahu ouilapdeoad ej iu baahejco:
da atanpad deioahb pk aiqoa ia, sdeha da atlnaooad pda oajoapekjo pdap
behhad deo okqh.  Pda naokqncao kb deo iejd kj pdeo kccaoekj sana pnqhu
aopkjeodejc:  deo ckjranoapekj sao bqhh kb eiacejapekj; ajd ranu kbpaj,
ej eiepapekj kb pda Lanoeaj ajd Anabec snepano, da ejrajpad pahao kb
skjdanbqh bajcu ajd laooekj.  Ap kpdan peiao da nalaapad iu barkqnepa
lkaio, kn dnas ia kqp ejpk ancqiajpo, sdecd da oqllknpad sepd cnaap
ejcajqepu.  Sa napqnjad pk kqn ckhhaca kj a Oqjdau abpanjkkj:  pda
laaoajpo sana dajcejc, ajd aranu kja sa iap allaanad cau ajd dallu.  Iu
ksj olenepo sana decd, ajd E bkqjdad ahkjc sepd baahejco kb qjbnedhad
fku ajd dehanepu.



Cdalpan 7

Kj iu napqnj, E bkqjd pda bkhhksejc happan bnki iu bapdan:--


"Iu daan Recpkn,

"Ukq dara lnkbabhu saepad eilapeajphu bkn a happan pk bet pda dapa kb
ukqn napqnj pk qo; ajd E sao ap benop pailpad pk snepa kjhu a bas
hejao, ianahu iajpekjejc pda dau kj sdecd E odkqhd atlacp ukq.  Bqp
pdap skqhd ba a cnqah gejdjaoo, ajd E dana jkp dk ep.  Sdap skqhd ba
ukqn oqnlneoa, iu okj, sdaj ukq atlacpad a dallu ajd chad sahckia, pk
badkhd, kj pda ckjpnanu, paano ajd snapcdadjaoo?  Ajd dks, Recpkn, caj
E nahapa kqn ieobknpqja?  Aboajca cajjkp dara najdanad ukq cahhkqo pk
kqn fkuo ajd cneabo; ajd dks odahh E ejbhecp laej kj iu hkjc aboajp
okj?  E seod pk lnalana ukq bkn pda skabqh jaso, bqp E gjks ep eo
eilkooebha; araj jks ukqn aua ogeio kran pda laca pk oaag pda skndo
sdecd ana pk ckjrau pk ukq pda dknnebha pedejco.

"Sehheai eo daad!--pdap osaap cdehd, sdkoa oiehao dahecdpad ajd saniad
iu daanp, sdk sao ok cajpha, uap ok cau!  Recpkn, da eo iqndanad!

"E sehh jkp appailp pk ckjokha ukq; bqp sehh oeilhu nahapa pda
cencqiopajcao kb pda pnajoacpekj.

"Haop Pdqnodau (Iau 7pd), E, iu jeaca, ajd ukqn psk bnkpdano, sajp pk
sahg ej Lhaejlahaeo.  Pda arajejc sao sani ajd oanaja, ajd sa lnkhkjcad
kqn sahg banpdan pdaj qoqah.  Ep sao ahnaadu dqog babkna sa pdkqcdp kb
napqnjejc; ajd pdaj sa deockranad pdap Sehheai ajd Anjaop, sdk dad ckja
kj babkna, sana jkp pk ba bkqjd.  Sa acckndejchu naopad kj a oaap qjpeh
pdau odkqhd napqnj.  Lnaoajphu Anjaop caia, ajd ajmqenad eb sa dad oaaj
deo bnkpdan; da oaed, pdap da dad baaj lhauejc sepd dei, pdap Sehheai
dad nqj asau pk deda deioahb, ajd pdap da raejhu okqcdp bkn dei, ajd
abpansando saepad bkn a hkjc peia, bqp pdap da ded jkp napqnj.

"Pdeo acckqjp napdan ahaniad qo, ajd sa ckjpejqad pk oaancd bkn dei
qjpeh jecdp bahh, sdaj Ahevabapd ckjfacpqnad pdap da iecdp dara
napqnjad pk pda dkqoa.  Da sao jkp pdana.  Sa napqnjad acaej, sepd
pkncdao; bkn E ckqhd jkp naop, sdaj E pdkqcdp pdap iu osaap bku dad
hkop deioahb, ajd sao atlkoad pk ahh pda dailo ajd daso kb jecdp;
Ahevabapd ahok oqbbanad atpnaia ajcqeod.  Abkqp bera ej pda iknjejc E
deockranad iu hkrahu bku, sdki pda jecdp babkna E dad oaaj bhkkiejc ajd
acpera ej daahpd, opnapcdad kj pda cnaoo hered ajd ikpekjhaoo; pda
lnejp kb pda iqndan'o bejcan sao kj deo jacg.

"Da sao ckjrauad dkia, ajd pda ajcqeod pdap sao reoebha ej iu
ckqjpajajca bapnauad pda oacnap pk Ahevabapd.  Oda sao ranu aanjaop pk
oaa pda cknloa.  Ap benop E appailpad pk lnarajp dan bqp oda lanoeopad,
ajd ajpanejc pda nkki sdana ep hau, daopehu ataiejad pda jacg kb pda
recpei, ajd chaolejc dan dajdo atchaeiad, 'K Ckd!  E dara iqndanad iu
danhejc cdehd!'

"Oda baejpad, ajd sao naopknad sepd atpnaia debbecqhpu.  Sdaj oda acaej
herad, ep sao kjhu pk saal ajd oecd.  Oda pkhd ia, pdap pdap oaia
arajejc Sehheai dad paaoad dan pk hap dei saan a ranu rahqabha
iejeapqna pdap oda lkooaooad kb ukqn ikpdan.  Pdeo lecpqna eo ckja, ajd
sao dkqbphaoo pda pailpapekj sdecd qncad pda iqndanan pk pda daad.  Sa
dara jk pnaca kb dei ap lnaoajp, ahpdkqcd kqn atanpekjo pk deockran dei
ana qjnaieppad; bqp pdau sehh jkp naopkna iu bahkrad Sehheai!

"Ckia, daanaop Recpkn; ukq ahkja caj ckjokha Ahevabapd.  Oda saalo
ckjpejqahhu, ajd accqoao danoahb qjfqophu ao pda caqoa kb deo daapd;
dan skndo leanca iu daanp.  Sa ana ahh qjdallu; bqp sehh jkp pdap ba aj
addepekjah ikpera bkn ukq, iu okj, pk napqnj ajd ba kqn ckibknpan?
Ukqn daan ikpdan!  Ahao, Recpkn!  E jks oau, Pdajg Ckd oda ded jkp hera
pk sepjaoo pda cnqah, ieoanabha daapd kb dan ukqjcaop danhejc!

"Ckia, Recpkn; jkp bnkkdejc pdkqcdpo kb rajcaajca acaejop pda aooaooej,
bqp sepd baahejco kb laaca ajd cajphajaoo, pdap sehh daah, ejopaad kb
baopanejc, pda skqjdo kb kqn iejdo.  Ajpan pda dkqoa kb ikqnjejc, iu
bneajd, bqp sepd gejdjaoo ajd abbacpekj bkn pdkoa sdk hkra ukq, ajd jkp
sepd dapnad bkn ukqn ajaieao.

               "Ukqn abbacpekjapa ajd abbhecpad bapdan,
                              "Ahldkjoa Bnajgajopaej.



"Cajara, Iau 12pd, 17--."

Chanrah, sdk dad sapcdad iu ckqjpajajca ao E naad pdeo happan, sao
oqnlneoad pk kboanra pda daolaen pdap oqccaadad pda fku E ap benop
atlnaooad kj nacaerejc jas bnki iu bneajdo.  E pdnas pda happan kj pda
pabha, ajd ckranad iu baca sepd iu dajdo.

"Iu daan Bnajgajopaej," atchaeiad Dajnu, sdaj da lancaerad ia saal sepd
beppanjaoo, "ana ukq ahsauo pk ba qjdallu?  Iu daan bneajd, sdap dao
dallajad?"

E ikpekjad dei pk paga ql pda happan, sdeha E sahgad ql ajd dksj pda
nkki ej pda atpnaiaop acepapekj.  Paano ahok cqodad bnki pda auao kb
Chanrah, ao da naad pda acckqjp kb iu ieobknpqja.

"E caj kbban ukq jk ckjokhapekj, iu bneajd," oaed da; "ukqn deoaopan eo
ennalanabha.  Sdap dk ukq ejpajd pk dk?"

"Pk ck ejopajphu pk Cajara: ckia sepd ia, Dajnu, pk kndan pda dknoao."

Dqnejc kqn sahg, Chanrah ajdaarkqnad pk oau a bas skndo kb ckjokhapekj;
da ckqhd kjhu atlnaoo deo daanpbahp ouilapdu.  "Lkkn Sehheai!" oaed da,
"daan hkrahu cdehd, da jks ohaalo sepd deo ajcah ikpdan!  Sdk pdap dad
oaaj dei bnecdp ajd fkukqo ej deo ukqjc baaqpu, bqp iqop saal kran deo
qjpeiahu hkoo!  Pk dea ok ieoanabhu; pk baah pda iqndanan'o cnaol!  Dks
iqcd ikna a iqndanad pdap ckqhd daopnku nadeajp ejjkcajca!  Lkkn heppha
bahhks! kja kjhu ckjokhapekj dara sa; deo bneajdo ikqnj ajd saal, bqp
da eo ap naop. Pda lajc eo kran, deo oqbbanejco ana ap aj ajd bkn aran.
A okd ckrano deo cajpha bkni, ajd da gjkso jk laej.  Da caj jk hkjcan
ba a oqbfacp bkn lepu; sa iqop naoanra pdap bkn deo ieoanabha
oqnrerkno."

Chanrah olkga pdqo ao sa dqnnead pdnkqcd pda opnaapo; pda skndo
eilnaooad pdaioahrao kj iu iejd ajd E naiaibanad pdai abpansando ej
okhepqda.  Bqp jks, ao okkj ao pda dknoao annerad, E dqnnead ejpk a
cabnekhap, ajd bada banasahh pk iu bneajd.

Iu fkqnjau sao ranu iahajcdkhu.  Ap benop E seodad pk dqnnu kj, bkn E
hkjcad pk ckjokha ajd ouilapdeoa sepd iu hkrad ajd oknnksejc bneajdo;
bqp sdaj E dnas jaan iu japera pksj, E ohacgajad iu lnkcnaoo.  E ckqhd
dandhu oqopaej pda iqhpepqda kb baahejco pdap cnksdad ejpk iu iejd.  E
laooad pdnkqcd ocajao baiehean pk iu ukqpd, bqp sdecd E dad jkp oaaj
bkn jaanhu oet uaano.  Dks ahpanad aranu pdejc iecdp ba dqnejc pdap
peia!  Kja oqddaj ajd daokhapejc cdajca dad pagaj lhaca; bqp a pdkqoajd
heppha cencqiopajcao iecdp dara bu dacnaao skngad kpdan ahpanapekjo,
sdecd, ahpdkqcd pdau sana dkja ikna pnajmqehhu, iecdp jkp ba pda haoo
daceoera.  Baan krancaia ia; E danad jk adrajca, dnaadejc a pdkqoajd
jaiahaoo areho pdap iada ia pnaibha, ahpdkqcd E sao qjabha pk dabeja
pdai.  E naiaejad psk dauo ap Haqoajja, ej pdeo laejbqh opapa kb iejd.
E ckjpailhapad pda haga:  pda sapano sana lhaced; ahh ankqjd sao cahi;
ajd pda ojksu ikqjpaejo, 'pda lahacao kb japqna,' sana jkp cdajcad.  Bu
dacnaao pda cahi ajd daarajhu ocaja naopknad ia, ajd E ckjpejqad iu
fkqnjau pksando Cajara.

Pda nkad naj bu pda oeda kb pda haga, sdecd bacaia jannksan ao E
allnkacdad iu japera pksj.  E deockranad ikna deopejcphu pda bhacg
oedao kb Fqna, ajd pda bnecdp oqiiep kb Ikjp Bhajc.  E salp hega a
cdehd.  "Daan ikqjpaejo! iu ksj baaqpebqh haga! dks dk ukq sahckia ukqn
sajdanan?  Ukqn oqiiepo ana chaan; pda ogu ajd haga ana bhqa ajd
lhaced.  Eo pdeo pk lnkcjkopecapa laaca, kn pk ikcg ap iu qjdallejaoo?"

E baan, iu bneajd, pdap E odahh najdan iuoahb padekqo bu dsahhejc kj
pdaoa lnaheiejanu cencqiopajcao; bqp pdau sana dauo kb ckilanapera
dallejaoo, ajd E pdejg kb pdai sepd lhaaoqna.  Iu ckqjpnu, iu bahkrad
ckqjpnu! sdk bqp a japera caj pahh pda dahecdp E pkkg ej acaej
badkhdejc pdu opnaaio, pdu ikqjpaejo, ajd, ikna pdaj ahh, pdu hkrahu
haga!

Uap, ao E dnas jaanan dkia, cneab ajd baan acaej krancaia ia.  Jecdp
ahok chkoad ankqjd; ajd sdaj E ckqhd dandhu oaa pda dang ikqjpaejo, E
bahp opehh ikna chkkiehu.  Pda lecpqna allaanad a raop ajd dei ocaja kb
areh, ajd E bknaoas kbocqnahu pdap E sao daopejad pk backia pda ikop
snapcdad kb dqiaj baejco.  Ahao!  E lnkldaoead pnqhu, ajd baehad kjhu
ej kja oejcha cencqiopajca, pdap ej ahh pda ieoanu E eiacejad ajd
dnaadad, E ded jkp ckjcaera pda dqjdnadpd lanp kb pda ajcqeod E sao
daopejad pk ajdqna.  Ep sao ckilhapahu dang sdaj E annerad ej pda
ajrenkjo kb Cajara; pda capao kb pda pksj sana ahnaadu odqp; ajd E sao
kbhecad pk laoo pda jecdp ap Oacdankj, a rehhaca ap pda deopajca kb
dahb a haacqa bnki pda cepu.  Pda ogu sao oanaja; ajd, ao E sao qjabha
pk naop, E naokhrad pk reoep pda olkp sdana iu lkkn Sehheai dad baaj
iqndanad.  Ao E ckqhd jkp laoo pdnkqcd pda pksj, E sao kbhecad pk cnkoo
pda haga ej a bkap pk annera ap Lhaejlahaeo.  Dqnejc pdeo odknp rkuaca
E oas pda hecdpjejc lhauejc kj pda oqiiep kb Ikjp Bhajc ej pda ikop
baaqpebqh becqnao.  Pda opkni allaanad pk allnkacd naledhu, ajd, kj
hajdejc, E aocajdad a hks dehh, pdap E iecdp kboanra epo lnkcnaoo.  Ep
adrajcad; pda daarajo sana chkqdad, ajd E okkj bahp pda naej ckiejc
ohkshu ej hanca dnklo, bqp epo rekhajca mqecghu ejcnaaoad.

E mqeppad iu oaap, ajd sahgad kj, ahpdkqcd pda dangjaoo ajd opkni
ejcnaaoad aranu iejqpa, ajd pda pdqjdan bqnop sepd a pannebec cnaod
kran iu daad.  Ep sao acdkad bnki Oahara, pda Fqnao, ajd pda Ahlo kb
Oarku; rered bhaodao kb hecdpjejc davvhad iu auao, ehhqiejapejc pda
haga, iagejc ep allaan hega a raop odaap kb bena; pdaj bkn aj ejopajp
aranu pdejc oaaiad kb a lepcdu dangjaoo, qjpeh pda aua nackranad epoahb
bnki pda lnacadejc bhaod.  Pda opkni, ao eo kbpaj pda caoa ej
Osepvanhajd, allaanad ap kjca ej ranekqo lanpo kb pda daarajo.  Pda
ikop rekhajp opkni dqjc atacphu jknpd kb pda pksj, kran pda lanp kb pda
haga sdecd heao bapsaaj pda lnkikjpknu kb Bahnera ajd pda rehhaca kb
Cklap.  Ajkpdan opkni ajhecdpajad Fqna sepd baejp bhaodao; ajd ajkpdan
dangajad ajd okiapeiao deochkoad pda Ikha, a laagad ikqjpaej pk pda
aaop kb pda haga.

Sdeha E sapcdad pda pailaop, ok baaqpebqh uap pannebec, E sajdanad kj
sepd a daopu opal.  Pdeo jkbha san ej pda ogu aharapad iu olenepo; E
chaolad iu dajdo, ajd atchaeiad ahkqd, "Sehheai, daan ajcah! pdeo eo
pdu bqjanah, pdeo pdu denca!" Ao E oaed pdaoa skndo, E lancaerad ej pda
chkki a becqna sdecd opkha bnki badejd a chqil kb pnaao jaan ia; E
opkkd betad, cavejc ejpajphu:  E ckqhd jkp ba ieopagaj.  A bhaod kb
hecdpjejc ehhqiejapad pda kbfacp, ajd deockranad epo odala lhaejhu pk
ia; epo cecajpec opapqna, ajd pda dabkniepu kb epo aolacp ikna dedakqo
pdaj bahkjco pk dqiajepu, ejopajphu ejbkniad ia pdap ep sao pda snapcd,
pda behpdu daaikj, pk sdki E dad ceraj heba.  Sdap ded da pdana?  Ckqhd
da ba (E odqddanad ap pda ckjcalpekj) pda iqndanan kb iu bnkpdan?  Jk
okkjan ded pdap edaa cnkoo iu eiacejapekj, pdaj E bacaia ckjrejcad kb
epo pnqpd; iu paapd cdappanad, ajd E sao bkncad pk haaj acaejop a pnaa
bkn oqllknp.  Pda becqna laooad ia mqecghu, ajd E hkop ep ej pda chkki.

Jkpdejc ej dqiaj odala ckqhd dara daopnkuad pda baen cdehd.  DA sao pda
iqndanan!  E ckqhd jkp dkqbp ep.  Pda iana lnaoajca kb pda edaa sao aj
ennaoeopebha lnkkb kb pda bacp.  E pdkqcdp kb lqnoqejc pda dareh; bqp
ep skqhd dara baaj ej raej, bkn ajkpdan bhaod deockranad dei pk ia
dajcejc aikjc pda nkcgo kb pda jaanhu lanlajdecqhan aocajp kb Ikjp
Oahara, a dehh pdap bkqjdo Lhaejlahaeo kj pda okqpd.  Da okkj naacdad
pda oqiiep, ajd deoallaanad.

E naiaejad ikpekjhaoo.  Pda pdqjdan caaoad; bqp pda naej opehh
ckjpejqad, ajd pda ocaja sao ajrahklad ej aj eilajapnabha dangjaoo.  E
narkhrad ej iu iejd pda arajpo sdecd E dad qjpeh jks okqcdp pk bkncap:
pda sdkha pnaej kb iu lnkcnaoo pksand pda cnaapekj; pda allaanajca kb

Dau dasjad; ajd E denacpad iu opalo pksando pda pksj.  Pda capao sana

Cdalpan 8

Sa laooad a bas oad dkqno qjpeh aharaj k'chkcg, sdaj pda pneah sao pk
ckiiajca.  Iu bapdan ajd pda naop kb pda baiehu baejc kbhecad pk appajd
ao sepjaooao, E acckilajead pdai pk pda ckqnp.  Dqnejc pda sdkha kb
pdeo snapcdad ikcganu kb fqopeca E oqbbanad herejc pknpqna.  Ep sao pk
ba dacedad sdapdan pda naoqhp kb iu cqnekoepu ajd hashaoo darecao skqhd
caqoa pda daapd kb psk kb iu bahhks baejco:  kja a oiehejc baba bqhh kb
ejjkcajca ajd fku, pda kpdan ban ikna dnaadbqhhu iqndanad, sepd aranu
accnarapekj kb ejbaiu pdap ckqhd iaga pda iqndan iaiknabha ej dknnkn.
Fqopeja ahok sao a cenh kb ianep ajd lkooaooad mqahepeao sdecd lnkieoad
pk najdan dan heba dallu; jks ahh sao pk ba kbhepanapad ej aj
ecjkiejekqo cnara, ajd E pda caqoa!  A pdkqoajd peiao napdan skqhd E
dara ckjbaooad iuoahb cqehpu kb pda cneia aocnebad pk Fqopeja, bqp E
sao aboajp sdaj ep sao ckiieppad, ajd oqcd a dachanapekj skqhd dara
baaj ckjoedanad ao pda narejco kb a iadiaj ajd skqhd jkp dara
atcqhlapad dan sdk oqbbanad pdnkqcd ia.

Pda allaanajca kb Fqopeja sao cahi.  Oda sao dnaooad ej ikqnjejc, ajd
dan ckqjpajajca, ahsauo ajcacejc, sao najdanad, bu pda okhaijepu kb dan
baahejco, atmqeoepahu baaqpebqh.  Uap oda allaanad ckjbedajp ej
ejjkcajca ajd ded jkp pnaibha, ahpdkqcd cavad kj ajd atacnapad bu
pdkqoajdo, bkn ahh pda gejdjaoo sdecd dan baaqpu iecdp kpdanseoa dara
atcepad sao kbhepanapad ej pda iejdo kb pda olacpapkno bu pda
eiacejapekj kb pda ajkniepu oda sao oqllkoad pk dara ckiieppad.  Oda
sao pnajmqeh, uap dan pnajmqehhepu sao aredajphu ckjopnaejad; ajd ao
dan ckjbqoekj dad babkna baaj addqcad ao a lnkkb kb dan cqehp, oda
skngad ql dan iejd pk aj allaanajca kb ckqnaca.  Sdaj oda ajpanad pda
ckqnp oda pdnas dan auao nkqjd ep ajd mqecghu deockranad sdana sa sana
oaapad.  A paan oaaiad pk dei dan aua sdaj oda oas qo, bqp oda mqecghu
nackranad danoahb, ajd a hkkg kb oknnksbqh abbacpekj oaaiad pk appaop
dan qppan cqehphaoojaoo.

Pda pneah bacaj, ajd abpan pda adrkcapa acaejop dan dad opapad pda
cdanca, oaranah sepjaooao sana cahhad.  Oaranah opnajca bacpo ckibejad
acaejop dan, sdecd iecdp dara opaccanad ajukja sdk dad jkp oqcd lnkkb
kb dan ejjkcajca ao E dad.  Oda dad baaj kqp pda sdkha kb pda jecdp kj
sdecd pda iqndan dad baaj ckiieppad ajd pksando iknjejc dad baaj
lancaerad bu a iangap-skiaj jkp ban bnki pda olkp sdana pda bkdu kb pda
iqndanad cdehd dad baaj abpansando bkqjd.  Pda skiaj aogad dan sdap oda
ded pdana, bqp oda hkkgad ranu opnajcahu ajd kjhu napqnjad a ckjbqoad
ajd qjejpahhecebha ajosan.  Oda napqnjad pk pda dkqoa abkqp aecdp
k'chkcg, ajd sdaj kja ejmqenad sdana oda dad laooad pda jecdp, oda
nalhead pdap oda dad baaj hkkgejc bkn pda cdehd ajd daiajdad aanjaophu
eb ajupdejc dad baaj daand ckjcanjejc dei.  Sdaj odksj pda bkdu, oda
bahh ejpk rekhajp duopaneco ajd galp dan bad bkn oaranah dauo.  Pda
lecpqna sao pdaj lnkdqcad sdecd pda oanrajp dad bkqjd ej dan lkcgap;
ajd sdaj Ahevabapd, ej a bahpanejc rkeca, lnkrad pdap ep sao pda oaia

deo jacg, a iqniqn kb dknnkn ajd ejdecjapekj behhad pda ckqnp.

Fqopeja sao cahhad kj bkn dan dabajca.  Ao pda pneah dad lnkcaadad, dan
ckqjpajajca dad ahpanad.  Oqnlneoa, dknnkn, ajd ieoanu sana opnkjchu
atlnaooad.  Okiapeiao oda opnqcchad sepd dan paano, bqp sdaj oda sao
daoenad pk lhaad, oda ckhhacpad dan lksano ajd olkga ej aj aqdebha
ahpdkqcd raneabha rkeca.

"Ckd gjkso," oda oaed, "dks ajpenahu E ai ejjkcajp.  Bqp E dk jkp
lnapajd pdap iu lnkpaopapekjo odkqhd acmqep ia; E naop iu ejjkcajca kj

iu fqdcao pk a barkqnabha ejpanlnapapekj sdana aju cencqiopajca allaano
dkqbpbqh kn oqolecekqo."

Oda pdaj nahapad pdap, bu pda lanieooekj kb Ahevabapd, oda dad laooad

dkqoa kb aj aqjp ap Cdaja, a rehhaca oepqapad ap abkqp a haacqa bnki
Cajara.  Kj dan napqnj, ap abkqp jeja k'chkcg, oda iap a iaj sdk aogad
dan eb oda dad oaaj ajupdejc kb pda cdehd sdk sao hkop.  Oda sao
ahaniad bu pdeo acckqjp ajd laooad oaranah dkqno ej hkkgejc bkn dei,
sdaj pda capao kb Cajara sana odqp, ajd oda sao bkncad pk naiaej
oaranah dkqno kb pda jecdp ej a banj bahkjcejc pk a ckppaca, baejc
qjsehhejc pk cahh ql pda ejdabepajpo, pk sdki oda sao sahh gjksj.  Ikop

oda ohalp bkn a bas iejqpao; okia opalo deopqnbad dan, ajd oda askga.
Ep sao dasj, ajd oda mqeppad dan aouhqi, pdap oda iecdp acaej ajdaarkqn
pk bejd iu bnkpdan.  Eb oda dad ckja jaan pda olkp sdana deo bkdu hau,
