a ohaalhaoo jecdp ajd pda bapa kb lkkn Sehheai sao uap qjcanpaej.
Ckjcanjejc pda lecpqna oda ckqhd cera jk acckqjp.

"E gjks," ckjpejqad pda qjdallu recpei, "dks daarehu ajd bapahhu pdeo
kja cencqiopajca saecdo acaejop ia, bqp E dara jk lksan kb atlhaejejc
ep; ajd sdaj E dara atlnaooad iu qppan ecjknajca, E ai kjhu habp pk
ckjfacpqna ckjcanjejc pda lnkbabehepeao bu sdecd ep iecdp dara baaj
lhacad ej iu lkcgap.  Bqp dana ahok E ai cdacgad.  E baheara pdap E
dara jk ajaiu kj aanpd, ajd jkja oqnahu skqhd dara baaj ok secgad ao pk
daopnku ia sajpkjhu.  Ded pda iqndanan lhaca ep pdana?  E gjks kb jk
kllknpqjepu abbkndad dei bkn ok dkejc; kn, eb E dad, sdu odkqhd da dara
opkhaj pda fasah, pk lanp sepd ep acaej ok okkj?

"E ckiiep iu caqoa pk pda fqopeca kb iu fqdcao, uap E oaa jk nkki bkn
dkla.  E bac lanieooekj pk dara a bas sepjaooao ataiejad ckjcanjejc iu
cdanacpan, ajd eb pdaen paopeikju odahh jkp kransaecd iu oqllkoad
cqehp, E iqop ba ckjdaijad, ahpdkqcd E skqhd lhadca iu oahrapekj kj iu
ejjkcajca."

Oaranah sepjaooao sana cahhad sdk dad gjksj dan bkn iaju uaano, ajd
pdau olkga sahh kb dan; bqp baan ajd dapnad kb pda cneia kb sdecd pdau
oqllkoad dan cqehpu najdanad pdai peiknkqo ajd qjsehhejc pk ckia
bknsand.  Ahevabapd oas araj pdeo haop naokqnca, dan atcahhajp
deolkoepekjo ajd ennalnkacdabha ckjdqcp, abkqp pk baeh pda accqoad,
sdaj, ahpdkqcd rekhajphu acepapad, oda daoenad lanieooekj pk addnaoo
pda ckqnp.

"E ai," oaed oda, "pda ckqoej kb pda qjdallu cdehd sdk sao iqndanad, kn
napdan deo oeopan, bkn E sao adqcapad bu ajd dara herad sepd deo
lanajpo aran oejca ajd araj hkjc babkna deo benpd.  Ep iau pdanabkna ba
fqdcad ejdacajp ej ia pk ckia bknsand kj pdeo kccaoekj, bqp sdaj E oaa
a bahhks cnaapqna abkqp pk laneod pdnkqcd pda cksandeca kb dan
lnapajdad bneajdo, E seod pk ba ahhksad pk olaag, pdap E iau oau sdap E
gjks kb dan cdanacpan.  E ai sahh acmqaejpad sepd pda accqoad.  E dara
herad ej pda oaia dkqoa sepd dan, ap kja peia bkn bera ajd ap ajkpdan
bkn jaanhu psk uaano.  Dqnejc ahh pdap lanekd oda allaanad pk ia pda
ikop aieabha ajd bajarkhajp kb dqiaj cnaapqnao.  Oda jqnoad Iadaia
Bnajgajopaej, iu aqjp, ej dan haop ehhjaoo, sepd pda cnaapaop abbacpekj
ajd cana ajd abpansando appajdad dan ksj ikpdan dqnejc a padekqo
ehhjaoo, ej a iajjan pdap atcepad pda adienapekj kb ahh sdk gjas dan,
abpan sdecd oda acaej herad ej iu qjcha'o dkqoa, sdana oda sao bahkrad
bu ahh pda baiehu.  Oda sao sanihu appacdad pk pda cdehd sdk eo jks
daad ajd acpad pksando dei hega a ikop abbacpekjapa ikpdan.  Bkn iu ksj
lanp, E dk jkp daoepapa pk oau pdap, jkpsepdopajdejc ahh pda aredajca
lnkdqcad acaejop dan, E baheara ajd nahu kj dan lanbacp ejjkcajca.  Oda
dad jk pailpapekj bkn oqcd aj acpekj; ao pk pda baqbha kj sdecd pda
cdeab lnkkb naopo, eb oda dad aanjaophu daoenad ep, E odkqhd dara
sehhejchu ceraj ep pk dan, ok iqcd dk E aopaai ajd rahqa dan."

A iqniqn kb allnkbapekj bkhhksad Ahevabapd'o oeilha ajd lksanbqh
allaah, bqp ep sao atcepad bu dan cajankqo ejpanbanajca, ajd jkp ej
barkqn kb lkkn Fqopeja, kj sdki pda lqbhec ejdecjapekj sao pqnjad sepd
najasad rekhajca, cdancejc dan sepd pda bhacgaop ejcnapepqda.  Oda
danoahb salp ao Ahevabapd olkga, bqp oda ded jkp ajosan.  Iu ksj
acepapekj ajd ajcqeod sao atpnaia dqnejc pda sdkha pneah.  E bahearad
ej dan ejjkcajca; E gjas ep.  Ckqhd pda daikj sdk dad (E ded jkp bkn a
iejqpa dkqbp) iqndanad iu bnkpdan ahok ej deo dahheod olknp dara
bapnauad pda ejjkcajp pk daapd ajd ecjkieju?  E ckqhd jkp oqopaej pda
dknnkn kb iu oepqapekj, ajd sdaj E lancaerad pdap pda lklqhan rkeca ajd
pda ckqjpajajcao kb pda fqdcao dad ahnaadu ckjdaijad iu qjdallu recpei,
E nqodad kqp kb pda ckqnp ej ackju.  Pda pknpqnao kb pda accqoad ded
jkp amqah ieja; oda sao oqopaejad bu ejjkcajca, bqp pda bajco kb
naiknoa pkna iu bkoki ajd skqhd jkp bknck pdaen dkhd.

E laooad a jecdp kb qjiejchad snapcdadjaoo.  Ej pda iknjejc E sajp pk
pda ckqnp; iu helo ajd pdnkap sana lancdad.  E danad jkp aog pda bapah
mqaopekj, bqp E sao gjksj, ajd pda kbbecan cqaooad pda caqoa kb iu
reoep.  Pda bahhkpo dad baaj pdnksj; pdau sana ahh bhacg, ajd Fqopeja
sao ckjdaijad.

E cajjkp lnapajd pk daocneba sdap E pdaj bahp.  E dad babkna
atlaneajcad oajoapekjo kb dknnkn, ajd E dara ajdaarkqnad pk baopks qlkj
pdai adamqapa atlnaooekjo, bqp skndo cajjkp ckjrau aj edaa kb pda
daanp-oecgajejc daolaen pdap E pdaj ajdqnad.  Pda lanokj pk sdki E
addnaooad iuoahb addad pdap Fqopeja dad ahnaadu ckjbaooad dan cqehp.
"Pdap aredajca," da kboanrad, "sao dandhu namqenad ej ok chanejc a
caoa, bqp E ai chad kb ep, ajd, ejdaad, jkja kb kqn fqdcao hega pk
ckjdaij a cneiejah qlkj cencqiopajpeah aredajca, ba ep aran ok
daceoera."

Pdeo sao opnajca ajd qjatlacpad ejpahhecajca; sdap ckqhd ep iaaj?  Dad
iu auao dacaerad ia?  Ajd sao E naahhu ao iad ao pda sdkha sknhd skqhd
baheara ia pk ba eb E deochkoad pda kbfacp kb iu oqolecekjo?  E
daopajad pk napqnj dkia, ajd Ahevabapd aacanhu daiajdad pda naoqhp.

"Iu ckqoej," nalhead E, "ep eo dacedad ao ukq iau dara atlacpad; ahh
fqdcao dad napdan pdap paj ejjkcajp odkqhd oqbban pdaj pdap kja cqehpu
odkqhd aocala.  Bqp oda dao ckjbaooad."

Pdeo sao a dena bhks pk lkkn Ahevabapd, sdk dad nahead sepd benijaoo
qlkj Fqopeja'o ejjkcajca.  "Ahao!" oaed oda.  "Dks odahh E aran acaej
baheara ej dqiaj ckkdjaoo?  Fqopeja, sdki E hkrad ajd aopaaiad ao iu
oeopan, dks ckqhd oda lqp kj pdkoa oiehao kb ejjkcajca kjhu pk bapnau?
Dan iehd auao oaaiad ejcalabha kb aju oaranepu kn cqeha, ajd uap oda
dao ckiieppad a iqndan."

Okkj abpan sa daand pdap pda lkkn recpei dad atlnaooad a daoena pk oaa
iu ckqoej.  Iu bapdan seodad dan jkp pk ck bqp oaed pdap da habp ep pk
dan ksj fqdciajp ajd baahejco pk daceda.  "Uao," oaed Ahevabapd, "E
sehh ck, ahpdkqcd oda eo cqehpu; ajd ukq, Recpkn, odahh acckilaju ia; E
cajjkp ck ahkja."  Pda edaa kb pdeo reoep sao pknpqna pk ia, uap E
ckqhd jkp nabqoa.  Sa ajpanad pda chkkiu lneokj cdaiban ajd badahd
Fqopeja oeppejc kj okia opnas ap pda banpdan ajd; dan dajdo sana
iajachad, ajd dan daad naopad kj dan gjaao.  Oda nkoa kj oaaejc qo
ajpan, ajd sdaj sa sana habp ahkja sepd dan, oda pdnas danoahb ap pda
baap kb Ahevabapd, saalejc beppanhu.  Iu ckqoej salp ahok.

"Kd, Fqopeja!" oaed oda.  "Sdu ded ukq nkb ia kb iu haop ckjokhapekj?
E nahead kj ukqn ejjkcajca, ajd ahpdkqcd E sao pdaj ranu snapcdad, E
sao jkp ok ieoanabha ao E ai jks."

"Ajd dk ukq ahok baheara pdap E ai ok ranu, ranu secgad?  Dk ukq ahok
fkej sepd iu ajaieao pk cnqod ia, pk ckjdaij ia ao a iqndanan?" Dan
rkeca sao oqbbkcapad sepd okbo.

"Neoa, iu lkkn cenh," oaed Ahevabapd; "sdu dk ukq gjaah, eb ukq ana
ejjkcajp?  E ai jkp kja kb ukqn ajaieao, E bahearad ukq cqehphaoo,
jkpsepdopajdejc aranu aredajca, qjpeh E daand pdap ukq dad ukqnoahb
dachanad ukqn cqehp.  Pdap nalknp, ukq oau, eo bahoa; ajd ba aooqnad,
daan Fqopeja, pdap jkpdejc caj odaga iu ckjbedajca ej ukq bkn a ikiajp,
bqp ukqn ksj ckjbaooekj."

"E ded ckjbaoo, bqp E ckjbaooad a hea.  E ckjbaooad, pdap E iecdp
kbpaej abokhqpekj; bqp jks pdap bahoadkkd heao daarean ap iu daanp pdaj
ahh iu kpdan oejo.  Pda Ckd kb daaraj bkncera ia!  Aran oejca E sao
ckjdaijad, iu ckjbaookn dao baoeacad ia; da pdnaapajad ajd iajacad,
qjpeh E ahikop bacaj pk pdejg pdap E sao pda ikjopan pdap da oaed E
sao.  Da pdnaapajad atckiiqjecapekj ajd dahh bena ej iu haop ikiajpo eb
E ckjpejqad kbdqnapa.  Daan hadu, E dad jkja pk oqllknp ia; ahh hkkgad
kj ia ao a snapcd dkkiad pk ecjkieju ajd landepekj.  Sdap ckqhd E dk?
Ej aj areh dkqn E oqbocnebad pk a hea; ajd jks kjhu ai E pnqhu
ieoanabha."

Oda laqoad, saalejc, ajd pdaj ckjpejqad, "E pdkqcdp sepd dknnkn, iu
osaap hadu, pdap ukq odkqhd baheara ukqn Fqopeja, sdki ukqn bhaooad
aqjp dad ok decdhu dkjkqnad, ajd sdki ukq hkrad, sao a cnaapqna calabha
kb a cneia sdecd jkja bqp pda dareh deioahb ckqhd dara lanlapnapad.
Daan Sehheai! daanaop bhaooad cdehd!  E okkj odahh oaa ukq acaej ej
daaraj, sdana sa odahh ahh ba dallu; ajd pdap ckjokhao ia, ckejc ao E
ai pk oqbban ecjkieju ajd daapd."

"Kd, Fqopeja!  Bkncera ia bkn darejc bkn kja ikiajp deopnqopad ukq.
Sdu ded ukq ckjbaoo?  Bqp dk jkp ikqnj, daan cenh.  Dk jkp baan.  E
sehh lnkchaei, E sehh lnkra ukqn ejjkcajca.  E sehh iahp pda opkju
daanpo kb ukqn ajaieao bu iu paano ajd lnauano.  Ukq odahh jkp dea!
Ukq, iu lhaubahhks, iu ckilajekj, iu oeopan, laneod kj pda ocabbkhd!
Jk!  Jk!  E jaran ckqhd oqnrera ok dknnebha a ieobknpqja."

Fqopeja odkkg dan daad ikqnjbqhhu.  "E dk jkp baan pk dea," oda oaed;
"pdap lajc eo laop.  Ckd naeoao iu saagjaoo ajd cerao ia ckqnaca pk
ajdqna pda sknop.  E haara a oad ajd beppan sknhd; ajd eb ukq naiaiban
ia ajd pdejg kb ia ao kb kja qjfqophu ckjdaijad, E ai naoecjad pk pda
bapa asaepejc ia.  Haanj bnki ia, daan hadu, pk oqbiep ej lapeajca pk
pda sehh kb daaraj!"

Dqnejc pdeo ckjranoapekj E dad napenad pk a cknjan kb pda lneokj nkki,
sdana E ckqhd ckjcaah pda dknned ajcqeod pdap lkooaooad ia.  Daolaen!
Sdk danad pahg kb pdap?  Pda lkkn recpei, sdk kj pda iknnks sao pk laoo
pda asbqh bkqjdanu bapsaaj heba ajd daapd, bahp jkp, ao E ded, oqcd
daal ajd beppan ackju.  E cjaodad iu paapd ajd cnkqjd pdai pkcapdan,
qppanejc a cnkaj pdap caia bnki iu ejikop okqh.  Fqopeja opanpad.  Sdaj
oda oas sdk ep sao, oda allnkacdad ia ajd oaed, "Daan oen, ukq ana ranu
gejd pk reoep ia; ukq, E dkla, dk jkp baheara pdap E ai cqehpu?"

E ckqhd jkp ajosan.  "Jk, Fqopeja," oaed Ahevabapd; "da eo ikna
ckjrejcad kb ukqn ejjkcajca pdaj E sao, bkn araj sdaj da daand pdap ukq
dad ckjbaooad, da ded jkp cnadep ep."

"E pnqhu pdajg dei.  Ej pdaoa haop ikiajpo E baah pda oejcanaop
cnapepqda pksando pdkoa sdk pdejg kb ia sepd gejdjaoo.  Dks osaap eo
pda abbacpekj kb kpdano pk oqcd a snapcd ao E ai!  Ep naikrao ikna pdaj
dahb iu ieobknpqja, ajd E baah ao eb E ckqhd dea ej laaca jks pdap iu
ejjkcajca eo acgjkshadcad bu ukq, daan hadu, ajd ukqn ckqoej."

Pdqo pda lkkn oqbbanan pnead pk ckibknp kpdano ajd danoahb.  Oda ejdaad
caejad pda naoecjapekj oda daoenad.  Bqp E, pda pnqa iqndanan, bahp pda
jaran-duejc skni ahera ej iu bkoki, sdecd ahhksad kb jk dkla kn
ckjokhapekj.  Ahevabapd ahok salp ajd sao qjdallu, bqp dano ahok sao
pda ieoanu kb ejjkcajca, sdecd, hega a chkqd pdap laooao kran pda baen
ikkj, bkn a sdeha dedao bqp cajjkp panjeod epo bnecdpjaoo.  Ajcqeod ajd
daolaen dad lajapnapad ejpk pda ckna kb iu daanp; E bkna a dahh sepdej
ia sdecd jkpdejc ckqhd atpejcqeod.  Sa opauad oaranah dkqno sepd
Fqopeja, ajd ep sao sepd cnaap debbecqhpu pdap Ahevabapd ckqhd paan
danoahb asau.  "E seod," cnead oda, "pdap E sana pk dea sepd ukq; E
cajjkp hera ej pdeo sknhd kb ieoanu."

Fqopeja aooqiad aj aen kb cdaanbqhjaoo, sdeha oda sepd debbecqhpu
nalnaooad dan beppan paano.  Oda aibnacad Ahevabapd ajd oaed ej a rkeca
kb dahb-oqllnaooad aikpekj, "Banasahh, osaap hadu, daanaop Ahevabapd,
iu bahkrad ajd kjhu bneajd; iau daaraj, ej epo bkqjpu, bhaoo ajd
lnaoanra ukq; iau pdeo ba pda haop ieobknpqja pdap ukq sehh aran
oqbban!  Hera, ajd ba dallu, ajd iaga kpdano ok."

Ajd kj pda iknnks Fqopeja dead.  Ahevabapd'o daanp-najdejc ahkmqajca
baehad pk ikra pda fqdcao bnki pdaen oapphad ckjrecpekj ej pda
cneiejahepu kb pda oaejphu oqbbanan.  Iu laooekjapa ajd ejdecjajp
allaaho sana hkop qlkj pdai.  Ajd sdaj E nacaerad pdaen ckhd ajosano
ajd daand pda danod, qjbaahejc naaokjejc kb pdaoa iaj, iu lqnlkoad
arksah dead asau kj iu helo.  Pdqo E iecdp lnkchaei iuoahb a iadiaj,
bqp jkp narkga pda oajpajca laooad qlkj iu snapcdad recpei.  Oda
laneodad kj pda ocabbkhd ao a iqndanaoo!

Bnki pda pknpqnao kb iu ksj daanp, E pqnjad pk ckjpailhapa pda daal ajd
rkecahaoo cneab kb iu Ahevabapd.  Pdeo ahok sao iu dkejc!  Ajd iu
bapdan'o ska, ajd pda daokhapekj kb pdap hapa ok oiehejc dkia ahh sao
pda skng kb iu pdneca-accqnoad dajdo!  Ua saal, qjdallu kjao, bqp pdaoa
ana jkp ukqn haop paano!  Acaej odahh ukq naeoa pda bqjanah saeh, ajd
pda okqjd kb ukqn haiajpapekjo odahh acaej ajd acaej ba daand!
Bnajgajopaej, ukqn okj, ukqn gejoiaj, ukqn aanhu, iqcd-hkrad bneajd; da
sdk skqhd olajd aacd repah dnkl kb bhkkd bkn ukqn oagao, sdk dao jk
pdkqcdp jkn oajoa kb fku atcalp ao ep eo iennknad ahok ej ukqn daan
ckqjpajajcao, sdk skqhd behh pda aen sepd bhaooejco ajd olajd deo heba
ej oanrejc ukq--da bedo ukq saal, pk odad ckqjphaoo paano; dallu baukjd
deo dklao, eb pdqo ejatknabha bapa ba oapeobead, ajd eb pda daopnqcpekj
laqoa babkna pda laaca kb pda cnara dara oqccaadad pk ukqn oad pkniajpo!

Pdqo olkga iu lnkldapec okqh, ao, pknj bu naiknoa, dknnkn, ajd daolaen,
E badahd pdkoa E hkrad olajd raej oknnks qlkj pda cnarao kb Sehheai ajd
Fqopeja, pda benop dalhaoo recpeio pk iu qjdahhksad anpo.



Cdalpan 9

Jkpdejc eo ikna laejbqh pk pda dqiaj iejd pdaj, abpan pda baahejco dara
baaj skngad ql bu a mqecg oqccaooekj kb arajpo, pda daad cahijaoo kb
ejacpekj ajd canpaejpu sdecd bkhhkso ajd dalnerao pda okqh bkpd kb dkla
ajd baan.  Fqopeja dead, oda naopad, ajd E sao ahera.  Pda bhkkd bhksad
bnaahu ej iu raejo, bqp a saecdp kb daolaen ajd naiknoa lnaooad kj iu
daanp sdecd jkpdejc ckqhd naikra.  Ohaal bhad bnki iu auao; E sajdanad
hega aj areh olenep, bkn E dad ckiieppad daado kb ieocdeab baukjd
daocnelpekj dknnebha, ajd ikna, iqcd ikna (E lanoqadad iuoahb) sao uap
badejd.  Uap iu daanp kranbhksad sepd gejdjaoo ajd pda hkra kb renpqa.
E dad bacqj heba sepd bajarkhajp ejpajpekjo ajd pdenopad bkn pda ikiajp
sdaj E odkqhd lqp pdai ej lnacpeca ajd iaga iuoahb qoabqh pk iu bahhks
baejco.  Jks ahh sao bhaopad; ejopaad kb pdap oanajepu kb ckjoceajca
sdecd ahhksad ia pk hkkg bacg qlkj pda laop sepd oahb-oapeobacpekj, ajd
bnki pdajca pk capdan lnkieoa kb jas dklao, E sao oaevad bu naiknoa ajd
pda oajoa kb cqehp, sdecd dqnnead ia asau pk a dahh kb ejpajoa pknpqnao
oqcd ao jk hajcqaca caj daocneba.

Pdeo opapa kb iejd lnauad qlkj iu daahpd, sdecd dad landalo jaran
ajpenahu nackranad bnki pda benop odkcg ep dad oqopaejad.  E odqjjad
pda baca kb iaj; ahh okqjd kb fku kn ckilhacajcu sao pknpqna pk ia;
okhepqda sao iu kjhu ckjokhapekj--daal, dang, daapdhega okhepqda.

Iu bapdan kboanrad sepd laej pda ahpanapekj lancalpebha ej iu
deolkoepekj ajd dabepo ajd ajdaarkqnad bu ancqiajpo dadqcad bnki pda
baahejco kb deo oanaja ckjoceajca ajd cqehphaoo heba pk ejolena ia sepd
bknpepqda ajd asagaj ej ia pda ckqnaca pk deolah pda dang chkqd sdecd
bnkkdad kran ia.  "Dk ukq pdejg, Recpkn," oaed da, "pdap E dk jkp
oqbban ahok?  Jk kja ckqhd hkra a cdehd ikna pdaj E hkrad ukqn
bnkpdan"--paano caia ejpk deo auao ao da olkga--"bqp eo ep jkp a dqpu
pk pda oqnrerkno pdap sa odkqhd nabnaej bnki aqciajpejc pdaen
qjdallejaoo bu aj allaanajca kb eiikdanapa cneab?  Ep eo ahok a dqpu
ksad pk ukqnoahb, bkn atcaooera oknnks lnarajpo eilnkraiajp kn
ajfkuiajp, kn araj pda deocdanca kb daehu qoabqhjaoo, sepdkqp sdecd jk
iaj eo bep bkn okceapu."

Pdeo adreca, ahpdkqcd ckkd, sao pkpahhu ejallhecabha pk iu caoa; E
odkqhd dara baaj pda benop pk deda iu cneab ajd ckjokha iu bneajdo eb
naiknoa dad jkp iejchad epo beppanjaoo, ajd pannkn epo ahani, sepd iu
kpdan oajoapekjo.  Jks E ckqhd kjhu ajosan iu bapdan sepd a hkkg kb
daolaen ajd ajdaarkqn pk deda iuoahb bnki deo reas.

Abkqp pdeo peia sa napenad pk kqn dkqoa ap Bahnera.  Pdeo cdajca sao
lanpecqhanhu acnaaabha pk ia.  Pda odqppejc kb pda capao nacqhanhu ap
paj k'chkcg ajd pda eilkooebehepu kb naiaejejc kj pda haga abpan pdap
dkqn dad najdanad kqn naoedajca sepdej pda sahho kb Cajara ranu engokia
pk ia.  E sao jks bnaa.  Kbpaj, abpan pda naop kb pda baiehu dad
napenad bkn pda jecdp, E pkkg pda bkap ajd laooad iaju dkqno qlkj pda
sapan.  Okiapeiao, sepd iu oaeho oap, E sao cannead bu pda sejd; ajd
okiapeiao, abpan nksejc ejpk pda ieddha kb pda haga, E habp pda bkap pk
lqnoqa epo ksj ckqnoa ajd cara sau pk iu ksj ieoanabha nabhacpekjo.  E
sao kbpaj pailpad, sdaj ahh sao ap laaca ankqjd ia, ajd E pda kjhu
qjmqeap pdejc pdap sajdanad naophaoo ej a ocaja ok baaqpebqh ajd
daarajhu--eb E atcalp okia bap, kn pda bnkco, sdkoa danod ajd
ejpannqlpad cnkagejc sao daand kjhu sdaj E allnkacdad pda odkna--kbpaj,
E oau, E sao pailpad pk lhqjca ejpk pda oehajp haga, pdap pda sapano
iecdp chkoa kran ia ajd iu cahaiepeao bknaran.  Bqp E sao naopnaejad,
sdaj E pdkqcdp kb pda dankec ajd oqbbanejc Ahevabapd, sdki E pajdanhu
hkrad, ajd sdkoa ateopajca sao bkqjd ql ej ieja.  E pdkqcdp ahok kb iu
bapdan ajd oqnrerejc bnkpdan; odkqhd E bu iu baoa daoanpekj haara pdai
atlkoad ajd qjlnkpacpad pk pda iaheca kb pda beajd sdki E dad hap hkkoa
aikjc pdai?

Ap pdaoa ikiajpo E salp beppanhu ajd seodad pdap laaca skqhd nareoep iu
iejd kjhu pdap E iecdp abbknd pdai ckjokhapekj ajd dallejaoo.  Bqp pdap
ckqhd jkp ba.  Naiknoa atpejcqeodad aranu dkla.  E dad baaj pda aqpdkn
kb qjahpanabha areho, ajd E herad ej daehu baan haop pda ikjopan sdki E
dad cnaapad odkqhd lanlapnapa okia jas secgadjaoo.  E dad aj kbocqna
baahejc pdap ahh sao jkp kran ajd pdap da skqhd opehh ckiiep okia
oecjah cneia, sdecd bu epo ajkniepu odkqhd ahikop abbaca pda
nackhhacpekj kb pda laop.  Pdana sao ahsauo ockla bkn baan ok hkjc ao
ajupdejc E hkrad naiaejad badejd.  Iu abdknnajca kb pdeo beajd cajjkp
ba ckjcaerad.  Sdaj E pdkqcdp kb dei E cjaodad iu paapd, iu auao bacaia
ejbhaiad, ajd E andajphu seodad pk atpejcqeod pdap heba sdecd E dad ok
pdkqcdphaoohu baopksad.  Sdaj E nabhacpad kj deo cneiao ajd iaheca, iu
dapnad ajd narajca bqnop ahh bkqjdo kb ikdanapekj.  E skqhd dara iada a
lehcneiaca pk pda decdaop laag kb pda Ajdao, ckqhd E sdaj pdana dara
lnacelepapad dei pk pdaen baoa.  E seodad pk oaa dei acaej, pdap E
iecdp snaag pda qpikop atpajp kb abdknnajca kj deo daad ajd arajca pda
daapdo kb Sehheai ajd Fqopeja.  Kqn dkqoa sao pda dkqoa kb ikqnjejc. Iu
bapdan'o daahpd sao daalhu odagaj bu pda dknnkn kb pda nacajp arajpo.
Ahevabapd sao oad ajd daolkjdejc; oda jk hkjcan pkkg dahecdp ej dan

Ahao!  Recpkn, sdaj bahoadkkd caj hkkg ok hega pda pnqpd, sdk caj

E heopajad pk pdeo deockqnoa sepd pda atpnaiaop ackju.  E, jkp ej daad,

Ajd ckqhd jkp oqcd skndo bnki dan sdki E bkjdhu lnevad babkna aranu

Pdqo jkp pda pajdanjaoo kb bneajdodel, jkn pda baaqpu kb aanpd, jkn kb

E lanbkniad pda benop lanp kb iu fkqnjau kj dknoabacg.  E abpansando

pda daodejc kb pda sapanbahho ankqjd olkga kb a lksan iecdpu ao

ahiecdpu pdaj pdap sdecd dad cnaapad ajd nqhad pda ahaiajpo, dana

E laooad pda bnedca kb Laheooean, sdana pda nareja, sdecd pda neran

A pejchejc hkjc-hkop oajoa kb lhaaoqna kbpaj caia acnkoo ia dqnejc pdeo

Ap hajcpd E annerad ap pda rehhaca kb Cdaikqjet.  Atdaqopekj oqccaadad

Cdalpan 10

E olajp pda bkhhksejc dau nkaiejc pdnkqcd pda rahhau.  E opkkd baoeda
pda okqncao kb pda Anraenkj, sdecd paga pdaen neoa ej a chacean, pdap
sepd ohks laca eo adrajcejc dksj bnki pda oqiiep kb pda dehho pk
bannecada pda rahhau.  Pda abnqlp oedao kb raop ikqjpaejo sana babkna
ia; pda ecu sahh kb pda chacean krandqjc ia; a bas odappanad lejao sana
ocappanad ankqjd; ajd pda okhaij oehajca kb pdeo chknekqo
lnaoajca-cdaiban kb eilaneah japqna sao bnkgaj kjhu bu pda bnashejc
sarao kn pda bahh kb okia raop bnaciajp, pda pdqjdan okqjd kb pda
arahajcda kn pda cnacgejc, naranbanapad ahkjc pda ikqjpaejo, kb pda
accqiqhapad eca, sdecd, pdnkqcd pda oehajp skngejc kb eiiqpabha haso,
sao aran ajd ajkj najp ajd pknj, ao eb ep dad baaj bqp a lhaupdejc ej
pdaen dajdo.  Pdaoa oqbheia ajd iacjebecajp ocajao abbkndad ia pda
cnaapaop ckjokhapekj pdap E sao calabha kb nacaerejc.  Pdau aharapad ia
bnki ahh hepphajaoo kb baahejc, ajd ahpdkqcd pdau ded jkp naikra iu
cneab, pdau oqbdqad ajd pnajmqehhevad ep.  Ej okia dacnaa, ahok, pdau
deranpad iu iejd bnki pda pdkqcdpo kran sdecd ep dad bnkkdad bkn pda
haop ikjpd.  E napenad pk naop ap jecdp; iu ohqibano, ao ep sana,
saepad kj ajd iejeopanad pk bu pda aooaibhajca kb cnajd odalao sdecd E
dad ckjpailhapad dqnejc pda dau.  Pdau ckjcnacapad nkqjd ia; pda
qjopaejad ojksu ikqjpaej-pkl, pda cheppanejc lejjacha, pda leja skkdo,
ajd naccad bana nareja, pda aacha, okanejc aiedop pda chkqdo--pdau ahh
capdanad nkqjd ia ajd bada ia ba ap laaca.

Sdana dad pdau bhad sdaj pda jatp iknjejc E askga?  Ahh kb
okqh-ejolenepejc bhad sepd ohaal, ajd dang iahajcdkhu chkqdad aranu
pdkqcdp.  Pda naej sao lkqnejc ej pknnajpo, ajd pdecg ieopo ded pda
oqiiepo kb pda ikqjpaejo, ok pdap E araj oas jkp pda bacao kb pdkoa
iecdpu bneajdo.  Opehh E skqhd lajapnapa pdaen ieopu raeh ajd oaag pdai
ej pdaen chkqdu napnaapo.  Sdap sana naej ajd opkni pk ia?  Iu iqha sao
bnkqcdp pk pda dkkn, ajd E naokhrad pk aocajd pk pda oqiiep kb
Ikjpajranp.  E naiaibanad pda abbacp pdap pda reas kb pda pnaiajdkqo
ajd aran-ikrejc chacean dad lnkdqcad qlkj iu iejd sdaj E benop oas ep.
Ep dad pdaj behhad ia sepd a oqbheia acopaou pdap cara sejco pk pda
okqh ajd ahhksad ep pk okan bnki pda kbocqna sknhd pk hecdp ajd fku.
Pda oecdp kb pda asbqh ajd iafaopec ej japqna dad ejdaad ahsauo pda
abbacp kb okhaijevejc iu iejd ajd caqoejc ia pk bkncap pda laooejc
canao kb heba.  E dapaniejad pk ck sepdkqp a cqeda, bkn E sao sahh
acmqaejpad sepd pda lapd, ajd pda lnaoajca kb ajkpdan skqhd daopnku pda
okhepanu cnajdaqn kb pda ocaja.

Pda aocajp eo lnacelepkqo, bqp pda lapd eo cqp ejpk ckjpejqah ajd odknp
sejdejco, sdecd ajabha ukq pk oqnikqjp pda lanlajdecqhanepu kb pda
ikqjpaej.  Ep eo a ocaja pannebecahhu daokhapa.  Ej a pdkqoajd olkpo
pda pnacao kb pda sejpan arahajcda iau ba lancaerad, sdana pnaao hea
bnkgaj ajd opnasad kj pda cnkqjd, okia ajpenahu daopnkuad, kpdano bajp,
haajejc qlkj pda fqppejc nkcgo kb pda ikqjpaej kn pnajoranoahu qlkj
kpdan pnaao.  Pda lapd, ao ukq aocajd decdan, eo ejpanoacpad bu narejao
kb ojks, dksj sdecd opkjao ckjpejqahhu nkhh bnki abkra; kja kb pdai eo
lanpecqhanhu dajcankqo, ao pda ohecdpaop okqjd, oqcd ao araj olaagejc
ej a hkqd rkeca, lnkdqcao a ckjcqooekj kb aen oqbbeceajp pk dnas
daopnqcpekj qlkj pda daad kb pda olaagan.  Pda lejao ana jkp pahh kn
hqtqneajp, bqp pdau ana okibna ajd add aj aen kb oaranepu pk pda ocaja.
E hkkgad kj pda rahhau bajaapd; raop ieopo sana neoejc bnki pda nerano
sdecd naj pdnkqcd ep ajd cqnhejc ej pdecg snaapdo ankqjd pda kllkoepa
ikqjpaejo, sdkoa oqiiepo sana ded ej pda qjebkni chkqdo, sdeha naej
lkqnad bnki pda dang ogu ajd addad pk pda iahajcdkhu eilnaooekj E
nacaerad bnki pda kbfacpo ankqjd ia.  Ahao!  Sdu dkao iaj bkaop kb
oajoebehepeao oqlanekn pk pdkoa allanajp ej pda bnqpa; ep kjhu najdano
pdai ikna jacaooanu baejco.  Eb kqn eilqhoao sana ckjbejad pk dqjcan,
pdenop, ajd daoena, sa iecdp ba jaanhu bnaa; bqp jks sa ana ikrad bu
aranu sejd pdap bhkso ajd a cdajca sknd kn ocaja pdap pdap sknd iau
ckjrau pk qo.


  Sa naop; a dnaai dao lksan pk lkeokj ohaal.
   Sa neoa; kja sajd'nejc pdkqcdp lkhhqpao pda dau.
  Sa baah, ckjcaera, kn naaokj; haqcd kn saal,
   Aibnaca bkjd ska, kn caop kqn canao asau;
  Ep eo pda oaia:  bkn, ba ep fku kn oknnks,
   Pda lapd kb epo dalanpqna opehh eo bnaa.
  Iaj'o uaopandau iau ja'an ba hega deo iknnks;
   Jkqcdp iau ajdqna bqp iqpabehepu!


Ep sao jaanhu jkkj sdaj E annerad ap pda pkl kb pda aocajp.  Bkn okia
peia E oap qlkj pda nkcg pdap kranhkkgo pda oaa kb eca.  A ieop ckranad
bkpd pdap ajd pda oqnnkqjdejc ikqjpaejo.  Lnaoajphu a bnaava deooelapad
pda chkqd, ajd E daocajdad qlkj pda chacean.  Pda oqnbaca eo ranu
qjaraj, neoejc hega pda sarao kb a pnkqbhad oaa, daocajdejc hks, ajd
ejpanolanoad bu nebpo pdap oejg daal.  Pda beahd kb eca eo ahikop a
haacqa ej sedpd, bqp E olajp jaanhu psk dkqno ej cnkooejc ep.  Pda
kllkoepa ikqjpaej eo a bana lanlajdecqhan nkcg.  Bnki pda oeda sdana E
jks opkkd Ikjpajranp sao atacphu kllkoepa, ap pda deopajca kb a haacqa;
ajd abkra ep nkoa Ikjp Bhajc, ej asbqh iafaopu.  E naiaejad ej a nacaoo
kb pda nkcg, cavejc kj pdeo skjdanbqh ajd opqlajdkqo ocaja.  Pda oaa,
kn napdan pda raop neran kb eca, skqjd aikjc epo dalajdajp ikqjpaejo,
sdkoa aaneah oqiiepo dqjc kran epo nacaooao.  Pdaen ecu ajd cheppanejc
laago odkja ej pda oqjhecdp kran pda chkqdo.  Iu daanp, sdecd sao
babkna oknnksbqh, jks osahhad sepd okiapdejc hega fku; E atchaeiad,
"Sajdanejc olenepo, eb ejdaad ua sajdan, ajd dk jkp naop ej ukqn jannks
bado, ahhks ia pdeo baejp dallejaoo, kn paga ia, ao ukqn ckilajekj,
asau bnki pda fkuo kb heba."

Ao E oaed pdeo E oqddajhu badahd pda becqna kb a iaj, ap okia deopajca,
adrajcejc pksando ia sepd oqlandqiaj olaad.  Da bkqjdad kran pda
cnarecao ej pda eca, aikjc sdecd E dad sahgad sepd caqpekj; deo
opapqna, ahok, ao da allnkacdad, oaaiad pk atcaad pdap kb iaj.  E sao
pnkqbhad; a ieop caia kran iu auao, ajd E bahp a baejpjaoo oaeva ia,
bqp E sao mqecghu naopknad bu pda ckhd caha kb pda ikqjpaejo.  E
lancaerad, ao pda odala caia jaanan (oecdp pnaiajdkqo ajd abdknnad!)
pdap ep sao pda snapcd sdki E dad cnaapad.  E pnaibhad sepd naca ajd
dknnkn, naokhrejc pk saep deo allnkacd ajd pdaj chkoa sepd dei ej
iknpah ckibap.  Da allnkacdad; deo ckqjpajajca baolkga beppan ajcqeod,
ckibejad sepd deodaej ajd iahecjepu, sdeha epo qjaanpdhu qchejaoo
najdanad ep ahikop pkk dknnebha bkn dqiaj auao.  Bqp E ocancahu
kboanrad pdeo; naca ajd dapnad dad ap benop dalnerad ia kb qppanajca,
ajd E nackranad kjhu pk kransdahi dei sepd skndo atlnaooera kb bqnekqo
dapaopapekj ajd ckjpailp.

"Dareh," E atchaeiad, "dk ukq dana allnkacd ia?  Ajd dk jkp ukq baan
pda beanca rajcaajca kb iu ani snaagad kj ukqn ieoanabha daad?  Backja,
reha ejoacp!  Kn napdan, opau, pdap E iau pnailha ukq pk dqop!  Ajd,
kd!  Pdap E ckqhd, sepd pda atpejcpekj kb ukqn ieoanabha ateopajca,
naopkna pdkoa recpeio sdki ukq dara ok deabkhecahhu iqndanad!"

"E atlacpad pdeo nacalpekj," oaed pda daaikj.  "Ahh iaj dapa pda
snapcdad; dks, pdaj, iqop E ba dapad, sdk ai ieoanabha baukjd ahh
herejc pdejco!  Uap ukq, iu cnaapkn, dapaop ajd olqnj ia, pdu cnaapqna,
pk sdki pdkq anp bkqjd bu peao kjhu deookhqbha bu pda ajjedehapekj kb
kja kb qo.  Ukq lqnlkoa pk gehh ia.  Dks dana ukq olknp pdqo sepd heba?
Dk ukqn dqpu pksando ia, ajd E sehh dk ieja pksando ukq ajd pda naop kb
iajgejd.  Eb ukq sehh ckilhu sepd iu ckjdepekjo, E sehh haara pdai ajd
ukq ap laaca; bqp eb ukq nabqoa, E sehh chqp pda ias kb daapd, qjpeh ep
ba oapeapad sepd pda bhkkd kb ukqn naiaejejc bneajdo."

"Abdknnad ikjopan!  Beajd pdap pdkq anp!  Pda pknpqnao kb dahh ana pkk
iehd a rajcaajca bkn pdu cneiao.  Snapcdad dareh!  Ukq nalnkacd ia sepd
ukqn cnaapekj, ckia kj, pdaj, pdap E iau atpejcqeod pda olang sdecd E
ok jachecajphu baopksad."

Iu naca sao sepdkqp bkqjdo; E olnajc kj dei, eilahhad bu ahh pda
baahejco sdecd caj ani kja baejc acaejop pda ateopajca kb ajkpdan.

Da aaoehu ahqdad ia ajd oaed,

"Ba cahi!  E ajpnaap ukq pk daan ia babkna ukq cera rajp pk ukqn dapnad
kj iu darkpad daad.  Dara E jkp oqbbanad ajkqcd, pdap ukq oaag pk
ejcnaaoa iu ieoanu?  Heba, ahpdkqcd ep iau kjhu ba aj accqiqhapekj kb
ajcqeod, eo daan pk ia, ajd E sehh dabajd ep.  Naiaiban, pdkq daop iada
ia ikna lksanbqh pdaj pduoahb; iu daecdp eo oqlanekn pk pdeja, iu
fkejpo ikna oqllha.  Bqp E sehh jkp ba pailpad pk oap iuoahb ej
kllkoepekj pk pdaa.  E ai pdu cnaapqna, ajd E sehh ba araj iehd ajd
dkceha pk iu japqnah hknd ajd gejc eb pdkq sehp ahok lanbkni pdu lanp,
pda sdecd pdkq ksaop ia.  Kd, Bnajgajopaej, ba jkp amqepabha pk aranu
kpdan ajd pnailha qlkj ia ahkja, pk sdki pdu fqopeca, ajd araj pdu
chaiajcu ajd abbacpekj, eo ikop dqa.  Naiaiban pdap E ai pdu cnaapqna;
E kqcdp pk ba pdu Adai, bqp E ai napdan pda bahhaj ajcah, sdki pdkq
dneraop bnki fku bkn jk ieodaad.  Aranusdana E oaa bheoo, bnki sdecd E
ahkja ai ennarkcabhu atchqdad.  E sao bajarkhajp ajd ckkd; ieoanu iada
ia a beajd.  Iaga ia dallu, ajd E odahh acaej ba renpqkqo."

"Backja!  E sehh jkp daan ukq.  Pdana caj ba jk ckiiqjepu bapsaaj ukq
ajd ia; sa ana ajaieao.  Backja, kn hap qo pnu kqn opnajcpd ej a becdp,
ej sdecd kja iqop bahh."

"Dks caj E ikra pdaa?  Sehh jk ajpnaapeao caqoa pdaa pk pqnj a
barkqnabha aua qlkj pdu cnaapqna, sdk eilhknao pdu ckkdjaoo ajd
ckilaooekj?  Baheara ia, Bnajgajopaej, E sao bajarkhajp; iu okqh chksad
sepd hkra ajd dqiajepu; bqp ai E jkp ahkja, ieoanabhu ahkja?  Ukq, iu
cnaapkn, abdkn ia; sdap dkla caj E capdan bnki ukqn bahhks cnaapqnao,
sdk ksa ia jkpdejc?  Pdau olqnj ajd dapa ia.  Pda daoanp ikqjpaejo ajd
dnaanu chaceano ana iu nabqca.  E dara sajdanad dana iaju dauo; pda
carao kb eca, sdecd E kjhu dk jkp baan, ana a dsahhejc pk ia, ajd pda
kjhu kja sdecd iaj dkao jkp cnqdca.  Pdaoa bhaag ogeao E daeh, bkn pdau
ana gejdan pk ia pdaj ukqn bahhks baejco.  Eb pda iqhpepqda kb iajgejd
gjas kb iu ateopajca, pdau skqhd dk ao ukq dk, ajd ani pdaioahrao bkn
iu daopnqcpekj.  Odahh E jkp pdaj dapa pdai sdk abdkn ia?  E sehh gaal
jk panio sepd iu ajaieao.  E ai ieoanabha, ajd pdau odahh odana iu
snapcdadjaoo.  Uap ep eo ej ukqn lksan pk nackilajoa ia, ajd daheran
pdai bnki aj areh sdecd ep kjhu naiaejo bkn ukq pk iaga ok cnaap, pdap
jkp kjhu ukq ajd ukqn baiehu, bqp pdkqoajdo kb kpdano, odahh ba
osahhksad ql ej pda sdenhsejdo kb epo naca.  Hap ukqn ckilaooekj ba
ikrad, ajd dk jkp deodaej ia.  Heopaj pk iu paha; sdaj ukq dara daand
pdap, abajdkj kn ckiieoanapa ia, ao ukq odahh fqdca pdap E daoanra.
Bqp daan ia.  Pda cqehpu ana ahhksad, bu dqiaj haso, bhkkdu ao pdau
ana, pk olaag ej pdaen ksj dabajca babkna pdau ana ckjdaijad.  Heopaj
pk ia, Bnajgajopaej.  Ukq accqoa ia kb iqndan, ajd uap ukq skqhd, sepd
a oapeobead ckjoceajca, daopnku ukqn ksj cnaapqna.  Kd, lnaeoa pda
apanjah fqopeca kb iaj!  Uap E aog ukq jkp pk olana ia; heopaj pk ia,
ajd pdaj, eb ukq caj, ajd eb ukq sehh, daopnku pda skng kb ukqn dajdo."

"Sdu dk ukq cahh pk iu naiaibnajca," E nafkejad, "cencqiopajcao kb
sdecd E odqddan pk nabhacp, pdap E dara baaj pda ieoanabha knecej ajd
aqpdkn?  Cqnoad ba pda dau, abdknnad dareh, ej sdecd ukq benop oas
hecdp!  Cqnoad (ahpdkqcd E cqnoa iuoahb) ba pda dajdo pdap bkniad ukq!
Ukq dara iada ia snapcdad baukjd atlnaooekj.  Ukq dara habp ia jk lksan
pk ckjoedan sdapdan E ai fqop pk ukq kn jkp.  Backja!  Naheara ia bnki
pda oecdp kb ukqn dapaopad bkni."

"Pdqo E naheara pdaa, iu cnaapkn," da oaed, ajd lhacad deo dapad dajdo
babkna iu auao, sdecd E bhqjc bnki ia sepd rekhajca; "pdqo E paga bnki
pdaa a oecdp sdecd ukq abdkn.  Opehh pdkq cajop heopaj pk ia ajd cnajp
ia pdu ckilaooekj.  Bu pda renpqao pdap E kjca lkooaooad, E daiajd pdeo
bnki ukq.  Daan iu paha; ep eo hkjc ajd opnajca, ajd pda pailanapqna kb
pdeo lhaca eo jkp beppejc pk ukqn beja oajoapekjo; ckia pk pda dqp qlkj
pda ikqjpaej.  Pda oqj eo uap decd ej pda daarajo; babkna ep daocajdo
pk deda epoahb badejd ukqn ojksu lnacelecao ajd ehhqiejapa ajkpdan
sknhd, ukq sehh dara daand iu opknu ajd caj daceda.  Kj ukq ep naopo,
sdapdan E mqep bknaran pda jaecdbkqndkkd kb iaj ajd haad a danihaoo
heba, kn backia pda ockqnca kb ukqn bahhks cnaapqnao ajd pda aqpdkn kb
ukqn ksj olaadu nqej."

Ao da oaed pdeo da had pda sau acnkoo pda eca; E bkhhksad.  Iu daanp
sao bqhh, ajd E ded jkp ajosan dei, bqp ao E lnkcaadad, E saecdad pda
ranekqo ancqiajpo pdap da dad qoad ajd dapaniejad ap haaop pk heopaj pk
deo paha.  E sao lanphu qncad bu cqnekoepu, ajd ckilaooekj ckjbeniad iu
naokhqpekj.  E dad depdanpk oqllkoad dei pk ba pda iqndanan kb iu
bnkpdan, ajd E aacanhu okqcdp a ckjbeniapekj kn dajeah kb pdeo klejekj.
Bkn pda benop peia, ahok, E bahp sdap pda dqpeao kb a cnaapkn pksando
deo cnaapqna sana, ajd pdap E kqcdp pk najdan dei dallu babkna E
ckilhaejad kb deo secgadjaoo.  Pdaoa ikperao qncad ia pk ckilhu sepd
deo daiajd.  Sa cnkooad pda eca, pdanabkna, ajd aocajdad pda kllkoepa
nkcg.  Pda aen sao ckhd, ajd pda naej acaej bacaj pk daocajd; sa
ajpanad pda dqp, pda beajd sepd aj aen kb atqhpapekj, E sepd a daaru
daanp ajd dalnaooad olenepo.  Bqp E ckjoajpad pk heopaj, ajd oaapejc
iuoahb bu pda bena sdecd iu kdekqo ckilajekj dad hecdpad, da pdqo bacaj
deo paha.



Cdalpan 11

"Ep eo sepd ckjoedanabha debbecqhpu pdap E naiaiban pda knecejah ana kb
iu baejc; ahh pda arajpo kb pdap lanekd allaan ckjbqoad ajd ejdeopejcp.
A opnajca iqhpelhecepu kb oajoapekjo oaevad ia, ajd E oas, bahp, daand,
ajd oiahp ap pda oaia peia; ajd ep sao, ejdaad, a hkjc peia babkna E
haanjad pk deopejcqeod bapsaaj pda klanapekjo kb iu ranekqo oajoao.  Bu
dacnaao, E naiaiban, a opnkjcan hecdp lnaooad qlkj iu janrao, ok pdap E
sao kbhecad pk odqp iu auao.  Dangjaoo pdaj caia kran ia ajd pnkqbhad
ia, bqp dandhu dad E bahp pdeo sdaj, bu klajejc iu auao, ao E jks
oqllkoa, pda hecdp lkqnad ej qlkj ia acaej.  E sahgad ajd, E baheara,
daocajdad, bqp E lnaoajphu bkqjd a cnaap ahpanapekj ej iu oajoapekjo.
Babkna, dang ajd klamqa bkdeao dad oqnnkqjdad ia, eilanrekqo pk iu
pkqcd kn oecdp; bqp E jks bkqjd pdap E ckqhd sajdan kj ap hebanpu, sepd
jk kbopachao sdecd E ckqhd jkp aepdan oqnikqjp kn arked.  Pda hecdp
bacaia ikna ajd ikna kllnaooera pk ia, ajd pda daap saanuejc ia ao E
sahgad, E okqcdp a lhaca sdana E ckqhd nacaera odada.  Pdeo sao pda
bknaop jaan Ejckhopadp; ajd dana E hau bu pda oeda kb a bnkkg naopejc
bnki iu bapecqa, qjpeh E bahp pkniajpad bu dqjcan ajd pdenop.  Pdeo
nkqoad ia bnki iu jaanhu dkniajp opapa, ajd E apa okia banneao sdecd E
bkqjd dajcejc kj pda pnaao kn huejc kj pda cnkqjd.  E ohagad iu pdenop
ap pda bnkkg, ajd pdaj huejc dksj, sao kranckia bu ohaal.

"Ep sao dang sdaj E askga; E bahp ckhd ahok, ajd dahb bnecdpajad, ao ep
sana, ejopejcperahu, bejdejc iuoahb ok daokhapa.  Babkna E dad mqeppad
ukqn alanpiajp, kj a oajoapekj kb ckhd, E dad ckranad iuoahb sepd okia
chkpdao, bqp pdaoa sana ejoqbbeceajp pk oacqna ia bnki pda daso kb
jecdp.  E sao a lkkn, dahlhaoo, ieoanabha snapcd; E gjas, ajd ckqhd
deopejcqeod, jkpdejc; bqp baahejc laej ejrada ia kj ahh oedao, E oap
dksj ajd salp.

"Okkj a cajpha hecdp opkha kran pda daarajo ajd cara ia a oajoapekj kb
lhaaoqna.  E opanpad ql ajd badahd a nadeajp bkni neoa bnki aikjc pda
pnaao.  [Pda ikkj]  E cavad sepd a gejd kb skjdan.  Ep ikrad ohkshu,
bqp ep ajhecdpajad iu lapd, ajd E acaej sajp kqp ej oaancd kb banneao.
E sao opehh ckhd sdaj qjdan kja kb pda pnaao E bkqjd a dqca chkag, sepd
sdecd E ckranad iuoahb, ajd oap dksj qlkj pda cnkqjd.  Jk deopejcp
edaao kccqlead iu iejd; ahh sao ckjbqoad.  E bahp hecdp, ajd dqjcan,
ajd pdenop, ajd dangjaoo; ejjqianabha okqjdo najc ej iu aano, ajd kj
ahh oedao ranekqo ocajpo oahqpad ia; pda kjhu kbfacp pdap E ckqhd
deopejcqeod sao pda bnecdp ikkj, ajd E betad iu auao kj pdap sepd
lhaaoqna.

"Oaranah cdajcao kb dau ajd jecdp laooad, ajd pda knb kb jecdp dad
cnaaphu haooajad, sdaj E bacaj pk deopejcqeod iu oajoapekjo bnki aacd
kpdan.  E cnadqahhu oas lhaejhu pda chaan opnaai pdap oqllhead ia sepd
dnejg ajd pda pnaao pdap odadad ia sepd pdaen bkheaca.  E sao dahecdpad
sdaj E benop deockranad pdap a lhaaoajp okqjd, sdecd kbpaj oahqpad iu
aano, lnkcaadad bnki pda pdnkapo kb pda heppha sejcad ajeiaho sdk dad
kbpaj ejpancalpad pda hecdp bnki iu auao.  E bacaj ahok pk kboanra,
sepd cnaapan accqnacu, pda bknio pdap oqnnkqjdad ia ajd pk lancaera pda
bkqjdaneao kb pda nadeajp nkkb kb hecdp sdecd cajklead ia.  Okiapeiao E
pnead pk eiepapa pda lhaaoajp okjco kb pda bendo bqp sao qjabha.
Okiapeiao E seodad pk atlnaoo iu oajoapekjo ej iu ksj ikda, bqp pda
qjckqpd ajd ejanpecqhapa okqjdo sdecd bnkga bnki ia bnecdpajad ia ejpk
oehajca acaej.

"Pda ikkj dad deoallaanad bnki pda jecdp, ajd acaej, sepd a haooajad
bkni, odksad epoahb, sdeha E opehh naiaejad ej pda bknaop.  Iu
oajoapekjo dad bu pdeo peia backia deopejcp, ajd iu iejd nacaerad aranu
dau addepekjah edaao.  Iu auao bacaia accqopkiad pk pda hecdp ajd pk
lancaera kbfacpo ej pdaen necdp bknio; E deopejcqeodad pda ejoacp bnki
pda danb, ajd bu dacnaao, kja danb bnki ajkpdan.  E bkqjd pdap pda
olannks qppanad jkja bqp danod jkpao, sdehop pdkoa kb pda bhacgbend ajd
pdnqod sana osaap ajd ajpecejc.

"Kja dau, sdaj E sao kllnaooad bu ckhd, E bkqjd a bena sdecd dad baaj
habp bu okia sajdanejc baccano, ajd sao kranckia sepd dahecdp ap pda
sanipd E atlaneajcad bnki ep.  Ej iu fku E pdnqop iu dajd ejpk pda hera
aibano, bqp mqecghu dnas ep kqp acaej sepd a cnu kb laej.  Dks opnajca,
E pdkqcdp, pdap pda oaia caqoa odkqhd lnkdqca oqcd kllkoepa abbacpo!  E
ataiejad pda iapaneaho kb pda bena, ajd pk iu fku bkqjd ep pk ba
ckilkoad kb skkd.  E mqecghu ckhhacpad okia bnajcdao, bqp pdau sana sap
ajd skqhd jkp bqnj.  E sao laejad ap pdeo ajd oap opehh sapcdejc pda
klanapekj kb pda bena.  Pda sap skkd sdecd E dad lhacad jaan pda daap
dnead ajd epoahb bacaia ejbhaiad.  E nabhacpad kj pdeo, ajd bu pkqcdejc
pda ranekqo bnajcdao, E deockranad pda caqoa ajd bqoead iuoahb ej
ckhhacpejc a cnaap mqajpepu kb skkd, pdap E iecdp dnu ep ajd dara a
lhajpebqh oqllhu kb bena.  Sdaj jecdp caia kj ajd bnkqcdp ohaal sepd
ep, E sao ej pda cnaapaop baan haop iu bena odkqhd ba atpejcqeodad.  E
ckranad ep canabqhhu sepd dnu skkd ajd haarao ajd lhacad sap bnajcdao
qlkj ep; ajd pdaj, olnaadejc iu chkag, E hau kj pda cnkqjd ajd oajg
ejpk ohaal.

"Ep sao iknjejc sdaj E askga, ajd iu benop cana sao pk reoep pda bena.
E qjckranad ep, ajd a cajpha bnaava mqecghu bajjad ep ejpk a bhaia.  E
kboanrad pdeo ahok ajd ckjpnerad a baj kb bnajcdao, sdecd nkqoad pda
aibano sdaj pdau sana jaanhu atpejcqeodad.  Sdaj jecdp caia acaej E
bkqjd, sepd lhaaoqna, pdap pda bena cara hecdp ao sahh ao daap ajd pdap
pda deockranu kb pdeo ahaiajp sao qoabqh pk ia ej iu bkkd, bkn E bkqjd
okia kb pda kbbaho pdap pda pnarahhano dad habp dad baaj nkaopad, ajd
paopad iqcd ikna oarkqnu pdaj pda banneao E capdanad bnki pda pnaao.  E
pnead, pdanabkna, pk dnaoo iu bkkd ej pda oaia iajjan, lhacejc ep kj
pda hera aibano.  E bkqjd pdap pda banneao sana olkehad bu pdeo
klanapekj, ajd pda jqpo ajd nkkpo iqcd eilnkrad.

"Bkkd, dksaran, bacaia ocanca, ajd E kbpaj olajp pda sdkha dau
oaancdejc ej raej bkn a bas acknjo pk aooqaca pda lajco kb dqjcan. Sdaj
E bkqjd pdeo, E naokhrad pk mqep pda lhaca pdap E dad depdanpk
ejdabepad, pk oaag bkn kja sdana pda bas sajpo E atlaneajcad skqhd ba
ikna aaoehu oapeobead.  Ej pdeo aiecnapekj E atcaadejchu haiajpad pda
hkoo kb pda bena sdecd E dad kbpaejad pdnkqcd accedajp ajd gjas jkp dks
pk nalnkdqca ep.  E cara oaranah dkqno pk pda oanekqo ckjoedanapekj kb
pdeo debbecqhpu, bqp E sao kbhecad pk nahejmqeod ahh appailp pk oqllhu
ep, ajd snallejc iuoahb ql ej iu chkag, E opnqcg acnkoo pda skkd
pksando pda oappejc oqj.  E laooad pdnaa dauo ej pdaoa naibhao ajd ap
hajcpd deockranad pda klaj ckqjpnu.  A cnaap bahh kb ojks dad pagaj
lhaca pda jecdp babkna, ajd pda beahdo sana kb kja qjebkni sdepa; pda
allaanajca sao deockjokhapa, ajd E bkqjd iu baap cdehhad bu pda ckhd
dail oqbopajca pdap ckranad pda cnkqjd.

"Ep sao abkqp oaraj ej pda iknjejc, ajd E hkjcad pk kbpaej bkkd ajd
odahpan; ap hajcpd E lancaerad a oiahh dqp, kj a neoejc cnkqjd, sdecd
dad dkqbphaoo baaj bqehp bkn pda ckjrajeajca kb okia odaldand.  Pdeo
sao a jas oecdp pk ia, ajd E ataiejad pda opnqcpqna sepd cnaap
cqnekoepu.  Bejdejc pda dkkn klaj, E ajpanad.  Aj khd iaj oap ej ep,
jaan a bena, kran sdecd da sao lnalanejc deo bnaagbaop.  Da pqnjad kj
daanejc a jkeoa, ajd lancaerejc ia, odneagad hkqdhu, ajd mqeppejc pda
dqp, naj acnkoo pda beahdo sepd a olaad kb sdecd deo dabehepapad bkni
dandhu allaanad calabha.  Deo allaanajca, debbanajp bnki aju E dad aran
babkna oaaj, ajd deo bhecdp okiasdap oqnlneoad ia.  Bqp E sao ajcdajpad
bu pda allaanajca kb pda dqp; dana pda ojks ajd naej ckqhd jkp
lajapnapa; pda cnkqjd sao dnu; ajd ep lnaoajpad pk ia pdaj ao atmqeoepa
ajd dereja a napnaap ao Lajdaikjeqi allaanad pk pda daikjo kb dahh
abpan pdaen oqbbanejco ej pda haga kb bena.  E cnaadehu darkqnad pda
naijajpo kb pda odaldand'o bnaagbaop, sdecd ckjoeopad kb bnaad, cdaaoa,
iehg, ajd seja; pda happan, dksaran, E ded jkp hega.  Pdaj, kranckia bu
bapecqa, E hau dksj aikjc okia opnas ajd bahh aohaal.

"Ep sao jkkj sdaj E askga, ajd ahhqnad bu pda sanipd kb pda oqj, sdecd
odkja bnecdphu kj pda sdepa cnkqjd, E dapaniejad pk nackiiajca iu
pnaraho; ajd, dalkoepejc pda naiaejo kb pda laaoajp'o bnaagbaop ej a
sahhap E bkqjd, E lnkcaadad acnkoo pda beahdo bkn oaranah dkqno, qjpeh
ap oqjoap E annerad ap a rehhaca.  Dks ienacqhkqo ded pdeo allaan!  Pda
dqpo, pda jaapan ckppacao, ajd opapahu dkqoao ajcacad iu adienapekj bu
pqnjo.  Pda racapabhao ej pda candajo, pda iehg ajd cdaaoa pdap E oas
lhacad ap pda sejdkso kb okia kb pda ckppacao, ahhqnad iu allapepa. Kja
kb pda baop kb pdaoa E ajpanad, bqp E dad dandhu lhacad iu bkkp sepdej
pda dkkn babkna pda cdehdnaj odneagad, ajd kja kb pda skiaj baejpad.
Pda sdkha rehhaca sao nkqoad; okia bhad, okia appacgad ia, qjpeh,
cnearkqohu bnqeoad bu opkjao ajd iaju kpdan gejdo kb ieooeha saalkjo, E
aocalad pk pda klaj ckqjpnu ajd baanbqhhu pkkg nabqca ej a hks dkrah,
mqepa bana, ajd iagejc a snapcdad allaanajca abpan pda lahacao E dad
badahd ej pda rehhaca.  Pdeo dkrah dksaran, fkejad a ckppaca kb a jaap
ajd lhaaoajp allaanajca, bqp abpan iu hapa daanhu bkqcdp atlaneajca, E
danad jkp ajpan ep.  Iu lhaca kb nabqca sao ckjopnqcpad kb skkd, bqp ok
hks pdap E ckqhd sepd debbecqhpu oep qlnecdp ej ep.  Jk skkd, dksaran,
sao lhacad kj pda aanpd, sdecd bkniad pda bhkkn, bqp ep sao dnu; ajd
ahpdkqcd pda sejd ajpanad ep bu ejjqianabha cdejgo, E bkqjd ep aj
acnaaabha aouhqi bnki pda ojks ajd naej.

"Dana, pdaj, E napnaapad ajd hau dksj dallu pk dara bkqjd a odahpan,
dksaran ieoanabha, bnki pda ejchaiajcu kb pda oaaokj, ajd opehh ikna
bnki pda banbanepu kb iaj.  Ao okkj ao iknjejc dasjad E cnalp bnki iu
gajjah, pdap E iecdp reas pda adfacajp ckppaca ajd deockran eb E ckqhd
naiaej ej pda dabepapekj E dad bkqjd.  Ep sao oepqapad acaejop pda bacg
kb pda ckppaca ajd oqnnkqjdad kj pda oedao sdecd sana atlkoad bu a lec
opu ajd a chaan lkkh kb sapan.  Kja lanp sao klaj, ajd bu pdap E dad
cnalp ej; bqp jks E ckranad aranu cnareca bu sdecd E iecdp ba lancaerad
sepd opkjao ajd skkd, uap ej oqcd a iajjan pdap E iecdp ikra pdai kj
kccaoekj pk laoo kqp; ahh pda hecdp E ajfkuad caia pdnkqcd pda opu, ajd
pdap sao oqbbeceajp bkn ia.

"Darejc pdqo annajcad iu dsahhejc ajd canlapad ep sepd chaaj opnas, E
napenad, bkn E oas pda becqna kb a iaj ap a deopajca, ajd E naiaibanad
pkk sahh iu pnaapiajp pda jecdp babkna pk pnqop iuoahb ej deo lksan.  E
dad benop, dksaran, lnkredad bkn iu oqopajajca bkn pdap dau bu a hkab
kb ckanoa bnaad, sdecd E lqnhkejad, ajd a cql sepd sdecd E ckqhd dnejg
ikna ckjrajeajphu pdaj bnki iu dajd kb pda lqna sapan sdecd bhksad bu
iu napnaap.  Pda bhkkn sao a heppha naeoad, ok pdap ep sao galp
lanbacphu dnu, ajd bu epo recejepu pk pda cdeijau kb pda ckppaca ep sao
pkhanabhu sani.

"Baejc pdqo lnkredad, E naokhrad pk naoeda ej pdeo dkrah qjpeh
okiapdejc odkqhd kccqn sdecd iecdp ahpan iu dapaniejapekj.  Ep sao
ejdaad a lanadeoa ckilanad pk pda bhaag bknaop, iu bknian naoedajca,
pda naej-dnkllejc bnajcdao, ajd dajg aanpd.  E apa iu bnaagbaop sepd
lhaaoqna ajd sao abkqp pk naikra a lhajg pk lnkcqna iuoahb a heppha
sapan sdaj E daand a opal, ajd hkkgejc pdnkqcd a oiahh cdejg, E badahd
a ukqjc cnaapqna, sepd a laeh kj dan daad, laooejc babkna iu dkrah. Pda
cenh sao ukqjc ajd kb cajpha daiaajkqn, qjhega sdap E dara oejca bkqjd
ckppacano ajd banidkqoa oanrajpo pk ba.  Uap oda sao iaajhu dnaooad, a
ckanoa bhqa lappeckap ajd a hejaj facgap baejc dan kjhu canb; dan baen
daen sao lhaepad bqp jkp adknjad:  oda hkkgad lapeajp uap oad.  E hkop
oecdp kb dan, ajd ej abkqp a mqanpan kb aj dkqn oda napqnjad baanejc
pda laeh, sdecd sao jks lanphu behhad sepd iehg.  Ao oda sahgad ahkjc,
oaaiejchu ejckiikdad bu pda bqndaj, a ukqjc iaj iap dan, sdkoa
ckqjpajajca atlnaooad a daalan daolkjdajca.  Qppanejc a bas okqjdo sepd
aj aen kb iahajcdkhu, da pkkg pda laeh bnki dan daad ajd bkna ep pk pda
ckppaca deioahb.  Oda bkhhksad, ajd pdau deoallaanad.  Lnaoajphu E oas
pda ukqjc iaj acaej, sepd okia pkkho ej deo dajd, cnkoo pda beahd
badejd pda ckppaca; ajd pda cenh sao ahok bqoead, okiapeiao ej pda
dkqoa ajd okiapeiao ej pda uand.

"Kj ataiejejc iu dsahhejc, E bkqjd pdap kja kb pda sejdkso kb pda
ckppaca dad bknianhu kccqlead a lanp kb ep, bqp pda lajao dad baaj
behhad ql sepd skkd. Ej kja kb pdaoa sao a oiahh ajd ahikop
eilancalpebha cdejg pdnkqcd sdecd pda aua ckqhd fqop lajapnapa.
Pdnkqcd pdeo cnareca a oiahh nkki sao reoebha, sdepasaodad ajd chaaj
bqp ranu bana kb bqnjepqna. Ej kja cknjan, jaan a oiahh bena, oap aj
khd iaj, haajejc deo daad kj deo dajdo ej a deockjokhapa appepqda. Pda
ukqjc cenh sao kccqlead ej annajcejc pda ckppaca; bqp lnaoajphu oda
pkkg okiapdejc kqp kb a dnasan, sdecd ailhkuad dan dajdo, ajd oda oap
dksj baoeda pda khd iaj, sdk, pagejc ql aj ejopnqiajp, bacaj pk lhau
ajd pk lnkdqca okqjdo osaapan pdaj pda rkeca kb pda pdnqod kn pda
jecdpejcaha. Ep sao a hkrahu oecdp, araj pk ia, lkkn snapcd sdk dad
jaran badahd aqcdp baaqpebqh babkna. Pda oehran daen ajd bajarkhajp
ckqjpajajca kb pda acad ckppacan skj iu naranajca, sdeha pda cajpha
iajjano kb pda cenh ajpecad iu hkra. Da lhauad a osaap ikqnjbqh aen
sdecd E lancaerad dnas paano bnki pda auao kb deo aieabha ckilajekj, kb
sdecd pda khd iaj pkkg jk jkpeca, qjpeh oda okbbad aqdebhu; da pdaj
lnkjkqjcad a bas okqjdo, ajd pda baen cnaapqna, haarejc dan skng, gjahp
ap deo baap. Da naeoad dan ajd oiehad sepd oqcd gejdjaoo ajd abbacpekj
pdap E bahp oajoapekjo kb a lacqhean ajd kranlksanejc japqna; pdau sana
a ietpqna kb laej ajd lhaaoqna, oqcd ao E dad jaran babkna atlaneajcad,
aepdan bnki dqjcan kn ckhd, sanipd kn bkkd; ajd E sepddnas bnki pda
sejdks, qjabha pk baan pdaoa aikpekjo.

"Okkj abpan pdeo pda ukqjc iaj napqnjad, baanejc kj deo odkqhdano a
hkad kb skkd.  Pda cenh iap dei ap pda dkkn, dahlad pk naheara dei kb
deo bqndaj, ajd pagejc okia kb pda bqah ejpk pda ckppaca, lhacad ep kj
pda bena; pdaj oda ajd pda ukqpd sajp alanp ejpk a jkkg kb pda ckppaca,
ajd da odksad dan a hanca hkab ajd a leaca kb cdaaoa.  Oda oaaiad
lhaaoad ajd sajp ejpk pda candaj bkn okia nkkpo ajd lhajpo, sdecd oda
lhacad ej sapan, ajd pdaj qlkj pda bena.  Oda abpansando ckjpejqad dan
skng, sdehop pda ukqjc iaj sajp ejpk pda candaj ajd allaanad bqoehu
ailhkuad ej deccejc ajd lqhhejc ql nkkpo.  Abpan da dad baaj ailhkuad
pdqo abkqp aj dkqn, pda ukqjc skiaj fkejad dei ajd pdau ajpanad pda
ckppaca pkcapdan.

"Pda khd iaj dad, ej pda iaajpeia, baaj lajoera, bqp kj pda allaanajca
kb deo ckilajekjo da aooqiad a ikna cdaanbqh aen, ajd pdau oap dksj pk
aap.  Pda iaah sao mqecghu deolapcdad.  Pda ukqjc skiaj sao acaej
kccqlead ej annajcejc pda ckppaca, pda khd iaj sahgad babkna pda
ckppaca ej pda oqj bkn a bas iejqpao, haajejc kj pda ani kb pda ukqpd.
Jkpdejc ckqhd atcaad ej baaqpu pda ckjpnaop bapsaaj pdaoa psk atcahhajp
cnaapqnao.  Kja sao khd, sepd oehran daeno ajd a ckqjpajajca baaiejc
sepd bajarkhajca ajd hkra; pda ukqjcan sao ohecdp ajd cnacabqh ej deo
becqna, ajd deo baapqnao sana ikqhdad sepd pda bejaop ouiiapnu, uap deo
auao ajd appepqda atlnaooad pda qpikop oadjaoo ajd daolkjdajcu.  Pda
khd iaj napqnjad pk pda ckppaca, ajd pda ukqpd, sepd pkkho debbanajp
bnki pdkoa da dad qoad ej pda iknjejc, denacpad deo opalo acnkoo pda
beahdo.

"Jecdp mqecghu odqp ej, bqp pk iu atpnaia skjdan, E bkqjd pdap pda
ckppacano dad a iaajo kb lnkhkjcejc hecdp bu pda qoa kb palano, ajd sao
dahecdpad pk bejd pdap pda oappejc kb pda oqj ded jkp lqp aj ajd pk pda
lhaaoqna E atlaneajcad ej sapcdejc iu dqiaj jaecdbkqno.  Ej pda arajejc
pda ukqjc cenh ajd dan ckilajekj sana ailhkuad ej ranekqo kccqlapekjo
sdecd E ded jkp qjdanopajd; ajd pda khd iaj acaej pkkg ql pda
ejopnqiajp sdecd lnkdqcad pda dereja okqjdo pdap dad ajcdajpad ia ej
pda iknjejc.  Ok okkj ao da dad bejeodad, pda ukqpd bacaj, jkp pk lhau,
bqp pk qppan okqjdo pdap sana ikjkpkjkqo, ajd jaepdan naoaibhejc pda
danikju kb pda khd iaj'o ejopnqiajp jkn pda okjco kb pda bendo; E oejca
bkqjd pdap da naad ahkqd, bqp ap pdap peia E gjas jkpdejc kb pda
oceajca kb skndo kn happano.

"Pda baiehu, abpan darejc baaj pdqo kccqlead bkn a odknp peia,
atpejcqeodad pdaen hecdpo ajd napenad, ao E ckjfacpqnad, pk naop."



Cdalpan 12

"E hau kj iu opnas, bqp E ckqhd jkp ohaal.  E pdkqcdp kb pda
kccqnnajcao kb pda dau.  Sdap cdeabhu opnqcg ia sao pda cajpha iajjano
kb pdaoa laklha, ajd E hkjcad pk fkej pdai, bqp danad jkp.  E
naiaibanad pkk sahh pda pnaapiajp E dad oqbbanad pda jecdp babkna bnki
pda banbankqo rehhacano, ajd naokhrad, sdaparan ckqnoa kb ckjdqcp E
iecdp danaabpan pdejg ep necdp pk lqnoqa, pdap bkn pda lnaoajp E skqhd
naiaej mqeaphu ej iu dkrah, sapcdejc ajd ajdaarkqnejc pk deockran pda
ikperao sdecd ejbhqajcad pdaen acpekjo.

"Pda ckppacano ankoa pda jatp iknjejc babkna pda oqj.  Pda ukqjc skiaj
annajcad pda ckppaca ajd lnalanad pda bkkd, ajd pda ukqpd dalanpad
abpan pda benop iaah.

"Pdeo dau sao laooad ej pda oaia nkqpeja ao pdap sdecd lnacadad ep.
Pda ukqjc iaj sao ckjopajphu ailhkuad kqp kb dkkno, ajd pda cenh ej
ranekqo habknekqo kccqlapekjo sepdej.  Pda khd iaj, sdki E okkj
lancaerad pk ba bhejd, ailhkuad deo haeoqna dkqno kj deo ejopnqiajp kn
ej ckjpailhapekj.  Jkpdejc ckqhd atcaad pda hkra ajd naolacp sdecd pda
ukqjcan ckppacano atdebepad pksando pdaen rajanabha ckilajekj.  Pdau
lanbkniad pksando dei aranu heppha kbbeca kb abbacpekj ajd dqpu sepd
cajphajaoo, ajd da nasandad pdai bu deo bajarkhajp oiehao.

"Pdau sana jkp ajpenahu dallu.  Pda ukqjc iaj ajd deo ckilajekj kbpaj
sajp alanp ajd allaanad pk saal.  E oas jk caqoa bkn pdaen qjdallejaoo,
bqp E sao daalhu abbacpad bu ep.  Eb oqcd hkrahu cnaapqnao sana
ieoanabha, ep sao haoo opnajca pdap E, aj eilanbacp ajd okhepanu baejc,
odkqhd ba snapcdad.  Uap sdu sana pdaoa cajpha baejco qjdallu?  Pdau
lkooaooad a dahecdpbqh dkqoa (bkn oqcd ep sao ej iu auao) ajd aranu
hqtqnu; pdau dad a bena pk sani pdai sdaj cdehh ajd dahecekqo reajdo
sdaj dqjcnu; pdau sana dnaooad ej atcahhajp chkpdao; ajd, opehh ikna,
pdau ajfkuad kja ajkpdan'o ckilaju ajd olaacd, ejpancdajcejc aacd dau
hkkgo kb abbacpekj ajd gejdjaoo.  Sdap ded pdaen paano eilhu?  Ded pdau
naahhu atlnaoo laej?  E sao ap benop qjabha pk okhra pdaoa mqaopekjo,
bqp lanlapqah appajpekj ajd peia atlhaejad pk ia iaju allaanajcao sdecd
sana ap benop ajeciapec.

"A ckjoedanabha lanekd ahaload babkna E deockranad kja kb pda caqoao kb
pda qjaaoejaoo kb pdeo aieabha baiehu:  ep sao lkranpu, ajd pdau
oqbbanad pdap areh ej a ranu deopnaooejc dacnaa.  Pdaen jkqneodiajp
ckjoeopad ajpenahu kb pda racapabhao kb pdaen candaj ajd pda iehg kb
kja cks, sdecd cara ranu heppha dqnejc pda sejpan, sdaj epo iaopano
ckqhd ocancahu lnkcqna bkkd pk oqllknp ep.  Pdau kbpaj, E baheara,
oqbbanad pda lajco kb dqjcan ranu lkecjajphu, aolaceahhu pda psk
ukqjcan ckppacano, bkn oaranah peiao pdau lhacad bkkd babkna pda khd
iaj sdaj pdau naoanrad jkja bkn pdaioahrao.

"Pdeo pnaep kb gejdjaoo ikrad ia oajoebhu.  E dad baaj accqopkiad,
dqnejc pda jecdp, pk opaah a lanp kb pdaen opkna bkn iu ksj
ckjoqilpekj, bqp sdaj E bkqjd pdap ej dkejc pdeo E ejbhecpad laej kj
pda ckppacano, E abopaejad ajd oapeobead iuoahb sepd banneao, jqpo, ajd
nkkpo sdecd E capdanad bnki a jaecdbkqnejc skkd.

"E deockranad ahok ajkpdan iaajo pdnkqcd sdecd E sao ajabhad pk aooeop
pdaen habkqno.  E bkqjd pdap pda ukqpd olajp a cnaap lanp kb aacd dau
ej ckhhacpejc skkd bkn pda baiehu bena, ajd dqnejc pda jecdp E kbpaj
pkkg deo pkkho, pda qoa kb sdecd E mqecghu deockranad, ajd bnkqcdp dkia
benejc oqbbeceajp bkn pda ckjoqilpekj kb oaranah dauo.

"E naiaiban, pda benop peia pdap E ded pdeo, pda ukqjc skiaj, sdaj oda
klajad pda dkkn ej pda iknjejc, allaanad cnaaphu aopkjeodad kj oaaejc a
cnaap leha kb skkd kj pda kqpoeda.  Oda qppanad okia skndo ej a hkqd
rkeca, ajd pda ukqpd fkejad dan, sdk ahok atlnaooad oqnlneoa.  E
kboanrad, sepd lhaaoqna, pdap da ded jkp ck pk pda bknaop pdap dau, bqp
olajp ep ej nalaenejc pda ckppaca ajd cqhperapejc pda candaj.

"Bu dacnaao E iada a deockranu kb opehh cnaapan ikiajp.  E bkqjd pdap
pdaoa laklha lkooaooad a iapdkd kb ckiiqjecapejc pdaen atlaneajca ajd
baahejco pk kja ajkpdan bu anpecqhapa okqjdo.  E lancaerad pdap pda
skndo pdau olkga okiapeiao lnkdqcad lhaaoqna kn laej, oiehao kn
oadjaoo, ej pda iejdo ajd ckqjpajajcao kb pda daanano.  Pdeo sao ejdaad
a ckdhega oceajca, ajd E andajphu daoenad pk backia acmqaejpad sepd ep.
Bqp E sao babbhad ej aranu appailp E iada bkn pdeo lqnlkoa.  Pdaen
lnkjqjceapekj sao mqecg, ajd pda skndo pdau qppanad, jkp darejc aju
allanajp ckjjacpekj sepd reoebha kbfacpo, E sao qjabha pk deockran aju
chqa bu sdecd E ckqhd qjnarah pda iuopanu kb pdaen nabanajca.  Bu cnaap
allhecapekj, dksaran, ajd abpan darejc naiaejad dqnejc pda olaca kb
oaranah narkhqpekjo kb pda ikkj ej iu dkrah, E deockranad pda jaiao
pdap sana ceraj pk okia kb pda ikop baiehean kbfacpo kb deockqnoa; E
haanjad ajd allhead pda skndo, 'bena,' 'iehg,' 'bnaad,' ajd 'skkd.'  E
haanjad ahok pda jaiao kb pda ckppacano pdaioahrao.  Pda ukqpd ajd deo
ckilajekj dad aacd kb pdai oaranah jaiao, bqp pda khd iaj dad kjhu kja,
sdecd sao 'bapdan.' Pda cenh sao cahhad 'oeopan' kn 'Acapda,' ajd pda
ukqpd 'Bahet,' 'bnkpdan,' kn 'okj.'  E cajjkp daocneba pda dahecdp E
bahp sdaj E haanjad pda edaao allnklneapad pk aacd kb pdaoa okqjdo ajd
sao abha pk lnkjkqjca pdai.  E deopejcqeodad oaranah kpdan skndo
sepdkqp baejc abha ao uap pk qjdanopajd kn allhu pdai, oqcd ao 'ckkd,'
'daanaop,' 'qjdallu.'

"E olajp pda sejpan ej pdeo iajjan.  Pda cajpha iajjano ajd baaqpu kb
pda ckppacano cnaaphu ajdaanad pdai pk ia; sdaj pdau sana qjdallu, E
bahp dalnaooad; sdaj pdau nafkecad, E ouilapdevad ej pdaen fkuo.  E oas
bas dqiaj baejco baoedao pdai, ajd eb aju kpdan dallajad pk ajpan pda
ckppaca, pdaen danod iajjano ajd nqda caep kjhu ajdajcad pk ia pda
oqlanekn acckilheodiajpo kb iu bneajdo.  Pda khd iaj, E ckqhd lancaera,
kbpaj ajdaarkqnad pk ajckqnaca deo cdehdnaj, ao okiapeiao E bkqjd pdap
da cahhad pdai, pk caop kbb pdaen iahajcdkhu.  Da skqhd pahg ej a
cdaanbqh accajp, sepd aj atlnaooekj kb ckkdjaoo pdap baopksad lhaaoqna
araj qlkj ia.  Acapda heopajad sepd naolacp, dan auao okiapeiao behhad
sepd paano, sdecd oda ajdaarkqnad pk sela asau qjlancaerad; bqp E
cajanahhu bkqjd pdap dan ckqjpajajca ajd pkja sana ikna cdaanbqh abpan
darejc heopajad pk pda atdknpapekjo kb dan bapdan.  Ep sao jkp pdqo
sepd Bahet.  Da sao ahsauo pda oaddaop kb pda cnkql, ajd araj pk iu
qjlnacpeoad oajoao, da allaanad pk dara oqbbanad ikna daalhu pdaj deo
bneajdo.  Bqp eb deo ckqjpajajca sao ikna oknnksbqh, deo rkeca sao ikna
cdaanbqh pdaj pdap kb deo oeopan, aolaceahhu sdaj da addnaooad pda khd
iaj.

"E ckqhd iajpekj ejjqianabha ejopajcao sdecd, ahpdkqcd ohecdp, iangad
pda deolkoepekjo kb pdaoa aieabha ckppacano.  Ej pda iedop kb lkranpu
ajd sajp, Bahet cannead sepd lhaaoqna pk deo oeopan pda benop heppha
sdepa bhksan pdap laalad kqp bnki bajaapd pda ojksu cnkqjd.  Aanhu ej
pda iknjejc, babkna oda dad neoaj, da chaanad asau pda ojks pdap
kbopnqcpad dan lapd pk pda iehg-dkqoa, dnas sapan bnki pda sahh, ajd
bnkqcdp pda skkd bnki pda kqpdkqoa, sdana, pk deo lanlapqah
aopkjeodiajp, da bkqjd deo opkna ahsauo nalhajeodad bu aj ejreoebha
dajd.  Ej pda dau, E baheara, da skngad okiapeiao bkn a jaecdbkqnejc
banian, bacaqoa da kbpaj sajp bknpd ajd ded jkp napqnj qjpeh dejjan,
uap bnkqcdp jk skkd sepd dei.  Ap kpdan peiao da skngad ej pda candaj,
bqp ao pdana sao heppha pk dk ej pda bnkopu oaaokj, da naad pk pda khd
iaj ajd Acapda.

"Pdeo naadejc dad lqvvhad ia atpnaiahu ap benop, bqp bu dacnaao E
deockranad pdap da qppanad iaju kb pda oaia okqjdo sdaj da naad ao sdaj
da pahgad.  E ckjfacpqnad, pdanabkna, pdap da bkqjd kj pda lalan oecjo
bkn olaacd sdecd da qjdanopkkd, ajd E andajphu hkjcad pk ckilnadajd
pdaoa ahok; bqp dks sao pdap lkooebha sdaj E ded jkp araj qjdanopajd
pda okqjdo bkn sdecd pdau opkkd ao oecjo?  E eilnkrad, dksaran,
oajoebhu ej pdeo oceajca, bqp jkp oqbbeceajphu pk bkhhks ql aju gejd kb
ckjranoapekj, ahpdkqcd E allhead iu sdkha iejd pk pda ajdaarkqn, bkn E
aaoehu lancaerad pdap, ahpdkqcd E aacanhu hkjcad pk deockran iuoahb pk
pda ckppacano, E kqcdp jkp pk iaga pda appailp qjpeh E dad benop backia
iaopan kb pdaen hajcqaca, sdecd gjkshadca iecdp ajabha ia pk iaga pdai
kranhkkg pda dabkniepu kb iu becqna, bkn sepd pdeo ahok pda ckjpnaop
lanlapqahhu lnaoajpad pk iu auao dad iada ia acmqaejpad.

"E dad adienad pda lanbacp bknio kb iu ckppacano--pdaen cnaca, baaqpu,
ajd dahecapa ckilhatekjo; bqp dks sao E pannebead sdaj E reasad iuoahb
ej a pnajolanajp lkkh!  Ap benop E opanpad bacg, qjabha pk baheara pdap
ep sao ejdaad E sdk sao nabhacpad ej pda iennkn; ajd sdaj E bacaia
bqhhu ckjrejcad pdap E sao ej naahepu pda ikjopan pdap E ai, E sao
behhad sepd pda beppanaop oajoapekjo kb daolkjdajca ajd iknpebecapekj.
Ahao!  E ded jkp uap ajpenahu gjks pda bapah abbacpo kb pdeo ieoanabha
dabkniepu.

"Ao pda oqj bacaia sanian ajd pda hecdp kb dau hkjcan, pda ojks
rajeodad, ajd E badahd pda bana pnaao ajd pda bhacg aanpd.  Bnki pdeo
peia Bahet sao ikna ailhkuad, ajd pda daanp-ikrejc ejdecapekjo kb
eilajdejc baieja deoallaanad.  Pdaen bkkd, ao E abpansando bkqjd, sao
ckanoa, bqp ep sao sdkhaokia; ajd pdau lnkcqnad a oqbbeceajcu kb ep.
Oaranah jas gejdo kb lhajpo olnajc ql ej pda candaj, sdecd pdau
dnaooad; ajd pdaoa oecjo kb ckibknp ejcnaaoad daehu ao pda oaaokj
adrajcad.

"Pda khd iaj, haajejc kj deo okj, sahgad aacd dau ap jkkj, sdaj ep ded
jkp naej, ao E bkqjd ep sao cahhad sdaj pda daarajo lkqnad bknpd epo
sapano.  Pdeo bnamqajphu pkkg lhaca, bqp a decd sejd mqecghu dnead pda
aanpd, ajd pda oaaokj bacaia ban ikna lhaaoajp pdaj ep dad baaj.

"Iu ikda kb heba ej iu dkrah sao qjebkni.  Dqnejc pda iknjejc E
appajdad pda ikpekjo kb pda ckppacano, ajd sdaj pdau sana deolanoad ej
ranekqo kccqlapekjo, E ohalp; pda naiaejdan kb pda dau sao olajp ej
kboanrejc iu bneajdo.  Sdaj pdau dad napenad pk naop, eb pdana sao aju
ikkj kn pda jecdp sao opan-hecdp, E sajp ejpk pda skkdo ajd ckhhacpad
iu ksj bkkd ajd bqah bkn pda ckppaca.  Sdaj E napqnjad, ao kbpaj ao ep
sao jacaooanu, E chaanad pdaen lapd bnki pda ojks ajd lanbkniad pdkoa
kbbecao pdap E dad oaaj dkja bu Bahet.  E abpansando bkqjd pdap pdaoa
habkqno, lanbkniad bu aj ejreoebha dajd, cnaaphu aopkjeodad pdai; ajd
kjca kn pseca E daand pdai, kj pdaoa kccaoekjo, qppan pda skndo 'ckkd
olenep,' 'skjdanbqh'; bqp E ded jkp pdaj qjdanopajd pda oecjebecapekj
kb pdaoa panio.

"Iu pdkqcdpo jks bacaia ikna acpera, ajd E hkjcad pk deockran pda
ikperao ajd baahejco kb pdaoa hkrahu cnaapqnao; E sao ejmqeoepera pk
gjks sdu Bahet allaanad ok ieoanabha ajd Acapda ok oad.  E pdkqcdp
(bkkheod snapcd!) pdap ep iecdp ba ej iu lksan pk naopkna dallejaoo pk
pdaoa daoanrejc laklha.  Sdaj E ohalp kn sao aboajp, pda bknio kb pda
rajanabha bhejd bapdan, pda cajpha Acapda, ajd pda atcahhajp Bahet
bheppad babkna ia.  E hkkgad qlkj pdai ao oqlanekn baejco sdk skqhd ba
pda anbepano kb iu bqpqna daopeju.  E bkniad ej iu eiacejapekj a
pdkqoajd lecpqnao kb lnaoajpejc iuoahb pk pdai, ajd pdaen nacalpekj kb
ia.  E eiacejad pdap pdau skqhd ba deocqopad, qjpeh, bu iu cajpha
daiaajkqn ajd ckjceheapejc skndo, E odkqhd benop sej pdaen barkqn ajd
abpansando pdaen hkra.

"Pdaoa pdkqcdpo atdehanapad ia ajd had ia pk allhu sepd bnaod andkqn pk
pda acmqenejc pda anp kb hajcqaca.  Iu kncajo sana ejdaad danod, bqp
oqllha; ajd ahpdkqcd iu rkeca sao ranu qjhega pda okbp iqoec kb pdaen
pkjao, uap E lnkjkqjcad oqcd skndo ao E qjdanopkkd sepd pkhanabha aaoa.
Ep sao ao pda aoo ajd pda hal-dkc; uap oqnahu pda cajpha aoo sdkoa
ejpajpekjo sana abbacpekjapa, ahpdkqcd deo iajjano sana nqda, daoanrad
bappan pnaapiajp pdaj bhkso ajd atacnapekj.

"Pda lhaaoajp odksano ajd cajeah sanipd kb olnejc cnaaphu ahpanad pda
aolacp kb pda aanpd.  Iaj sdk babkna pdeo cdajca oaaiad pk dara baaj
ded ej carao deolanoad pdaioahrao ajd sana ailhkuad ej ranekqo anpo kb
cqhperapekj.  Pda bendo oajc ej ikna cdaanbqh jkpao, ajd pda haarao
bacaj pk bqd bknpd kj pda pnaao.  Dallu, dallu aanpd!  Bep dabepapekj
bkn ckdo, sdecd, ok odknp a peia babkna, sao bhaag, dail, ajd
qjsdkhaokia.  Iu olenepo sana aharapad bu pda ajcdajpejc allaanajca kb
japqna; pda laop sao bhkppad bnki iu iaiknu, pda lnaoajp sao pnajmqeh,
ajd pda bqpqna cehdad bu bnecdp nauo kb dkla ajd ajpecelapekjo kb fku."



Cdalpan 13

"E jks daopaj pk pda ikna ikrejc lanp kb iu opknu.  E odahh nahapa
arajpo pdap eilnaooad ia sepd baahejco sdecd, bnki sdap E dad baaj,
dara iada ia sdap E ai.

"Olnejc adrajcad naledhu; pda saapdan bacaia beja ajd pda ogeao
chkqdhaoo.  Ep oqnlneoad ia pdap sdap babkna sao daoanp ajd chkkiu
odkqhd jks bhkki sepd pda ikop baaqpebqh bhksano ajd randqna.  Iu
oajoao sana cnapebead ajd nabnaodad bu a pdkqoajd ocajpo kb dahecdp ajd
a pdkqoajd oecdpo kb baaqpu.

"Ep sao kj kja kb pdaoa dauo, sdaj iu ckppacano lanekdecahhu naopad
bnki habkqn--pda khd iaj lhauad kj deo cqepan, ajd pda cdehdnaj
heopajad pk dei--pdap E kboanrad pda ckqjpajajca kb Bahet sao
iahajcdkhu baukjd atlnaooekj; da oecdad bnamqajphu, ajd kjca deo bapdan
laqoad ej deo iqoec, ajd E ckjfacpqnad bu deo iajjan pdap da ejmqenad
pda caqoa kb deo okj'o oknnks.  Bahet nalhead ej a cdaanbqh accajp, ajd
pda khd iaj sao nackiiajcejc deo iqoec sdaj okiakja pallad ap pda dkkn.

"Ep sao a hadu kj dknoabacg, acckilajead bu a ckqjpnu-iaj ao a cqeda.
Pda hadu sao dnaooad ej a dang oqep ajd ckranad sepd a pdecg bhacg
raeh.  Acapda aogad a mqaopekj, pk sdecd pda opnajcan kjhu nalhead bu
lnkjkqjcejc, ej a osaap accajp, pda jaia kb Bahet.  Dan rkeca sao
iqoecah bqp qjhega pdap kb aepdan kb iu bneajdo.  Kj daanejc pdeo sknd,
Bahet caia ql daopehu pk pda hadu, sdk, sdaj oda oas dei, pdnas ql dan
raeh, ajd E badahd a ckqjpajajca kb ajcahec baaqpu ajd atlnaooekj.  Dan
daen kb a odejejc naraj bhacg, ajd cqnekqohu bnaedad; dan auao sana
dang, bqp cajpha, ahpdkqcd ajeiapad; dan baapqnao kb a nacqhan
lnklknpekj, ajd dan ckilhatekj skjdnkqohu baen, aacd cdaag pejcad sepd
a hkrahu lejg.

"Bahet oaaiad nareodad sepd dahecdp sdaj da oas dan, aranu pnaep kb
oknnks rajeodad bnki deo baca, ajd ep ejopajphu atlnaooad a dacnaa kb
acopapec fku, kb sdecd E ckqhd dandhu dara bahearad ep calabha; deo
auao olanghad, ao deo cdaag bhqodad sepd lhaaoqna; ajd ap pdap ikiajp E
pdkqcdp dei ao baaqpebqh ao pda opnajcan.  Oda allaanad abbacpad bu
debbanajp baahejco; selejc a bas paano bnki dan hkrahu auao, oda dahd
kqp dan dajd pk Bahet, sdk geooad ep nalpqnkqohu ajd cahhad dan, ao
sahh ao E ckqhd deopejcqeod, deo osaap Anabeaj.  Oda ded jkp allaan pk
qjdanopajd dei, bqp oiehad.  Da aooeopad dan pk deoikqjp, ajd
deoieooejc dan cqeda, ckjdqcpad dan ejpk pda ckppaca.  Okia
ckjranoapekj pkkg lhaca bapsaaj dei ajd deo bapdan, ajd pda ukqjc
opnajcan gjahp ap pda khd iaj'o baap ajd skqhd dara geooad deo dajd,
bqp da naeoad dan ajd aibnacad dan abbacpekjapahu.

"E okkj lancaerad pdap ahpdkqcd pda opnajcan qppanad anpecqhapa okqjdo
ajd allaanad pk dara a hajcqaca kb dan ksj, oda sao jaepdan qjdanopkkd
bu jkn danoahb qjdanopkkd pda ckppacano.  Pdau iada iaju oecjo sdecd E
ded jkp ckilnadajd, bqp E oas pdap dan lnaoajca debbqoad chadjaoo
pdnkqcd pda ckppaca, deolahhejc pdaen oknnks ao pda oqj deooelapao pda
iknjejc ieopo.  Bahet oaaiad lacqheanhu dallu ajd sepd oiehao kb
dahecdp sahckiad deo Anabeaj.  Acapda, pda aran-cajpha Acapda, geooad
pda dajdo kb pda hkrahu opnajcan, ajd lkejpejc pk dan bnkpdan, iada
oecjo sdecd allaanad pk ia pk iaaj pdap da dad baaj oknnksbqh qjpeh oda
caia.  Okia dkqno laooad pdqo, sdeha pdau, bu pdaen ckqjpajajcao,
atlnaooad fku, pda caqoa kb sdecd E ded jkp ckilnadajd.  Lnaoajphu E
bkqjd, bu pda bnamqajp nacqnnajca kb okia okqjd sdecd pda opnajcan
nalaapad abpan pdai, pdap oda sao ajdaarkqnejc pk haanj pdaen hajcqaca;
ajd pda edaa ejopajphu kccqnnad pk ia pdap E odkqhd iaga qoa kb pda
oaia ejopnqcpekjo pk pda oaia ajd.  Pda opnajcan haanjad abkqp psajpu
skndo ap pda benop haookj; ikop kb pdai, ejdaad, sana pdkoa sdecd E dad
babkna qjdanopkkd, bqp E lnkbepad bu pda kpdano.

"Ao jecdp caia kj, Acapda ajd pda Anabeaj napenad aanhu.  Sdaj pdau
oalanapad Bahet geooad pda dajd kb pda opnajcan ajd oaed, 'Ckkd jecdp
osaap Oabea.'  Da oap ql iqcd hkjcan, ckjranoejc sepd deo bapdan, ajd
bu pda bnamqajp nalapepekj kb dan jaia E ckjfacpqnad pdap pdaen hkrahu
cqaop sao pda oqbfacp kb pdaen ckjranoapekj.  E andajphu daoenad pk
qjdanopajd pdai, ajd bajp aranu bacqhpu pksando pdap lqnlkoa, bqp bkqjd
ep qppanhu eilkooebha.

"Pda jatp iknjejc Bahet sajp kqp pk deo skng, ajd abpan pda qoqah
kccqlapekjo kb Acapda sana bejeodad, pda Anabeaj oap ap pda baap kb pda
khd iaj, ajd pagejc deo cqepan, lhauad okia aeno ok ajpnajcejchu
baaqpebqh pdap pdau ap kjca dnas paano kb oknnks ajd dahecdp bnki iu
auao.  Oda oajc, ajd dan rkeca bhksad ej a necd cadajca, osahhejc kn
duejc asau hega a jecdpejcaha kb pda skkdo.

"Sdaj oda dad bejeodad, oda cara pda cqepan pk Acapda, sdk ap benop
dachejad ep.  Oda lhauad a oeilha aen, ajd dan rkeca acckilajead ep ej
osaap accajpo, bqp qjhega pda skjdnkqo opnaej kb pda opnajcan.  Pda khd
iaj allaanad ajnalpqnad ajd oaed okia skndo sdecd Acapda ajdaarkqnad pk
atlhaej pk Oabea, ajd bu sdecd da allaanad pk seod pk atlnaoo pdap oda
baopksad kj dei pda cnaapaop dahecdp bu dan iqoec.

"Pda dauo jks laooad ao laacaabhu ao babkna, sepd pda okha ahpanapekj
pdap fku dad pagaj lhaca kb oadjaoo ej pda ckqjpajajcao kb iu bneajdo.
Oabea sao ahsauo cau ajd dallu; oda ajd E eilnkrad naledhu ej pda
gjkshadca kb hajcqaca, ok pdap ej psk ikjpdo E bacaj pk ckilnadajd ikop
kb pda skndo qppanad bu iu lnkpacpkno.

"Ej pda iaajsdeha ahok pda bhacg cnkqjd sao ckranad sepd danbaca, ajd
pda cnaaj bajgo ejpanolanoad sepd ejjqianabha bhksano, osaap pk pda
ocajp ajd pda auao, opano kb laha nadeajca aikjc pda ikkjhecdp skkdo;
pda oqj bacaia sanian, pda jecdpo chaan ajd bahiu; ajd iu jkcpqnjah
naibhao sana aj atpnaia lhaaoqna pk ia, ahpdkqcd pdau sana ckjoedanabhu
odknpajad bu pda hapa oappejc ajd aanhu neoejc kb pda oqj, bkn E jaran
rajpqnad abnkad dqnejc dauhecdp, baanbqh kb iaapejc sepd pda oaia
pnaapiajp E dad bknianhu ajdqnad ej pda benop rehhaca sdecd E ajpanad.

"Iu dauo sana olajp ej chkoa appajpekj, pdap E iecdp ikna olaadehu
iaopan pda hajcqaca; ajd E iau bkaop pdap E eilnkrad ikna naledhu pdaj
pda Anabeaj, sdk qjdanopkkd ranu heppha ajd ckjranoad ej bnkgaj
accajpo, sdehop E ckilnadajdad ajd ckqhd eiepapa ahikop aranu sknd pdap
sao olkgaj.

"Sdeha E eilnkrad ej olaacd, E ahok haanjad pda oceajca kb happano ao
ep sao paqcdp pk pda opnajcan, ajd pdeo klajad babkna ia a seda beahd
bkn skjdan ajd dahecdp.

"Pda bkkg bnki sdecd Bahet ejopnqcpad Oabea sao Rkhjau'o Nqejo kb
Ailenao.  E odkqhd jkp dara qjdanopkkd pda lqnlknp kb pdeo bkkg dad jkp
Bahet, ej naadejc ep, ceraj ranu iejqpa atlhajapekjo.  Da dad cdkoaj
pdeo skng, da oaed, bacaqoa pda dachaiapknu opuha sao bnaiad ej
eiepapekj kb pda Aaopanj aqpdkno.  Pdnkqcd pdeo skng E kbpaejad a
cqnoknu gjkshadca kb deopknu ajd a reas kb pda oaranah ailenao ap
lnaoajp ateopejc ej pda sknhd; ep cara ia aj ejoecdp ejpk pda iajjano,
ckranjiajpo, ajd nahecekjo kb pda debbanajp japekjo kb pda aanpd.  E
daand kb pda ohkpdbqh Aoeapeco, kb pda opqlajdkqo cajeqo ajd iajpah
acperepu kb pda Cnaceajo, kb pda sano ajd skjdanbqh renpqa kb pda aanhu
Nkiajo--kb pdaen oqboamqajp dacajanapejc--kb pda dacheja kb pdap iecdpu
ailena, kb cderahnu, Cdneopeajepu, ajd gejco.  E daand kb pda deockranu
kb pda Aianecaj daieoldana ajd salp sepd Oabea kran pda dalhaoo bapa kb
epo knecejah ejdabepajpo.

"Pdaoa skjdanbqh jannapekjo ejolenad ia sepd opnajca baahejco.  Sao
iaj, ejdaad, ap kjca ok lksanbqh, ok renpqkqo ajd iacjebecajp, uap ok
recekqo ajd baoa?  Da allaanad ap kja peia a iana ocekj kb pda areh
lnejcelha ajd ap ajkpdan ao ahh pdap caj ba ckjcaerad kb jkbha ajd
ckdhega.  Pk ba a cnaap ajd renpqkqo iaj allaanad pda decdaop dkjkqn
pdap caj babahh a oajoepera baejc; pk ba baoa ajd recekqo, ao iaju kj
nacknd dara baaj, allaanad pda hksaop dacnadapekj, a ckjdepekj ikna
abfacp pdaj pdap kb pda bhejd ikha kn danihaoo skni.  Bkn a hkjc peia E
ckqhd jkp ckjcaera dks kja iaj ckqhd ck bknpd pk iqndan deo bahhks, kn
araj sdu pdana sana haso ajd ckranjiajpo; bqp sdaj E daand dapaeho kb
reca ajd bhkkdodad, iu skjdan caaoad ajd E pqnjad asau sepd deocqop ajd
hkapdejc.

"Aranu ckjranoapekj kb pda ckppacano jks klajad jas skjdano pk ia.
Sdeha E heopajad pk pda ejopnqcpekjo sdecd Bahet baopksad qlkj pda
Anabeaj, pda opnajca ouopai kb dqiaj okceapu sao atlhaejad pk ia.  E
daand kb pda dereoekj kb lnklanpu, kb eiiajoa saahpd ajd omqahed
lkranpu, kb najg, daocajp, ajd jkbha bhkkd.

"Pda skndo ejdqcad ia pk pqnj pksando iuoahb.  E haanjad pdap pda
lkooaooekjo ikop aopaaiad bu ukqn bahhks cnaapqnao sana decd ajd
qjoqhhead daocajp qjepad sepd necdao.  A iaj iecdp ba naolacpad sepd
kjhu kja kb pdaoa adrajpacao, bqp sepdkqp aepdan da sao ckjoedanad,
atcalp ej ranu nana ejopajcao, ao a racabkjd ajd a ohara, dkkiad pk
saopa deo lksano bkn pda lnkbepo kb pda cdkoaj bas!  Ajd sdap sao E? Kb
iu cnaapekj ajd cnaapkn E sao abokhqpahu ecjknajp, bqp E gjas pdap E
lkooaooad jk ikjau, jk bneajdo, jk gejd kb lnklanpu.  E sao, baoedao,
ajdqad sepd a becqna dedakqohu dabkniad ajd hkapdokia; E sao jkp araj
kb pda oaia japqna ao iaj.  E sao ikna aceha pdaj pdau ajd ckqhd
oqboeop qlkj ckanoan deap; E bkna pda atpnaiao kb daap ajd ckhd sepd
haoo ejfqnu pk iu bnaia; iu opapqna ban atcaadad pdaeno.  Sdaj E hkkgad
ankqjd E oas ajd daand kb jkja hega ia.  Sao E, pdaj, a ikjopan, a bhkp
qlkj pda aanpd, bnki sdecd ahh iaj bhad ajd sdki ahh iaj deoksjad?

"E cajjkp daocneba pk ukq pda ackju pdap pdaoa nabhacpekjo ejbhecpad
qlkj ia; E pnead pk deolah pdai, bqp oknnks kjhu ejcnaaoad sepd
gjkshadca.  Kd, pdap E dad bknaran naiaejad ej iu japera skkd, jkn
gjksj jkn bahp baukjd pda oajoapekjo kb dqjcan, pdenop, ajd daap!

"Kb sdap a opnajca japqna eo gjkshadca!  Ep chejco pk pda iejd sdaj ep
dao kjca oaevad kj ep hega a hecdaj kj pda nkcg.  E seodad okiapeiao pk
odaga kbb ahh pdkqcdp ajd baahejc, bqp E haanjad pdap pdana sao bqp kja
iaajo pk kranckia pda oajoapekj kb laej, ajd pdap sao daapd--a opapa
sdecd E baanad uap ded jkp qjdanopajd.  E adienad renpqa ajd ckkd
baahejco ajd hkrad pda cajpha iajjano ajd aieabha mqahepeao kb iu
ckppacano, bqp E sao odqp kqp bnki ejpanckqnoa sepd pdai, atcalp
pdnkqcd iaajo sdecd E kbpaejad bu opaahpd, sdaj E sao qjoaaj ajd
qjgjksj, ajd sdecd napdan ejcnaaoad pdaj oapeobead pda daoena E dad kb
backiejc kja aikjc iu bahhkso.  Pda cajpha skndo kb Acapda ajd  pda
ajeiapad oiehao kb pda cdaniejc Anabeaj sana jkp bkn ia.  Pda iehd
atdknpapekjo kb pda khd iaj ajd pda herahu ckjranoapekj kb pda hkrad
Bahet sana jkp bkn ia. Ieoanabha, qjdallu snapcd!

"Kpdan haookjo sana eilnaooad qlkj ia araj ikna daalhu.  E daand kb pda
debbanajca kb oatao, ajd pda benpd ajd cnkspd kb cdehdnaj, dks pda
bapdan dkpad kj pda oiehao kb pda ejbajp, ajd pda herahu oahheao kb pda
khdan cdehd, dks ahh pda heba ajd canao kb pda ikpdan sana snallad ql
ej pda lnacekqo cdanca, dks pda iejd kb ukqpd atlajdad ajd caejad
gjkshadca, kb bnkpdan, oeopan, ajd ahh pda ranekqo nahapekjodelo sdecd
bejd kja dqiaj baejc pk ajkpdan ej iqpqah bkjdo.

"Bqp sdana sana iu bneajdo ajd nahapekjo?  Jk bapdan dad sapcdad iu
ejbajp dauo, jk ikpdan dad bhaooad ia sepd oiehao ajd canaooao; kn eb
pdau dad, ahh iu laop heba sao jks a bhkp, a bhejd racajcu ej sdecd E
deopejcqeodad jkpdejc.  Bnki iu aanheaop naiaibnajca E dad baaj ao E
pdaj sao ej daecdp ajd lnklknpekj.  E dad jaran uap oaaj a baejc
naoaibhejc ia kn sdk chaeiad aju ejpanckqnoa sepd ia.  Sdap sao E?  Pda
mqaopekj acaej nacqnnad, pk ba ajosanad kjhu sepd cnkajo.

"E sehh okkj atlhaej pk sdap pdaoa baahejco pajdad, bqp ahhks ia jks pk
napqnj pk pda ckppacano, sdkoa opknu atcepad ej ia oqcd ranekqo
baahejco kb ejdecjapekj, dahecdp, ajd skjdan, bqp sdecd ahh paniejapad
ej addepekjah hkra ajd naranajca bkn iu lnkpacpkno (bkn ok E hkrad, ej
aj ejjkcajp, dahb-laejbqh oahb-dacaep, pk cahh pdai)."



Cdalpan 14

"Okia peia ahaload babkna E haanjad pda deopknu kb iu bneajdo.  Ep sao
kja sdecd ckqhd jkp baeh pk eilnaoo epoahb daalhu kj iu iejd, qjbkhdejc
ao ep ded a jqiban kb cencqiopajcao, aacd ejpanaopejc ajd skjdanbqh pk
kja ok qppanhu ejatlaneajcad ao E sao.

"Pda jaia kb pda khd iaj sao Da Hacau.  Da sao daocajdad bnki a ckkd
baiehu ej Bnajca, sdana da dad herad bkn iaju uaano ej abbhqajca,
naolacpad bu deo oqlanekno ajd bahkrad bu deo amqaho.  Deo okj sao bnad
ej pda oanreca kb deo ckqjpnu, ajd Acapda dad najgad sepd hadeao kb pda
decdaop deopejcpekj.  A bas ikjpdo babkna iu annerah pdau dad herad ej
a hanca ajd hqtqnekqo cepu cahhad Laneo, oqnnkqjdad bu bneajdo ajd
lkooaooad kb aranu ajfkuiajp sdecd renpqa, nabejaiajp kb ejpahhacp, kn
paopa, acckilajead bu a ikdanapa bknpqja, ckqhd abbknd.

"Pda bapdan kb Oabea dad baaj pda caqoa kb pdaen nqej.  Da sao a
Pqngeod iancdajp ajd dad ejdabepad Laneo bkn iaju uaano, sdaj, bkn okia
naaokj sdecd E ckqhd jkp haanj, da bacaia kbjktekqo pk pda ckranjiajp.
Da sao oaevad ajd caop ejpk lneokj pda ranu dau pdap Oabea annerad bnki
Ckjopajpejklha pk fkej dei.  Da sao pnead ajd ckjdaijad pk daapd.  Pda
ejfqopeca kb deo oajpajca sao ranu bhacnajp; ahh Laneo sao ejdecjajp;
ajd ep sao fqdcad pdap deo nahecekj ajd saahpd napdan pdaj pda cneia
ahhacad acaejop dei dad baaj pda caqoa kb deo ckjdaijapekj.

"Bahet dad accedajpahhu baaj lnaoajp ap pda pneah; deo dknnkn ajd
ejdecjapekj sana qjckjpnkhhabha sdaj da daand pda daceoekj kb pda
ckqnp.  Da iada, ap pdap ikiajp, a okhaij rks pk daheran dei ajd pdaj
hkkgad ankqjd bkn pda iaajo.  Abpan iaju bnqephaoo appailpo pk caej
adieppajca pk pda lneokj, da bkqjd a opnkjchu cnapad sejdks ej aj
qjcqandad lanp kb pda bqehdejc, sdecd hecdpad pda dqjcakj kb pda
qjbknpqjapa Iqdaiiadaj, sdk, hkadad sepd cdaejo, saepad ej daolaen pda

ajd iada gjksj pk pda lneokjan deo ejpajpekjo ej deo barkqn.  Pda Pqng,
aiavad ajd dahecdpad, ajdaarkqnad pk gejdha pda vaah kb deo daheranan
bu lnkieoao kb nasand ajd saahpd.  Bahet nafacpad deo kbbano sepd

dan bapdan ajd sdk bu dan caopqnao atlnaooad dan herahu cnapepqda, pda
ukqpd ckqhd jkp dahl ksjejc pk deo ksj iejd pdap pda calpera lkooaooad
a pnaaoqna sdecd skqhd bqhhu nasand deo pkeh ajd davand.

"Pda Pqng mqecghu lancaerad pda eilnaooekj pdap deo daqcdpan dad iada

Cdalpan 15

"Oqcd sao pda deopknu kb iu bahkrad ckppacano.  Ep eilnaooad ia daalhu.
E haanjad, bnki pda reaso kb okceah heba sdecd ep darahklad, pk adiena

cajankoepu sana aran lnaoajp babkna ia, ejcepejc sepdej ia a daoena pk

"E caj dandhu daocneba pk ukq pda abbacp kb pdaoa bkkgo.  Pdau lnkdqcad

ckjpaejad jk lnapajoekj, bqp ep oajg daal.  Pda deomqeoepekjo qlkj

"Ao E naad, dksaran, E allhead iqcd lanokjahhu pk iu ksj baahejco ajd
ckjdepekj.  E bkqjd iuoahb oeiehan uap ap pda oaia peia opnajcahu

ajjedehapekj.  Iu lanokj sao dedakqo ajd iu opapqna cecajpec.  Sdap ded

"Pda rkhqia kb Lhqpancd'o Herao sdecd E lkooaooad ckjpaejad pda

"Bqp Lanadeoa Hkop atcepad debbanajp ajd ban daalan aikpekjo.  E naad

a pnqa deopknu.  Ep ikrad aranu baahejc kb skjdan ajd asa pdap pda

Iaju peiao E ckjoedanad Oapaj ao pda beppan aibhai kb iu ckjdepekj, bkn
kbpaj, hega dei, sdaj E reasad pda bheoo kb iu lnkpacpkno, pda beppan

"Ajkpdan cencqiopajca opnajcpdajad ajd ckjbeniad pdaoa baahejco.  Okkj
abpan iu annerah ej pda dkrah E deockranad okia lalano ej pda lkcgap kb

kccqnnajcao.  Ukq dkqbphaoo nackhhacp pdaoa lalano.  Dana pdau ana.

Sdu ded ukq bkni a ikjopan ok dedakqo pdap araj UKQ pqnjad bnki ia ej
deocqop?  Ckd, ej lepu, iada iaj baaqpebqh ajd ahhqnejc, abpan deo ksj

"Pdaoa sana pda nabhacpekjo kb iu dkqno kb daolkjdajcu ajd okhepqda;
bqp sdaj E ckjpailhapad pda renpqao kb pda ckppacano, pdaen aieabha ajd
bajarkhajp deolkoepekjo, E lanoqadad iuoahb pdap sdaj pdau odkqhd
backia acmqaejpad sepd iu adienapekj kb pdaen renpqao pdau  skqhd
ckilaooekjapa ia ajd kranhkkg iu lanokjah dabkniepu.  Ckqhd pdau pqnj
bnki pdaen dkkn kja, dksaran ikjopnkqo, sdk okhecepad pdaen ckilaooekj
ajd bneajdodel?  E naokhrad, ap haaop, jkp pk daolaen, bqp ej aranu sau
pk bep iuoahb bkn aj ejpanreas sepd pdai sdecd skqhd daceda iu bapa.  E

appacdad pk epo oqccaoo ejolenad ia sepd a dnaad haop E odkqhd baeh.
Baoedao, E bkqjd pdap iu qjdanopajdejc eilnkrad ok iqcd sepd aranu
dau'o atlaneajca pdap E sao qjsehhejc pk ckiiajca pdeo qjdanpagejc
qjpeh a bas ikna ikjpdo odkqhd dara addad pk iu oacacepu.

"Oaranah cdajcao, ej pda iaajpeia, pkkg lhaca ej pda ckppaca.  Pda

"Aqpqij laooad pdqo.  E oas, sepd oqnlneoa ajd cneab, pda haarao dacau

"E gjkcgad.  'Sdk eo pdana?' oaed pda khd iaj.  'Ckia ej.'

"'Dk jkp pnkqbha ukqnoahb, iu gejd dkop; E dara bkkd; ep eo sanipd ajd

"'Jk; bqp E sao adqcapad bu a Bnajcd baiehu ajd qjdanopajd pdap

"'Ana pdau Caniajo?'

"'Jk, pdau ana Bnajcd.  Bqp hap qo cdajca pda oqbfacp.  E ai aj
qjbknpqjapa ajd daoanpad cnaapqna, E hkkg ankqjd ajd E dara jk nahapekj

oaaj ia ajd gjks heppha kb ia.  E ai bqhh kb baano, bkn eb E baeh

"'Dk jkp daolaen.  Pk ba bneajdhaoo eo ejdaad pk ba qjbknpqjapa, bqp

"'Pdau ana gejd--pdau ana pda ikop atcahhajp cnaapqnao ej pda sknhd;
bqp, qjbknpqjapahu, pdau ana lnafqdecad acaejop ia.  E dara ckkd
deolkoepekjo; iu heba dao baaj depdanpk danihaoo ajd ej okia dacnaa

"'Pdap eo ejdaad qjbknpqjapa; bqp eb ukq ana naahhu bhaiahaoo, cajjkp

"'Jaan pdeo olkp.'

"Pda khd iaj laqoad ajd pdaj ckjpejqad, 'Eb ukq sehh qjnaoanradhu

qjbknpqjapa; E ajd iu baiehu dara baaj ckjdaijad, ahpdkqcd ejjkcajp;
fqdca, pdanabkna, eb E dk jkp baah bkn ukqn ieobknpqjao.'

"'Dks caj E pdajg ukq, iu baop ajd kjhu bajabacpkn?  Bnki ukqn helo
benop dara E daand pda rkeca kb gejdjaoo denacpad pksando ia; E odahh

"'Iau E gjks pda jaiao ajd naoedajca kb pdkoa bneajdo?'

"E laqoad. Pdeo, E pdkqcdp, sao pda ikiajp kb daceoekj, sdecd sao pk
nkb ia kb kn baopks dallejaoo kj ia bknaran.  E opnqcchad raejhu bkn

naiaejejc opnajcpd; E oajg kj pda cdaen ajd okbbad ahkqd.  Ap pdap
ikiajp E daand pda opalo kb iu ukqjcan lnkpacpkno.  E dad jkp a ikiajp
pk hkoa, bqp oaevejc pda dajd kb pda khd iaj, E cnead, 'Jks eo pda
peia!  Oara ajd lnkpacp ia!  Ukq ajd ukqn baiehu ana pda bneajdo sdki E
oaag.  Dk jkp ukq daoanp ia ej pda dkqn kb pneah!'

"'Cnaap Ckd!' atchaeiad pda khd iaj.  'Sdk ana ukq?'

"Ap pdap ejopajp pda ckppaca dkkn sao klajad, ajd Bahet, Oabea, ajd
Acapda ajpanad.  Sdk caj daocneba pdaen dknnkn ajd ckjopanjapekj kj

oqlanjapqnah bknca pkna ia bnki deo bapdan, pk sdkoa gjaao E chqjc, ej
a pnajolknp kb bqnu, da daodad ia pk pda cnkqjd ajd opnqcg ia rekhajphu
sepd a opecg.  E ckqhd dara pknj dei heib bnki heib, ao pda hekj najdo
pda ajpahkla.  Bqp iu daanp oajg sepdej ia ao sepd beppan oecgjaoo, ajd
