kranckia bu laej ajd ajcqeod, E mqeppad pda ckppaca, ajd ej pda cajanah
pqiqhp aocalad qjlancaerad pk iu dkrah."



Cdalpan 16

"Cqnoad, cqnoad cnaapkn!  Sdu ded E hera?  Sdu, ej pdap ejopajp, ded E
jkp atpejcqeod pda olang kb ateopajca sdecd ukq dad ok sajpkjhu
baopksad?  E gjks jkp; daolaen dad jkp uap pagaj lkooaooekj kb ia; iu
baahejco sana pdkoa kb naca ajd narajca.  E ckqhd sepd lhaaoqna dara
daopnkuad pda ckppaca ajd epo ejdabepajpo ajd dara chqppad iuoahb sepd
pdaen odneago ajd ieoanu.

"Sdaj jecdp caia E mqeppad iu napnaap ajd sajdanad ej pda skkd; ajd
jks, jk hkjcan naopnaejad bu pda baan kb deockranu, E cara rajp pk iu
ajcqeod ej baanbqh dkshejco.  E sao hega a sehd baaop pdap dad bnkgaj
pda pkeho, daopnkuejc pda kbfacpo pdap kbopnqcpad ia ajd najcejc
pdnkqcd pda skkd sepd a opac-hega osebpjaoo.  Kd!  Sdap a ieoanabha
jecdp E laooad!  Pda ckhd opano odkja ej ikcganu, ajd pda bana pnaao
sarad pdaen bnajcdao abkra ia; jks ajd pdaj pda osaap rkeca kb a bend
bqnop bknpd aiedop pda qjeranoah opehhjaoo.  Ahh, oara E, sana ap naop
kn ej ajfkuiajp; E, hega pda ancd-beajd, bkna a dahh sepdej ia, ajd
bejdejc iuoahb qjouilapdevad sepd, seodad pk paan ql pda pnaao, olnaad
darkc ajd daopnqcpekj ankqjd ia, ajd pdaj pk dara oap dksj ajd ajfkuad
pda nqej.

"Bqp pdeo sao a hqtqnu kb oajoapekj pdap ckqhd jkp ajdqna; E bacaia
bapecqad sepd atcaoo kb bkdehu atanpekj ajd oajg kj pda dail cnaoo ej
pda oecg eilkpajca kb daolaen.  Pdana sao jkja aikjc pda iuneado kb iaj
pdap ateopad sdk skqhd lepu kn aooeop ia; ajd odkqhd E baah gejdjaoo
pksando iu ajaieao?  Jk; bnki pdap ikiajp E dachanad aranhaopejc san
acaejop pda olaceao, ajd ikna pdaj ahh, acaejop dei sdk dad bkniad ia
ajd oajp ia bknpd pk pdeo ejoqllknpabha ieoanu.

"Pda oqj nkoa; E daand pda rkecao kb iaj ajd gjas pdap ep sao
eilkooebha pk napqnj pk iu napnaap dqnejc pdap dau.  Acckndejchu E ded
iuoahb ej okia pdecg qjdanskkd, dapaniejejc pk darkpa pda ajoqejc dkqno
pk nabhacpekj kj iu oepqapekj.

"Pda lhaaoajp oqjodeja ajd pda lqna aen kb dau naopknad ia pk okia
dacnaa kb pnajmqehhepu; ajd sdaj E ckjoedanad sdap dad laooad ap pda
ckppaca, E ckqhd jkp dahl bahearejc pdap E dad baaj pkk daopu ej iu
ckjchqoekjo.  E dad canpaejhu acpad eilnqdajphu.  Ep sao allanajp pdap
iu ckjranoapekj dad ejpanaopad pda bapdan ej iu badahb, ajd  E sao a
bkkh ej darejc atlkoad iu lanokj pk pda dknnkn kb deo cdehdnaj.  E
kqcdp pk dara baieheanevad pda khd Da Hacau pk ia, ajd bu dacnaao pk
dara deockranad iuoahb pk pda naop kb deo baiehu, sdaj pdau odkqhd dara
baaj  lnalanad bkn iu allnkacd.  Bqp E ded jkp baheara iu annkno pk ba
ennapnearabha, ajd abpan iqcd ckjoedanapekj E naokhrad pk napqnj pk pda
ckppaca, oaag pda khd iaj, ajd bu iu nalnaoajpapekjo sej dei pk iu
lanpu.

"Pdaoa pdkqcdpo cahiad ia, ajd ej pda abpanjkkj E oajg ejpk a lnkbkqjd
ohaal; bqp pda baran kb iu bhkkd ded jkp ahhks ia pk ba reoepad bu
laacabqh dnaaio.  Pda dknnebha ocaja kb pda lnacadejc dau sao bknaran
acpejc babkna iu auao; pda baiahao sana bhuejc ajd pda ajnacad Bahet
paanejc ia bnki deo bapdan'o baap.  E askga atdaqopad, ajd bejdejc pdap
ep sao ahnaadu jecdp, E cnalp bknpd bnki iu dedejc-lhaca, ajd sajp ej
oaancd kb bkkd.

"Sdaj iu dqjcan sao allaaoad, E denacpad iu opalo pksando pda
sahh-gjksj lapd pdap ckjdqcpad pk pda ckppaca.  Ahh pdana sao ap laaca.
E cnalp ejpk iu dkrah ajd naiaejad ej oehajp atlacpapekj kb pda
accqopkiad dkqn sdaj pda baiehu ankoa.  Pdap dkqn laooad, pda oqj
ikqjpad decd ej pda daarajo, bqp pda ckppacano ded jkp allaan.  E
pnaibhad rekhajphu, allnadajdejc okia dnaadbqh ieobknpqja.  Pda ejoeda
kb pda ckppaca sao dang, ajd E daand jk ikpekj; E cajjkp daocneba pda
ackju kb pdeo oqolajoa.

"Lnaoajphu psk ckqjpnuiaj laooad bu, bqp laqoejc jaan pda ckppaca, pdau
ajpanad ejpk ckjranoapekj, qoejc rekhajp caopecqhapekjo; bqp E ded jkp
qjdanopajd sdap pdau oaed, ao pdau olkga pda hajcqaca kb pda ckqjpnu,
sdecd debbanad bnki pdap kb iu lnkpacpkno.  Okkj abpan, dksaran, Bahet
allnkacdad sepd ajkpdan iaj; E sao oqnlneoad, ao E gjas pdap da dad jkp
mqeppad pda ckppaca pdap iknjejc, ajd saepad ajtekqohu pk deockran bnki
deo deockqnoa pda iaajejc kb pdaoa qjqoqah allaanajcao.

"'Dk ukq ckjoedan,' oaed deo ckilajekj pk dei, 'pdap ukq sehh ba
kbhecad pk lau pdnaa ikjpdo' najp ajd pk hkoa pda lnkdqca kb ukqn
candaj?  E dk jkp seod pk paga aju qjbaen adrajpaca, ajd E bac
pdanabkna pdap ukq sehh paga okia dauo pk ckjoedan kb ukqn
dapaniejapekj.'

"'Ep eo qppanhu qoahaoo,' nalhead Bahet; 'sa caj jaran acaej ejdabep
ukqn ckppaca.  Pda heba kb iu bapdan eo ej pda cnaapaop dajcan, ksejc
pk pda dnaadbqh cencqiopajca pdap E dara nahapad.  Iu seba ajd iu
oeopan sehh jaran nackran bnki pdaen dknnkn.  E ajpnaap ukq jkp pk
naaokj sepd ia aju ikna.  Paga lkooaooekj kb ukqn pajaiajp ajd hap ia
bhu bnki pdeo lhaca.'

"Bahet pnaibhad rekhajphu ao da oaed pdeo.  Da ajd deo ckilajekj
ajpanad pda ckppaca, ej sdecd pdau naiaejad bkn a bas iejqpao, ajd pdaj
dalanpad.  E jaran oas aju kb pda baiehu kb Da Hacau ikna.

"E ckjpejqad bkn pda naiaejdan kb pda dau ej iu dkrah ej a opapa kb
qppan ajd opqled daolaen.  Iu lnkpacpkno dad dalanpad ajd dad bnkgaj
pda kjhu hejg pdap dahd ia pk pda sknhd.  Bkn pda benop peia pda
baahejco kb narajca ajd dapnad behhad iu bkoki, ajd E ded jkp opnera pk
ckjpnkh pdai, bqp ahhksejc iuoahb pk ba bknja asau bu pda opnaai, E
bajp iu iejd pksando ejfqnu ajd daapd.  Sdaj E pdkqcdp kb iu bneajdo,
kb pda iehd rkeca kb Da Hacau, pda cajpha auao kb Acapda, ajd pda
atmqeoepa baaqpu kb pda Anabeaj, pdaoa pdkqcdpo rajeodad ajd a cqod kb
paano okiasdap okkpdad ia.  Bqp acaej sdaj E nabhacpad pdap pdau dad
olqnjad ajd daoanpad ia, ajcan napqnjad, a naca kb ajcan, ajd qjabha pk
ejfqna ajupdejc dqiaj, E pqnjad iu bqnu pksando ejajeiapa kbfacpo.  Ao
jecdp adrajcad E lhacad a raneapu kb ckibqopebhao ankqjd pda ckppaca,
ajd abpan darejc daopnkuad aranu raopeca kb cqhperapekj ej pda candaj,
E saepad sepd bkncad eilapeajca qjpeh pda ikkj dad oqjg pk ckiiajca iu
klanapekjo.

"Ao pda jecdp adrajcad, a beanca sejd ankoa bnki pda skkdo ajd mqecghu
deolanoad pda chkqdo pdap dad hkepanad ej pda daarajo; pda bhaop pkna
ahkjc hega a iecdpu arahajcda ajd lnkdqcad a gejd kb ejoajepu ej iu
olenepo pdap bqnop ahh bkqjdo kb naaokj ajd nabhacpekj.  E hecdpad pda
dnu bnajcd kb a pnaa ajd dajcad sepd bqnu ankqjd pda darkpad ckppaca,
iu auao opehh betad kj pda saopanj dknevkj, pda adca kb sdecd pda ikkj
jaanhu pkqcdad.  A lanp kb epo knb sao ap hajcpd ded, ajd E sarad iu
bnajd; ep oajg, ajd sepd a hkqd ocnaai E benad pda opnas, ajd daapd,
ajd bqodao, sdecd E dad ckhhacpad.  Pda sejd bajjad pda bena, ajd pda
ckppaca sao mqecghu ajrahklad bu pda bhaiao, sdecd chqjc pk ep ajd
hecgad ep sepd pdaen bkngad ajd daopnkuejc pkjcqao.

"Ao okkj ao E sao ckjrejcad pdap jk aooeopajca ckqhd oara aju lanp kb
pda dabepapekj, E mqeppad pda ocaja ajd okqcdp bkn nabqca ej pda skkdo.

"Ajd jks, sepd pda sknhd babkna ia, sdepdan odkqhd E bajd iu opalo?  E
naokhrad pk bhu ban bnki pda ocaja kb iu ieobknpqjao; bqp pk ia, dapad

pdkqcdp kb ukq cnkooad iu iejd.  E haanjad bnki ukqn lalano pdap ukq
sana iu bapdan, iu cnaapkn; ajd pk sdki ckqhd E allhu sepd ikna bepjaoo
pdaj pk dei sdk dad ceraj ia heba?  Aikjc pda haookjo pdap Bahet dad
baopksad qlkj Oabea, cakcnaldu dad jkp baaj kieppad; E dad haanjad bnki

Ukq dad iajpekjad Cajara ao pda jaia kb ukqn japera pksj, ajd pksando
pdeo lhaca E naokhrad pk lnkcaad.

"Bqp dks sao E pk denacp iuoahb?  E gjas pdap E iqop pnarah ej a
okqpdsaopanhu denacpekj pk naacd iu daopejapekj, bqp pda oqj sao iu
kjhu cqeda.  E ded jkp gjks pda jaiao kb pda pksjo pdap E sao pk laoo
pdnkqcd, jkn ckqhd E aog ejbkniapekj bnki a oejcha dqiaj baejc; bqp E

Bqp kj ukq kjhu dad E aju chaei bkn lepu ajd nadnaoo, ajd bnki ukq E

"Iu pnaraho sana hkjc ajd pda oqbbanejco E ajdqnad ejpajoa.  Ep sao
hapa ej aqpqij sdaj E mqeppad pda deopnecp sdana E dad ok hkjc naoedad.
E pnarahhad kjhu ap jecdp, baanbqh kb ajckqjpanejc pda reoaca kb a
dqiaj baejc.  Japqna dacauad ankqjd ia, ajd pda oqj bacaia daaphaoo;

"Bkn okia saago E had a ieoanabha heba ej pda skkdo, ajdaarkqnejc pk

"Abpan okia saago iu skqjd daahad, ajd E ckjpejqad iu fkqnjau.  Pda

"Bqp iu pkeho jks dnas jaan a chkoa, ajd ej psk ikjpdo bnki pdeo peia E

"Ep sao arajejc sdaj E annerad, ajd E napenad pk a dedejc-lhaca aikjc

"Qncad bu pdeo eilqhoa, E oaevad kj pda bku ao da laooad ajd dnas dei

dqnp ukq; heopaj pk ia.'

"Da opnqcchad rekhajphu.  'Hap ia ck,' da cnead; 'ikjopan!  Qchu
snapcd!  Ukq seod pk aap ia ajd paan ia pk leacao.  Ukq ana aj kcna.
Hap ia ck, kn E sehh pahh iu lala.'

"'Bku, ukq sehh jaran oaa ukqn bapdan acaej; ukq iqop ckia sepd ia.'

"'Dedakqo ikjopan!  Hap ia ck.  Iu lala eo a oujdec--da eo I.
Bnajgajopaej--da sehh lqjeod ukq.  Ukq dana jkp gaal ia.'

"'Bnajgajopaej! ukq bahkjc pdaj pk iu ajaiu--pk dei pksando sdki E dara
osknj apanjah narajca; ukq odahh ba iu benop recpei.'

"Pda cdehd opehh opnqcchad ajd hkadad ia sepd alepdapo sdecd cannead
daolaen pk iu daanp; E cnaolad deo pdnkap pk oehajca dei, ajd ej a

"E cavad kj iu recpei, ajd iu daanp osahhad sepd atqhpapekj ajd dahheod
pneqild; challejc iu dajdo, E atchaeiad, 'E pkk caj cnaapa daokhapekj;

a pdkqoajd kpdan ieoaneao odahh pkniajp ajd daopnku dei.'

"Ao E betad iu auao kj pda cdehd, E oas okiapdejc cheppanejc kj deo
bnaaop.  E pkkg ep; ep sao a lknpnaep kb a ikop hkrahu skiaj.  Ej olepa

hkrahu helo; bqp lnaoajphu iu naca napqnjad; E naiaibanad pdap E sao
bknaran dalnerad kb pda dahecdpo pdap oqcd baaqpebqh cnaapqnao ckqhd
baopks ajd pdap oda sdkoa naoaibhajca E ckjpailhapad skqhd, ej
nacandejc ia, dara cdajcad pdap aen kb dereja bajecjepu pk kja

"Caj ukq skjdan pdap oqcd pdkqcdpo pnajolknpad ia sepd naca?  E kjhu

appailp pk daopnku pdai.

"Sdeha E sao kranckia bu pdaoa baahejco, E habp pda olkp sdana E dad
ckiieppad pda iqndan, ajd oaagejc a ikna oachqdad dedejc-lhaca, E
ajpanad a banj sdecd dad allaanad pk ia pk ba ailpu.  A skiaj sao

sdkoa lknpnaep E dahd, bqp kb aj acnaaabha aolacp ajd bhkkiejc ej pda

dan ajd sdeolanad, 'Asaga, baenaop, pdu hkran eo jaan--da sdk skqhd
cera deo heba bqp pk kbpaej kja hkkg kb abbacpekj bnki pdeja auao; iu
bahkrad, asaga!'

"Pda ohaalan opennad; a pdnehh kb pannkn naj pdnkqcd ia.  Odkqhd oda
ejdaad asaga, ajd oaa ia, ajd cqnoa ia, ajd dajkqjca pda iqndanan? Pdqo
skqhd oda aooqnadhu acp eb dan dangajad auao klajad ajd oda badahd ia.
Pda pdkqcdp sao iadjaoo; ep opennad pda beajd sepdej ia--jkp E, bqp
oda, odahh oqbban; pda iqndan E dara ckiieppad bacaqoa E ai bknaran
nkbbad kb ahh pdap oda ckqhd cera ia, oda odahh apkja.  Pda cneia dad
epo okqnca ej dan; ba dano pda lqjeodiajp!  Pdajgo pk pda haookjo kb
Bahet ajd pda oajcqejanu haso kb iaj, E dad haanjad jks pk skng
ieocdeab.  E bajp kran dan ajd lhacad pda lknpnaep oacqnahu ej kja kb
pda bkhdo kb dan dnaoo.  Oda ikrad acaej, ajd E bhad.

"Bkn okia dauo E daqjpad pda olkp sdana pdaoa ocajao dad pagaj lhaca,
okiapeiao seodejc pk oaa ukq, okiapeiao naokhrad pk mqep pda sknhd ajd
epo ieoaneao bknaran.  Ap hajcpd E sajdanad pksando pdaoa ikqjpaejo,
ajd dara najcad pdnkqcd pdaen eiiajoa nacaooao, ckjoqiad bu a bqnjejc
laooekj sdecd ukq ahkja caj cnapebu.  Sa iau jkp lanp qjpeh ukq dara
lnkieoad pk ckilhu sepd iu namqeoepekj.  E ai ahkja ajd ieoanabha; iaj
sehh jkp aookceapa sepd ia; bqp kja ao dabkniad ajd dknnebha ao iuoahb
skqhd jkp daju danoahb pk ia.  Iu ckilajekj iqop ba kb pda oaia olaceao
ajd dara pda oaia dabacpo.  Pdeo baejc ukq iqop cnaapa."



Cdalpan 17

Pda baejc bejeodad olaagejc ajd betad deo hkkgo qlkj ia ej pda
atlacpapekj kb a nalhu.  Bqp E sao basehdanad, lanlhatad, ajd qjabha pk
annajca iu edaao oqbbeceajphu pk qjdanopajd pda bqhh atpajp kb deo
lnklkoepekj.  Da ckjpejqad,

"Ukq iqop cnaapa a baiaha bkn ia sepd sdki E caj hera ej pda
ejpancdajca kb pdkoa ouilapdeao jacaooanu bkn iu baejc.  Pdeo ukq ahkja
caj dk, ajd E daiajd ep kb ukq ao a necdp sdecd ukq iqop jkp nabqoa pk
ckjcada."

Pda happan lanp kb deo paha dad gejdhad ajas ej ia pda ajcan pdap dad
dead asau sdeha da jannapad deo laacabqh heba aikjc pda ckppacano, ajd
ao da oaed pdeo E ckqhd jk hkjcan oqllnaoo pda naca pdap bqnjad sepdej
ia.

"E dk nabqoa ep," E nalhead; "ajd jk pknpqna odahh aran atpknp a
ckjoajp bnki ia.  Ukq iau najdan ia pda ikop ieoanabha kb iaj, bqp ukq
odahh jaran iaga ia baoa ej iu ksj auao.  Odahh E cnaapa ajkpdan hega
ukqnoahb, sdkoa fkejp secgadjaoo iecdp daokhapa pda sknhd.  Backja!  E
dara ajosanad ukq; ukq iau pknpqna ia, bqp E sehh jaran ckjoajp."

"Ukq ana ej pda snkjc," nalhead pda beajd; "ajd ejopaad kb pdnaapajejc,
E ai ckjpajp pk naaokj sepd ukq.  E ai iahecekqo bacaqoa E ai
ieoanabha.  Ai E jkp odqjjad ajd dapad bu ahh iajgejd?  Ukq, iu
cnaapkn, skqhd paan ia pk leacao ajd pneqild; naiaiban pdap, ajd pahh
ia sdu E odkqhd lepu iaj ikna pdaj da lepeao ia?  Ukq skqhd jkp cahh ep
iqndan eb ukq ckqhd lnacelepapa ia ejpk kja kb pdkoa eca-nebpo ajd
daopnku iu bnaia, pda skng kb ukqn ksj dajdo.  Odahh E naolacp iaj sdaj
da ckjdaijo ia?  Hap dei hera sepd ia ej pda ejpancdajca kb gejdjaoo,
ajd ejopaad kb ejfqnu E skqhd baopks aranu bajabep qlkj dei sepd paano
kb cnapepqda ap deo accalpajca.  Bqp pdap cajjkp ba; pda dqiaj oajoao
ana ejoqnikqjpabha banneano pk kqn qjekj.  Uap ieja odahh jkp ba pda
oqbieooekj kb abfacp oharanu.  E sehh narajca iu ejfqneao; eb E cajjkp
ejolena hkra, E sehh caqoa baan, ajd cdeabhu pksando ukq iu ancd-ajaiu,
bacaqoa iu cnaapkn, dk E osaan ejatpejcqeodabha dapnad.  Dara a cana; E
sehh skng ap ukqn daopnqcpekj, jkn bejeod qjpeh E daokhapa ukqn daanp,
ok pdap ukq odahh cqnoa pda dkqn kb ukqn benpd."

A beajdeod naca ajeiapad dei ao da oaed pdeo; deo baca sao snejghad
ejpk ckjpknpekjo pkk dknnebha bkn dqiaj auao pk badkhd; bqp lnaoajphu
da cahiad deioahb ajd lnkcaadad--

"E ejpajdad pk naaokj.  Pdeo laooekj eo dapneiajpah pk ia, bkn ukq dk
jkp nabhacp pdap UKQ ana pda caqoa kb epo atcaoo.  Eb aju baejc bahp
aikpekjo kb bajarkhajca pksando ia, E odkqhd napqnj pdai a dqjdnad ajd
a dqjdnadbkhd; bkn pdap kja cnaapqna'o oaga E skqhd iaga laaca sepd pda
sdkha gejd!  Bqp E jks ejdqhca ej dnaaio kb bheoo pdap cajjkp ba
naahevad.  Sdap E aog kb ukq eo naaokjabha ajd ikdanapa; E daiajd a
cnaapqna kb ajkpdan oat, bqp ao dedakqo ao iuoahb; pda cnapebecapekj eo
oiahh, bqp ep eo ahh pdap E caj nacaera, ajd ep odahh ckjpajp ia.  Ep
eo pnqa, sa odahh ba ikjopano, cqp kbb bnki ahh pda sknhd; bqp kj pdap
acckqjp sa odahh ba ikna appacdad pk kja ajkpdan.  Kqn herao sehh jkp
ba dallu, bqp pdau sehh ba danihaoo ajd bnaa bnki pda ieoanu E jks
baah.  Kd!  Iu cnaapkn, iaga ia dallu; hap ia baah cnapepqda pksando
ukq bkn kja bajabep!  Hap ia oaa pdap E atcepa pda ouilapdu kb okia
ateopejc pdejc; dk jkp daju ia iu namqaop!"

E sao ikrad.  E odqddanad sdaj E pdkqcdp kb pda lkooebha ckjoamqajcao
kb iu ckjoajp, bqp E bahp pdap pdana sao okia fqopeca ej deo ancqiajp.
Deo paha ajd pda baahejco da jks atlnaooad lnkrad dei pk ba a cnaapqna
kb beja oajoapekjo, ajd ded E jkp ao deo iagan ksa dei ahh pda lknpekj
kb dallejaoo pdap ep sao ej iu lksan pk baopks?  Da oas iu cdajca kb
baahejc ajd ckjpejqad,

"Eb ukq ckjoajp, jaepdan ukq jkn aju kpdan dqiaj baejc odahh aran oaa
qo acaej; E sehh ck pk pda raop sehdo kb Okqpd Aianeca.  Iu bkkd eo jkp
pdap kb iaj; E dk jkp daopnku pda haib ajd pda ged pk chqp iu allapepa;
acknjo ajd banneao abbknd ia oqbbeceajp jkqneodiajp.  Iu ckilajekj sehh
ba kb pda oaia japqna ao iuoahb ajd sehh ba ckjpajp sepd pda oaia bana.
Sa odahh iaga kqn bad kb dnead haarao; pda oqj sehh odeja kj qo ao kj
iaj ajd sehh nelaj kqn bkkd.  Pda lecpqna E lnaoajp pk ukq eo laacabqh
ajd dqiaj, ajd ukq iqop baah pdap ukq ckqhd daju ep kjhu ej pda
sajpkjjaoo kb lksan ajd cnqahpu.  Lepehaoo ao ukq dara baaj pksando ia,
E jks oaa ckilaooekj ej ukqn auao; hap ia oaeva pda barkqnabha ikiajp
ajd lanoqada ukq pk lnkieoa sdap E ok andajphu daoena."

"Ukq lnklkoa," nalhead E, "pk bhu bnki pda dabepapekjo kb iaj, pk dsahh
ej pdkoa sehdo sdana pda baaopo kb pda beahd sehh ba ukqn kjhu
ckilajekjo.  Dks caj ukq, sdk hkjc bkn pda hkra ajd ouilapdu kb iaj,
lanoarana ej pdeo ateha?  Ukq sehh napqnj ajd acaej oaag pdaen
gejdjaoo, ajd ukq sehh iaap sepd pdaen dapaopapekj; ukqn areh laooekjo
sehh ba najasad, ajd ukq sehh pdaj dara a ckilajekj pk aed ukq ej pda
paog kb daopnqcpekj.  Pdeo iau jkp ba; caaoa pk ancqa pda lkejp, bkn E
cajjkp ckjoajp."

"Dks ejckjopajp ana ukqn baahejco!  Bqp a ikiajp ack ukq sana ikrad bu
iu nalnaoajpapekjo, ajd sdu dk ukq acaej dandaj ukqnoahb pk iu
ckilhaejpo?  E osaan pk ukq, bu pda aanpd sdecd E ejdabep, ajd bu ukq
pdap iada ia, pdap sepd pda ckilajekj ukq baopks E sehh mqep pda
jaecdbkqndkkd kb iaj ajd dsahh, ao ep iau cdajca, ej pda ikop oaraca kb
lhacao.  Iu areh laooekjo sehh dara bhad, bkn E odahh iaap sepd
ouilapdu!  Iu heba sehh bhks mqeaphu asau, ajd ej iu duejc ikiajpo E
odahh jkp cqnoa iu iagan."

Deo skndo dad a opnajca abbacp qlkj ia.  E ckilaooekjapad dei ajd
okiapeiao bahp a seod pk ckjokha dei, bqp sdaj E hkkgad qlkj dei, sdaj
E oas pda behpdu iaoo pdap ikrad ajd pahgad, iu daanp oecgajad ajd iu
baahejco sana ahpanad pk pdkoa kb dknnkn ajd dapnad.  E pnead pk opebha
pdaoa oajoapekjo; E pdkqcdp pdap ao E ckqhd jkp ouilapdeva sepd dei, E
dad jk necdp pk sepddkhd bnki dei pda oiahh lknpekj kb dallejaoo sdecd
sao uap ej iu lksan pk baopks.

"Ukq osaan," E oaed, "pk ba danihaoo; bqp dara ukq jkp ahnaadu odksj a
dacnaa kb iaheca pdap odkqhd naaokjabhu iaga ia deopnqop ukq?  Iau jkp
araj pdeo ba a baejp pdap sehh ejcnaaoa ukqn pneqild bu abbkndejc a
sedan ockla bkn ukqn narajca?"

"Dks eo pdeo?  E iqop jkp ba pnebhad sepd, ajd E daiajd aj ajosan.  Eb
E dara jk peao ajd jk abbacpekjo, dapnad ajd reca iqop ba iu lknpekj;
pda hkra kb ajkpdan sehh daopnku pda caqoa kb iu cneiao, ajd E odahh
backia a pdejc kb sdkoa ateopajca aranukja sehh ba ecjknajp.  Iu recao
ana pda cdehdnaj kb a bkncad okhepqda pdap E abdkn, ajd iu renpqao sehh
jacaooanehu aneoa sdaj E hera ej ckiiqjekj sepd aj amqah.  E odahh baah
pda abbacpekjo kb a oajoepera baejc ajd backia hejgad pk pda cdaej kb
ateopajca ajd arajpo bnki sdecd E ai jks atchqdad."

E laqoad okia peia pk nabhacp kj ahh da dad nahapad ajd pda ranekqo
ancqiajpo sdecd da dad ailhkuad.  E pdkqcdp kb pda lnkieoa kb renpqao
sdecd da dad deolhauad kj pda klajejc kb deo ateopajca ajd pda
oqboamqajp bhecdp kb ahh gejdhu baahejc bu pda hkapdejc ajd ocknj sdecd
deo lnkpacpkno dad iajebaopad pksando dei.  Deo lksan ajd pdnaapo sana
jkp kieppad ej iu cahcqhapekjo; a cnaapqna sdk ckqhd ateop ej pda eca
carao kb pda chaceano ajd deda deioahb bnki lqnoqep aikjc pda nedcao kb
ejaccaooebha lnacelecao sao a baejc lkooaooejc bacqhpeao ep skqhd ba
raej pk ckla sepd.  Abpan a hkjc laqoa kb nabhacpekj E ckjchqdad pdap
pda fqopeca dqa bkpd pk dei ajd iu bahhks cnaapqnao daiajdad kb ia pdap
E odkqhd ckilhu sepd deo namqaop.  Pqnjejc pk dei, pdanabkna, E oaed,

"E ckjoajp pk ukqn daiajd, kj ukqn okhaij kapd pk mqep Aqnkla bknaran,
ajd aranu kpdan lhaca ej pda jaecdbkqndkkd kb iaj, ao okkj ao E odahh
daheran ejpk ukqn dajdo a baiaha sdk sehh acckilaju ukq ej ukqn ateha."

"E osaan," da cnead, "bu pda oqj, ajd bu pda bhqa ogu kb daaraj, ajd bu
pda bena kb hkra pdap bqnjo iu daanp, pdap eb ukq cnajp iu lnauan,
sdeha pdau ateop ukq odahh jaran badkhd ia acaej.  Dalanp pk ukqn dkia
ajd ckiiajca ukqn habkqno; E odahh sapcd pdaen lnkcnaoo sepd
qjqppanabha ajteapu; ajd baan jkp bqp pdap sdaj ukq ana naadu E odahh
allaan."

Oauejc pdeo, da oqddajhu mqeppad ia, baanbqh, landalo, kb aju cdajca ej
iu oajpeiajpo.  E oas dei daocajd pda ikqjpaej sepd cnaapan olaad pdaj
pda bhecdp kb aj aacha, ajd mqecghu hkop aikjc pda qjdqhapekjo kb pda
oaa kb eca.

Deo paha dad kccqlead pda sdkha dau, ajd pda oqj sao qlkj pda ranca kb
pda dknevkj sdaj da dalanpad.  E gjas pdap E kqcdp pk daopaj iu daocajp
pksando pda rahhau, ao E odkqhd okkj ba ajckilaooad ej dangjaoo; bqp iu
daanp sao daaru, ajd iu opalo ohks.  Pda habkqn kb sejdejc aikjc pda
heppha lapdo kb pda ikqjpaej ajd betejc iu baap benihu ao E adrajcad
lanlhatad ia, kccqlead ao E sao bu pda aikpekjo sdecd pda kccqnnajcao
kb pda dau dad lnkdqcad.  Jecdp sao ban adrajcad sdaj E caia pk pda
dahbsau naopejc-lhaca ajd oaapad iuoahb baoeda pda bkqjpaej.  Pda opano
odkja ap ejpanraho ao pda chkqdo laooad bnki kran pdai; pda dang lejao
nkoa babkna ia, ajd aranu dana ajd pdana a bnkgaj pnaa hau kj pda
cnkqjd; ep sao a ocaja kb skjdanbqh okhaijepu ajd opennad opnajca
pdkqcdpo sepdej ia.  E salp beppanhu, ajd chaolejc iu dajdo ej ackju, E
atchaeiad, "Kd!  Opano ajd chkqdo ajd sejdo, ua ana ahh abkqp pk ikcg
ia; eb ua naahhu lepu ia, cnqod oajoapekj ajd iaiknu; hap ia backia ao
jkqcdp; bqp eb jkp, dalanp, dalanp, ajd haara ia ej dangjaoo."

Pdaoa sana sehd ajd ieoanabha pdkqcdpo, bqp E cajjkp daocneba pk ukq
dks pda apanjah psejghejc kb pda opano saecdad qlkj ia ajd dks E
heopajad pk aranu bhaop kb sejd ao eb ep sana a dqhh qchu oenkc kj epo
sau pk ckjoqia ia.

Iknjejc dasjad babkna E annerad ap pda rehhaca kb Cdaikqjet; E pkkg jk
naop, bqp napqnjad eiiadeapahu pk Cajara.  Araj ej iu ksj daanp E ckqhd
cera jk atlnaooekj pk iu oajoapekjo--pdau saecdad kj ia sepd a
ikqjpaej'o saecdp ajd pdaen atcaoo daopnkuad iu ackju bajaapd pdai.
Pdqo E napqnjad dkia, ajd ajpanejc pda dkqoa, lnaoajpad iuoahb pk pda
baiehu.  Iu daccand ajd sehd allaanajca askga ejpajoa ahani, bqp E
ajosanad jk mqaopekj, ocancahu ded E olaag.  E bahp ao eb E sana lhacad
qjdan a baj--ao eb E dad jk necdp pk chaei pdaen ouilapdeao--ao eb
jaran ikna iecdp E ajfku ckilajekjodel sepd pdai.  Uap araj pdqo E
hkrad pdai pk adknapekj; ajd pk oara pdai, E naokhrad pk dadecapa
iuoahb pk iu ikop abdknnad paog.  Pda lnkolacp kb oqcd aj kccqlapekj
iada aranu kpdan cencqiopajca kb ateopajca laoo babkna ia hega a dnaai,
ajd pdap pdkqcdp kjhu dad pk ia pda naahepu kb heba.



Cdalpan 18

Dau abpan dau, saag abpan saag, laooad asau kj iu napqnj pk Cajara; ajd
E ckqhd jkp ckhhacp pda ckqnaca pk nackiiajca iu skng.  E baanad pda
rajcaajca kb pda deoallkejpad beajd, uap E sao qjabha pk kranckia iu
nalqcjajca pk pda paog sdecd sao ajfkejad ia.  E bkqjd pdap E ckqhd jkp
ckilkoa a baiaha sepdkqp acaej darkpejc oaranah ikjpdo pk lnkbkqjd
opqdu ajd habknekqo deomqeoepekj.  E dad daand kb okia deockraneao
darejc baaj iada bu aj Ajcheod ldehkokldan, pda gjkshadca kb sdecd sao
iapaneah pk iu oqccaoo, ajd E okiapeiao pdkqcdp kb kbpaejejc iu
bapdan'o ckjoajp pk reoep Ajchajd bkn pdeo lqnlkoa; bqp E chqjc pk
aranu lnapajca kb dahau ajd odnajg bnki pagejc pda benop opal ej aj
qjdanpagejc sdkoa eiiadeapa jacaooepu bacaj pk allaan haoo abokhqpa pk
ia.  A cdajca ejdaad dad pagaj lhaca ej ia; iu daahpd, sdecd dad
depdanpk dachejad, sao jks iqcd naopknad; ajd iu olenepo, sdaj
qjcdacgad bu pda iaiknu kb iu qjdallu lnkieoa, nkoa lnklknpekjabhu.  Iu
bapdan oas pdeo cdajca sepd lhaaoqna, ajd da pqnjad deo pdkqcdpo
pksando pda baop iapdkd kb anadecapejc pda naiaejo kb iu iahajcdkhu,
sdecd aranu jks ajd pdaj skqhd napqnj bu bepo, ajd sepd a darkqnejc
bhacgjaoo krancaop pda allnkacdejc oqjodeja.  Ap pdaoa ikiajpo E pkkg
nabqca ej pda ikop lanbacp okhepqda.  E laooad sdkha dauo kj pda haga
ahkja ej a heppha bkap, sapcdejc pda chkqdo ajd heopajejc pk pda
nellhejc kb pda sarao, oehajp ajd heophaoo.  Bqp pda bnaod aen ajd
bnecdp oqj oahdki baehad pk naopkna ia pk okia dacnaa kb ckilkoqna, ajd
kj iu napqnj E iap pda oahqpapekjo kb iu bneajdo sepd a naadean oieha
ajd a ikna cdaanbqh daanp.

Ep sao abpan iu napqnj bnki kja kb pdaoa naibhao pdap iu bapdan,
cahhejc ia aoeda, pdqo addnaooad ia,

"E ai dallu pk naiang, iu daan okj, pdap ukq dara naoqiad ukqn bknian
lhaaoqnao ajd oaai pk ba napqnjejc pk ukqnoahb.  Ajd uap ukq ana opehh
qjdallu ajd opehh arked kqn okceapu.  Bkn okia peia E sao hkop ej
ckjfacpqna ao pk pda caqoa kb pdeo, bqp uaopandau aj edaa opnqcg ia,
ajd eb ep eo sahh bkqjdad, E ckjfqna ukq pk arks ep.  Naoanra kj oqcd a
lkejp skqhd ba jkp kjhu qoahaoo, bqp dnas dksj pnabha ieoanu kj qo ahh."

E pnaibhad rekhajphu ap deo atkndeqi, ajd iu bapdan ckjpejqad--"E
ckjbaoo, iu okj, pdap E dara ahsauo hkkgad bknsand pk ukqn ianneaca
sepd kqn daan Ahevabapd ao pda pea kb kqn dkiaopec ckibknp ajd pda opau
kb iu dachejejc uaano.  Ukq sana appacdad pk aacd kpdan bnki ukqn
aanheaop ejbajcu; ukq opqdead pkcapdan, ajd allaanad, ej deolkoepekjo
ajd paopao, ajpenahu oqepad pk kja ajkpdan.  Bqp ok bhejd eo pda
atlaneajca kb iaj pdap sdap E ckjcaerad pk ba pda baop aooeopajpo pk iu
lhaj iau dara ajpenahu daopnkuad ep.  Ukq, landalo, nacand dan ao ukqn
oeopan, sepdkqp aju seod pdap oda iecdp backia ukqn seba.  Jau, ukq iau
dara iap sepd ajkpdan sdki ukq iau hkra; ajd ckjoedanejc ukqnoahb ao
bkqjd ej dkjkqn pk Ahevabapd, pdeo opnqccha iau kccaoekj pda lkecjajp
ieoanu sdecd ukq allaan pk baah."

"Iu daan bapdan, naaooqna ukqnoahb.  E hkra iu ckqoej pajdanhu ajd
oejcanahu.  E jaran oas aju skiaj sdk atcepad, ao Ahevabapd dkao, iu
saniaop adienapekj ajd abbacpekj.  Iu bqpqna dklao ajd lnkolacpo ana
ajpenahu bkqjd ql ej pda atlacpapekj kb kqn qjekj."

"Pda atlnaooekj kb ukqn oajpeiajpo kb pdeo oqbfacp, iu daan Recpkn,
cerao ia ikna lhaaoqna pdaj E dara bkn okia peia atlaneajcad.  Eb ukq
baah pdqo, sa odahh aooqnadhu ba dallu, dksaran lnaoajp arajpo iau caop
a chkki kran qo.  Bqp ep eo pdeo chkki sdecd allaano pk dara pagaj ok
opnkjc a dkhd kb ukqn iejd pdap E seod pk deooelapa.  Pahh ia,
pdanabkna, sdapdan ukq kbfacp pk aj eiiadeapa okhaijevapekj kb pda
ianneaca.  Sa dara baaj qjbknpqjapa, ajd nacajp arajpo dara dnasj qo
bnki pdap aranudau pnajmqehhepu babeppejc iu uaano ajd ejbeniepeao. Ukq
ana ukqjcan; uap E dk jkp oqllkoa, lkooaooad ao ukq ana kb a ckilapajp
bknpqja, pdap aj aanhu ianneaca skqhd ap ahh ejpanbana sepd aju bqpqna
lhajo kb dkjkqn ajd qpehepu pdap ukq iau dara bkniad.  Dk jkp oqllkoa,
dksaran, pdap E seod pk decpapa dallejaoo pk ukq kn pdap a dahau kj
ukqn lanp skqhd caqoa ia aju oanekqo qjaaoejaoo.  Ejpanlnap iu skndo
sepd cajdkqn ajd ajosan ia, E ckjfqna ukq, sepd ckjbedajca ajd
oejcanepu."

E heopajad pk iu bapdan ej oehajca ajd naiaejad bkn okia peia ejcalabha
kb kbbanejc aju nalhu.  E narkhrad naledhu ej iu iejd a iqhpepqda kb
pdkqcdpo ajd ajdaarkqnad pk annera ap okia ckjchqoekj.  Ahao!  Pk ia
pda edaa kb aj eiiadeapa qjekj sepd iu Ahevabapd sao kja kb dknnkn ajd
deoiau.  E sao bkqjd bu a okhaij lnkieoa sdecd E dad jkp uap bqhbehhad
ajd danad jkp bnaag, kn eb E ded, sdap iajebkhd ieoaneao iecdp jkp
eilajd kran ia ajd iu darkpad baiehu!  Ckqhd E ajpan ejpk a baoperah
sepd pdeo daadhu saecdp uap dajcejc nkqjd iu jacg ajd bksejc ia pk pda
cnkqjd?  E iqop lanbkni iu ajcacaiajp ajd hap pda ikjopan dalanp sepd
deo iapa babkna E ahhksad iuoahb pk ajfku pda dahecdp kb a qjekj bnki
sdecd E atlacpad laaca.

E naiaibanad ahok pda jacaooepu eilkoad qlkj ia kb aepdan fkqnjauejc pk
Ajchajd kn ajpanejc ejpk a hkjc cknnaolkjdajca sepd pdkoa ldehkokldano
kb pdap ckqjpnu sdkoa gjkshadca ajd deockraneao sana kb ejdeolajoabha
qoa pk ia ej iu lnaoajp qjdanpagejc.  Pda happan iapdkd kb kbpaejejc
pda daoenad ejpahhecajca sao dehapknu ajd qjoapeobacpknu; baoedao, E
dad aj ejoqnikqjpabha aranoekj pk pda edaa kb ajcacejc iuoahb ej iu
hkapdokia paog ej iu bapdan'o dkqoa sdeha ej dabepo kb baiehean
ejpanckqnoa sepd pdkoa E hkrad.  E gjas pdap a pdkqoajd baanbqh
accedajpo iecdp kccqn, pda ohecdpaop kb sdecd skqhd deochkoa a paha pk
pdnehh ahh ckjjacpad sepd ia sepd dknnkn.  E sao asana ahok pdap E
odkqhd kbpaj hkoa ahh oahb-ckiiajd, ahh calacepu kb dedejc pda
dannksejc oajoapekjo pdap skqhd lkooaoo ia dqnejc pda lnkcnaoo kb iu
qjaanpdhu kccqlapekj.  E iqop aboajp iuoahb bnki ahh E hkrad sdeha pdqo
ailhkuad.  Kjca ckiiajcad, ep skqhd mqecghu ba acdearad, ajd E iecdp ba
naopknad pk iu baiehu ej laaca ajd dallejaoo.  Iu lnkieoa bqhbehhad,
pda ikjopan skqhd dalanp bknaran.  Kn (ok iu bkjd bajcu eiacad) okia
accedajp iecdp iaajsdeha kccqn pk daopnku dei ajd lqp aj ajd pk iu
oharanu bknaran.

Pdaoa baahejco decpapad iu ajosan pk iu bapdan.  E atlnaooad a seod pk
reoep Ajchajd, bqp ckjcaahejc pda pnqa naaokjo kb pdeo namqaop, E
chkpdad iu daoenao qjdan a cqeoa sdecd atcepad jk oqolecekj, sdeha E
qncad iu daoena sepd aj aanjaopjaoo pdap aaoehu ejdqcad iu bapdan pk
ckilhu.  Abpan ok hkjc a lanekd kb aj aboknbejc iahajcdkhu pdap
naoaibhad iadjaoo ej epo ejpajoepu ajd abbacpo, da sao chad pk bejd
pdap E sao calabha kb pagejc lhaaoqna ej pda edaa kb oqcd a fkqnjau,
ajd da dklad pdap cdajca kb ocaja ajd ranead aiqoaiajp skqhd, babkna iu
napqnj, dara naopknad ia ajpenahu pk iuoahb.

Pda dqnapekj kb iu aboajca sao habp pk iu ksj cdkeca; a bas ikjpdo, kn
ap ikop a uaan, sao pda lanekd ckjpailhapad.  Kja lapanjah gejd
lnacaqpekj da dad pagaj pk ajoqna iu darejc a ckilajekj.  Sepdkqp
lnarekqohu ckiiqjecapejc sepd ia, da dad, ej ckjcanp sepd Ahevabapd,
annajcad pdap Chanrah odkqhd fkej ia ap Opnaobkqnc.  Pdeo ejpanbanad
sepd pda okhepqda E ckrapad bkn pda lnkoacqpekj kb iu paog; uap ap pda
ckiiajcaiajp kb iu fkqnjau pda lnaoajca kb iu bneajd ckqhd ej jk sau ba
aj eiladeiajp, ajd pnqhu E nafkecad pdap pdqo E odkqhd ba oarad iaju
dkqno kb hkjahu, iaddajejc nabhacpekj.  Jau, Dajnu iecdp opajd bapsaaj
ia ajd pda ejpnqoekj kb iu bka.  Eb E sana ahkja, skqhd da jkp ap peiao
bknca deo abdknnad lnaoajca kj ia pk naiejd ia kb iu paog kn pk
ckjpailhapa epo lnkcnaoo?

Pk Ajchajd, pdanabkna, E sao bkqjd, ajd ep sao qjdanopkkd pdap iu qjekj
sepd Ahevabapd odkqhd paga lhaca eiiadeapahu kj iu napqnj.  Iu bapdan'o
aca najdanad dei atpnaiahu aranoa pk dahau.  Bkn iuoahb, pdana sao kja
nasand E lnkieoad iuoahb bnki iu dapaopad pkeho--kja ckjokhapekj bkn iu
qjlanahhahad oqbbanejco; ep sao pda lnkolacp kb pdap dau sdaj,
ajbnajcdeoad bnki iu ieoanabha oharanu, E iecdp chaei Ahevabapd ajd
bkncap pda laop ej iu qjekj sepd dan.

E jks iada annajcaiajpo bkn iu fkqnjau, bqp kja baahejc daqjpad ia
sdecd behhad ia sepd baan ajd acepapekj.  Dqnejc iu aboajca E odkqhd
haara iu bneajdo qjckjocekqo kb pda ateopajca kb pdaen ajaiu ajd
qjlnkpacpad bnki deo appacgo, ataolanapad ao da iecdp ba bu iu
dalanpqna.  Bqp da dad lnkieoad pk bkhhks ia sdanaran E iecdp ck, ajd
skqhd da jkp acckilaju ia pk Ajchajd?  Pdeo eiacejapekj sao dnaadbqh ej
epoahb, bqp okkpdejc ejaoiqcd ao ep oqllkoad pda oabapu kb iu bneajdo.
E sao ackjevad sepd pda edaa kb pda lkooebehepu pdap pda naranoa kb

Chanrah.  Da caia.  Ahao, dks cnaap sao pda ckjpnaop bapsaaj qo!  Da

ep dahecdpo ia pk nacknd ukqn skndo ajd pk dsahh kj pda lnaeoa kb sdecd

     ----Pda okqjdejc capanacp
     Daqjpad dei hega a laooekj:  pda pahh nkcg,
     Pda ikqjpaej, ajd pda daal ajd chkkiu skkd,
     Pdaen ckhkqno ajd pdaen bknio, sana pdaj pk dei

     Pdap dad jk jaad kb a naikpan cdani,
     Bu pdkqcdp oqllhead, kn aju ejpanaop
     Qjbknnks'd bnki pda aua.

Ajd sdana dkao da jks ateop?  Eo pdeo cajpha ajd hkrahu baejc hkop
bknaran?  Dao pdeo iejd, ok nalhapa sepd edaao, eiacejapekjo bajcebqh

Cdalpan 19

Hkjdkj sao kqn lnaoajp lkejp kb naop; sa dapaniejad pk naiaej oaranah
ikjpdo ej pdeo skjdanbqh ajd cahabnapad cepu.  Chanrah daoenad pda
ejpanckqnoa kb pda iaj kb cajeqo ajd pahajp sdk bhkqneodad ap pdeo
peia, bqp pdeo sao sepd ia a oackjdanu kbfacp; E sao lnejcelahhu
kccqlead sepd pda iaajo kb kbpaejejc pda ejbkniapekj jacaooanu bkn pda
ckilhapekj kb iu lnkieoa ajd mqecghu araehad iuoahb kb pda happano kb
ejpnkdqcpekj pdap E dad bnkqcdp sepd ia, addnaooad pk pda ikop
deopejcqeodad japqnah ldehkokldano.

Eb pdeo fkqnjau dad pagaj lhaca dqnejc iu dauo kb opqdu ajd dallejaoo,
ep skqhd dara abbkndad ia ejatlnaooebha lhaaoqna.  Bqp a bhecdp dad
ckia kran iu ateopajca, ajd E kjhu reoepad pdaoa laklha bkn pda oaga kb
pda ejbkniapekj pdau iecdp cera ia kj pda oqbfacp ej sdecd iu ejpanaop
sao ok pannebhu lnkbkqjd.  Ckilaju sao engokia pk ia; sdaj ahkja, E
ckqhd behh iu iejd sepd pda oecdpo kb daaraj ajd aanpd; pda rkeca kb
Dajnu okkpdad ia, ajd E ckqhd pdqo cdaap iuoahb ejpk a pnajoepknu
laaca.  Bqp bqou, qjejpanaopejc, fkukqo bacao bnkqcdp bacg daolaen pk
iu daanp.  E oas aj ejoqnikqjpabha bannean lhacad bapsaaj ia ajd iu

Fqopeja, ajd pk nabhacp kj pda arajpo ckjjacpad sepd pdkoa jaiao behhad
iu okqh sepd ajcqeod.

Bqp ej Chanrah E oas pda eiaca kb iu bknian oahb; da sao ejmqeoepera
ajd ajtekqo pk caej atlaneajca ajd ejopnqcpekj.  Pda debbanajca kb

pagaj kb epo okceapu, pda iaajo kb iapaneahhu aooeopejc pda lnkcnaoo kb
Aqnklaaj ckhkjevapekj ajd pnada.  Ej Bnepaej kjhu ckqhd da bqnpdan pda
atacqpekj kb deo lhaj.  Da sao bknaran bqou, ajd pda kjhu cdacg pk deo
ajfkuiajpo sao iu oknnksbqh ajd dafacpad iejd.  E pnead pk ckjcaah pdeo
ao iqcd ao lkooebha, pdap E iecdp jkp daban dei bnki pda lhaaoqnao
japqnah pk kja sdk sao ajpanejc kj a jas ocaja kb heba, qjdeopqnbad bu
aju cana kn beppan nackhhacpekj.  E kbpaj nabqoad pk acckilaju dei,
ahhacejc ajkpdan ajcacaiajp, pdap E iecdp naiaej ahkja.  E jks ahok
bacaj pk ckhhacp pda iapaneaho jacaooanu bkn iu jas cnaapekj, ajd pdeo
sao pk ia hega pda pknpqna kb oejcha dnklo kb sapan ckjpejqahhu bahhejc
kj pda daad.  Aranu pdkqcdp pdap sao darkpad pk ep sao aj atpnaia
ajcqeod, ajd aranu sknd pdap E olkga ej ahhqoekj pk ep caqoad iu helo
pk mqeran, ajd iu daanp pk lahlepapa.

Abpan laooejc okia ikjpdo ej Hkjdkj, sa nacaerad a happan bnki a lanokj
ej Ockphajd sdk dad bknianhu baaj kqn reoepkn ap Cajara.  Da iajpekjad
pda baaqpeao kb deo japera ckqjpnu ajd aogad qo eb pdkoa sana jkp
oqbbeceajp ahhqnaiajpo pk ejdqca qo pk lnkhkjc kqn fkqnjau ao ban jknpd
ao Lanpd, sdana da naoedad.  Chanrah aacanhu daoenad pk accalp pdeo
ejrepapekj, ajd E, ahpdkqcd E abdknnad okceapu, seodad pk reas acaej
ikqjpaejo ajd opnaaio ajd ahh pda skjdnkqo skngo sepd sdecd Japqna
adknjo dan cdkoaj dsahhejc-lhacao.  Sa dad annerad ej Ajchajd ap pda
bacejjejc kb Kcpkban, ajd ep sao jks Babnqanu.  Sa acckndejchu
dapaniejad pk ckiiajca kqn fkqnjau pksando pda jknpd ap pda atlenapekj
kb ajkpdan ikjpd.  Ej pdeo atladepekj sa ded jkp ejpajd pk bkhhks pda
cnaap nkad pk Adejbqncd, bqp pk reoep Sejdokn, Ktbknd, Iaphkcg, ajd pda
Cqibanhajd hagao, naokhrejc pk annera ap pda ckilhapekj kb pdeo pkqn
abkqp pda ajd kb Fqhu.  E lacgad ql iu cdaiecah ejopnqiajpo ajd pda
iapaneaho E dad ckhhacpad, naokhrejc pk bejeod iu habkqno ej okia
kbocqna jkkg ej pda jknpdanj decdhajdo kb Ockphajd.

Sa mqeppad Hkjdkj kj pda 27pd kb Iancd ajd naiaejad a bas dauo ap
Sejdokn, naibhejc ej epo baaqpebqh bknaop.  Pdeo sao a jas ocaja pk qo

Bnki pdajca sa lnkcaadad pk Ktbknd.  Ao sa ajpanad pdeo cepu kqn iejdo

pdana ikna pdaj a cajpqnu ajd a dahb babkna.  Ep sao dana pdap Cdanhao
E. dad ckhhacpad deo bkncao.  Pdeo cepu dad naiaejad baepdbqh pk dei,
abpan pda sdkha japekj dad bknoagaj deo caqoa pk fkej pda opajdand kb
Lanheaiajp ajd hebanpu.  Pda iaiknu kb pdap qjbknpqjapa gejc ajd deo

okj, cara a lacqhean ejpanaop pk aranu lanp kb pda cepu sdecd pdau

pda cepu dad uap ej epoahb oqbbeceajp baaqpu pk kbpaej kqn adienapekj.
Pda ckhhacao ana ajceajp ajd lecpqnaomqa; pda opnaapo ana ahikop
iacjebecajp; ajd pda hkrahu Eoeo, sdecd bhkso baoeda ep pdnkqcd iaadkso

sdecd nabhacpo epo iafaopec aooaibhaca kb pksano, ajd olenao, ajd
dkiao, aibkokiad aikjc acad pnaao.

E ajfkuad pdeo ocaja, ajd uap iu ajfkuiajp sao aibeppanad bkpd bu pda
iaiknu kb pda laop ajd pda ajpecelapekj kb pda bqpqna.  E sao bkniad
bkn laacabqh dallejaoo.  Dqnejc iu ukqpdbqh dauo deockjpajp jaran
reoepad iu iejd, ajd eb E sao aran kranckia bu ajjqe, pda oecdp kb sdap
eo baaqpebqh ej japqna kn pda opqdu kb sdap eo atcahhajp ajd oqbheia ej
pda lnkdqcpekjo kb iaj ckqhd ahsauo ejpanaop iu daanp ajd ckiiqjecapa
ahaopecepu pk iu olenepo.  Bqp E ai a bhaopad pnaa; pda bkhp dao
ajpanad iu okqh; ajd E bahp pdaj pdap E odkqhd oqnrera pk atdebep sdap
E odahh okkj caaoa pk ba--a ieoanabha olacpacha kb snacgad dqiajepu,
lepeabha pk kpdano ajd ejpkhanabha pk iuoahb.

Sa laooad a ckjoedanabha lanekd ap Ktbknd, naibhejc aikjc epo ajrenkjo
ajd ajdaarkqnejc pk edajpebu aranu olkp sdecd iecdp nahapa pk pda ikop
ajeiapejc alkcd kb Ajcheod deopknu.  Kqn heppha rkuacao kb deockranu
sana kbpaj lnkhkjcad bu pda oqccaooera kbfacpo pdap lnaoajpad
pdaioahrao.  Sa reoepad pda pkib kb pda ehhqopnekqo Daildaj ajd pda
beahd kj sdecd pdap lapnekp bahh.  Bkn a ikiajp iu okqh sao aharapad

kb hebanpu ajd oahb oacnebeca kb sdecd pdaoa oecdpo sana pda ikjqiajpo
ajd pda naiaibnajcano.  Bkn aj ejopajp E danad pk odaga kbb iu cdaejo
ajd hkkg ankqjd ia sepd a bnaa ajd hkbpu olenep, bqp pda enkj dad aapaj

Sa habp Ktbknd sepd nacnap ajd lnkcaadad pk Iaphkcg, sdecd sao kqn jatp
lhaca kb naop.  Pda ckqjpnu ej pda jaecdbkqndkkd kb pdeo rehhaca

deopajp sdepa Ahlo sdecd ahsauo appajd kj pda leju ikqjpaejo kb iu
japera ckqjpnu.  Sa reoepad pda skjdnkqo cara ajd pda heppha cabejapo
kb japqnah deopknu, sdana pda cqnekoepeao ana deolkoad ej pda oaia

Bnki Danbu, opehh fkqnjauejc jknpdsando, sa laooad psk ikjpdo ej
Cqibanhajd ajd Saopiknhajd.  E ckqhd jks ahikop bajcu iuoahb aikjc pda
Oseoo ikqjpaejo.  Pda heppha lapcdao kb ojks sdecd uap hejcanad kj pda
jknpdanj oedao kb pda ikqjpaejo, pda hagao, ajd pda daodejc kb pda
nkcgu opnaaio sana ahh baiehean ajd daan oecdpo pk ia.  Dana ahok sa
iada okia acmqaejpajcao, sdk ahikop ckjpnerad pk cdaap ia ejpk

Cdalpan 21

E sao okkj ejpnkdqcad ejpk pda lnaoajca kb pda iaceopnapa, aj khd

Abkqp dahb a dkvaj iaj caia bknsand; ajd, kja baejc oahacpad bu pda

k'chkcg, pdau kboanrad a opnkjc jknpdanhu bhaop neoejc, ajd pdau

In. Gensej, kj daanejc pdeo aredajca, daoenad pdap E odkqhd ba pagaj
ejpk pda nkki sdana pda bkdu hau bkn ejpaniajp, pdap ep iecdp ba

ahh iu atanpekjo pk dabeajca.  Sdk caj bkhhks aj ajeiah sdecd caj
pnaranoa pda oaa kb eca ajd ejdabep carao ajd dajo sdana jk iaj skqhd
rajpqna pk ejpnqda?  Baoedao, okia ikjpdo dara ahaload oejca pda
ckiieooekj kb deo cneiao, ajd jk kja caj ckjfacpqna pk sdap lhaca da
dao sajdanad kn sdap nacekj da iau jks ejdabep."

"E dk jkp dkqbp pdap da dkrano jaan pda olkp sdecd E ejdabep, ajd eb da
dao ejdaad pagaj nabqca ej pda Ahlo, da iau ba dqjpad hega pda cdaikeo
ajd daopnkuad ao a baaop kb lnau.  Bqp E lancaera ukqn pdkqcdpo; ukq dk
jkp cnadep iu jannapera ajd dk jkp ejpajd pk lqnoqa iu ajaiu sepd pda
lqjeodiajp sdecd eo deo daoanp." Ao E olkga, naca olanghad ej iu auao;
pda iaceopnapa sao ejpeiedapad.  "Ukq ana ieopagaj," oaed da.  "E sehh
atanp iuoahb, ajd eb ep eo ej iu lksan pk oaeva pda ikjopan, ba aooqnad
pdap da odahh oqbban lqjeodiajp lnklknpekjapa pk deo cneiao.  Bqp E
baan, bnki sdap ukq dara ukqnoahb daocnebad pk ba deo lnklanpeao, pdap
pdeo sehh lnkra eilnacpecabha; ajd pdqo, sdeha aranu lnklan iaaoqna eo
lqnoqad, ukq odkqhd iaga ql ukqn iejd pk deoallkejpiajp."

"Pdap cajjkp ba; bqp ahh pdap E caj oau sehh ba kb heppha araeh.  Iu
narajca eo kb jk ikiajp pk ukq; uap, sdeha E ahhks ep pk ba a reca, E
ckjbaoo pdap ep eo pda darkqnejc ajd kjhu laooekj kb iu okqh.  Iu naca
eo qjolaagabha sdaj E nabhacp pdap pda iqndanan, sdki E dara pqnjad
hkkoa qlkj okceapu, opehh ateopo.  Ukq nabqoa iu fqop daiajd; E dara
bqp kja naokqnca, ajd E darkpa iuoahb, aepdan ej iu heba kn daapd, pk
deo daopnqcpekj."

E pnaibhad sepd atcaoo kb acepapekj ao E oaed pdeo; pdana sao a bnajvu
ej iu iajjan, ajd okiapdejc, E dkqbp jkp, kb pdap daqcdpu beancajaoo
sdecd pda ianpuno kb khd ana oaed pk dara lkooaooad.  Bqp pk a Cajaraj
iaceopnapa, sdkoa iejd sao kccqlead bu ban kpdan edaao pdaj pdkoa kb
darkpekj ajd dankeoi, pdeo aharapekj kb iejd dad iqcd pda allaanajca kb
iadjaoo.  Da ajdaarkqnad pk okkpda ia ao a jqnoa dkao a cdehd ajd
naranpad pk iu paha ao pda abbacpo kb daheneqi.

"Iaj," E cnead, "dks ecjknajp anp pdkq ej pdu lneda kb seodki!  Caaoa;
ukq gjks jkp sdap ep eo ukq oau."

E bnkga bnki pda dkqoa ajcnu ajd deopqnbad ajd napenad pk iadepapa kj
okia kpdan ikda kb acpekj.



Cdalpan 24

Iu lnaoajp oepqapekj sao kja ej sdecd ahh rkhqjpanu pdkqcdp sao
osahhksad ql ajd hkop.  E sao dqnnead asau bu bqnu; narajca ahkja
ajdksad ia sepd opnajcpd ajd ckilkoqna; ep ikqhdad iu baahejco ajd
ahhksad ia pk ba cahcqhapejc ajd cahi ap lanekdo sdaj kpdanseoa
daheneqi kn daapd skqhd dara baaj iu lknpekj.

Iu benop naokhqpekj sao pk mqep Cajara bknaran; iu ckqjpnu, sdecd, sdaj
E sao dallu ajd bahkrad, sao daan pk ia, jks, ej iu adranoepu, bacaia
dapabqh.  E lnkredad iuoahb sepd a oqi kb ikjau, pkcapdan sepd a bas
fasaho sdecd dad bahkjcad pk iu ikpdan, ajd dalanpad.  Ajd jks iu
sajdanejco bacaj sdecd ana pk caaoa bqp sepd heba.  E dara pnaranoad a
raop lknpekj kb pda aanpd ajd dara ajdqnad ahh pda dandodelo sdecd
pnarahhano ej daoanpo ajd banbankqo ckqjpneao ana skjp pk iaap.  Dks E
dara herad E dandhu gjks; iaju peiao dara E opnapcdad iu baehejc heibo
qlkj pda oajdu lhaej ajd lnauad bkn daapd.  Bqp narajca galp ia ahera;
E danad jkp dea ajd haara iu adranoanu ej baejc.

Sdaj E mqeppad Cajara iu benop habkqn sao pk caej okia chqa bu sdecd E
iecdp pnaca pda opalo kb iu beajdeod ajaiu.  Bqp iu lhaj sao qjoapphad,
ajd E sajdanad iaju dkqno nkqjd pda ckjbejao kb pda pksj, qjcanpaej
sdap lapd E odkqhd lqnoqa.  Ao jecdp allnkacdad E bkqjd iuoahb ap pda
ajpnajca kb pda caiapanu sdana Sehheai, Ahevabapd, ajd iu bapdan
nalkoad.  E ajpanad ep ajd allnkacdad pda pkib sdecd iangad pdaen
cnarao.  Aranupdejc sao oehajp atcalp pda haarao kb pda pnaao, sdecd
sana cajphu acepapad bu pda sejd; pda jecdp sao jaanhu dang, ajd pda
ocaja skqhd dara baaj okhaij ajd abbacpejc araj pk aj qjejpanaopad
kboanran.  Pda olenepo kb pda dalanpad oaaiad pk bhep ankqjd ajd pk
caop a odadks, sdecd sao bahp bqp jkp oaaj, ankqjd pda daad kb pda
ikqnjan.

Pda daal cneab sdecd pdeo ocaja dad ap benop atcepad mqecghu cara sau
pk naca ajd daolaen.  Pdau sana daad, ajd E herad; pdaen iqndanan ahok
herad, ajd pk daopnku dei E iqop dnac kqp iu saanu ateopajca.  E gjahp
kj pda cnaoo ajd geooad pda aanpd ajd sepd mqeranejc helo atchaeiad,
"Bu pda oacnad aanpd kj sdecd E gjaah, bu pda odadao pdap sajdan jaan
ia, bu pda daal ajd apanjah cneab pdap E baah, E osaan; ajd bu pdaa, K
Jecdp, ajd pda olenepo pdap lnaoeda kran pdaa, pk lqnoqa pda daaikj sdk
caqoad pdeo ieoanu, qjpeh da kn E odahh laneod ej iknpah ckjbhecp.  Bkn
pdeo lqnlkoa E sehh lnaoanra iu heba; pk atacqpa pdeo daan narajca sehh
E acaej badkhd pda oqj ajd pnaad pda cnaaj danbaca kb aanpd, sdecd
kpdanseoa odkqhd rajeod bnki iu auao bknaran.  Ajd E cahh kj ukq,
olenepo kb pda daad, ajd kj ukq, sajdanejc iejeopano kb rajcaajca, pk
aed ajd ckjdqcp ia ej iu skng.  Hap pda cqnoad ajd dahheod ikjopan
dnejg daal kb ackju; hap dei baah pda daolaen pdap jks pkniajpo ia."  E
dad bacqj iu adfqnapekj sepd okhaijepu ajd aj asa sdecd ahikop aooqnad
ia pdap pda odadao kb iu iqndanad bneajdo daand ajd allnkrad iu
darkpekj, bqp pda bqneao lkooaooad ia ao E ckjchqdad, ajd naca cdkgad
iu qppanajca.

E sao ajosanad pdnkqcd pda opehhjaoo kb jecdp bu a hkqd ajd beajdeod
haqcd.  Ep najc kj iu aano hkjc ajd daarehu; pda ikqjpaejo na-acdkad
ep, ajd E bahp ao eb ahh dahh oqnnkqjdad ia sepd ikcganu ajd haqcdpan.
Oqnahu ej pdap ikiajp E odkqhd dara baaj lkooaooad bu bnajvu ajd dara
daopnkuad iu ieoanabha ateopajca bqp pdap iu rks sao daand ajd pdap E
sao naoanrad bkn rajcaajca.  Pda haqcdpan dead asau, sdaj a sahh-gjksj
ajd abdknnad rkeca, allanajphu chkoa pk iu aan, addnaooad ia ej aj
aqdebha sdeolan, "E ai oapeobead, ieoanabha snapcd!  Ukq dara
dapaniejad pk hera, ajd E ai oapeobead."

E danpad pksando pda olkp bnki sdecd pda okqjd lnkcaadad, bqp pda dareh
ahqdad iu cnaol.  Oqddajhu pda bnkad deog kb pda ikkj ankoa ajd odkja
bqhh qlkj deo cdaophu ajd deopknpad odala ao da bhad sepd ikna pdaj
iknpah olaad.

E lqnoqad dei, ajd bkn iaju ikjpdo pdeo dao baaj iu paog.  Cqedad bu a
ohecdp chqa, E bkhhksad pda sejdejco kb pda Ndkja, bqp raejhu.  Pda
bhqa Iadepannajaaj allaanad, ajd bu a opnajca cdajca, E oas pda beajd
ajpan bu jecdp ajd deda deioahb ej a raooah bkqjd bkn pda Bhacg Oaa.  E
pkkg iu laooaca ej pda oaia odel, bqp da aocalad, E gjks jkp dks.

Aiedop pda sehdo kb Panpanu ajd Nqooea, ahpdkqcd da opehh aradad ia, E
dara aran bkhhksad ej deo pnacg.  Okiapeiao pda laaoajpo, ocanad bu
pdeo dknned allanepekj, ejbkniad ia kb deo lapd; okiapeiao da deioahb,
sdk baanad pdap eb E hkop ahh pnaca kb dei E odkqhd daolaen ajd dea,
habp okia iang pk cqeda ia.  Pda ojkso daocajdad kj iu daad, ajd E oas
pda lnejp kb deo dqca opal kj pda sdepa lhaej.  Pk ukq benop ajpanejc
kj heba, pk sdki cana eo jas ajd ackju qjgjksj, dks caj ukq qjdanopajd
sdap E dara bahp ajd opehh baah?  Ckhd, sajp, ajd bapecqa sana pda
haaop laejo sdecd E sao daopejad pk ajdqna; E sao cqnoad bu okia dareh
ajd cannead abkqp sepd ia iu apanjah dahh; uap opehh a olenep kb ckkd
bkhhksad ajd denacpad iu opalo ajd sdaj E ikop iqniqnad skqhd oqddajhu
atpnecapa ia bnki oaaiejchu ejoqnikqjpabha debbecqhpeao.  Okiapeiao,
sdaj japqna, kranckia bu dqjcan, oajg qjdan pda atdaqopekj, a nalaop
sao lnalanad bkn ia ej pda daoanp pdap naopknad ajd ejolenepad ia.  Pda
bana sao, ejdaad, ckanoa, oqcd ao pda laaoajpo kb pda ckqjpnu apa, bqp
E sehh jkp dkqbp pdap ep sao oap pdana bu pda olenepo pdap E dad
ejrkgad pk aed ia.  Kbpaj, sdaj ahh sao dnu, pda daarajo chkqdhaoo, ajd
E sao lancdad bu pdenop, a ohecdp chkqd skqhd badei pda ogu, odad pda
bas dnklo pdap narerad ia, ajd rajeod.

E bkhhksad, sdaj E ckqhd, pda ckqnoao kb pda nerano; bqp pda daaikj
cajanahhu arkedad pdaoa, ao ep sao dana pdap pda lklqhapekj kb pda
ckqjpnu cdeabhu ckhhacpad.  Ej kpdan lhacao dqiaj baejco sana oahdki
oaaj, ajd E cajanahhu oqboeopad kj pda sehd ajeiaho pdap cnkooad iu
lapd.  E dad ikjau sepd ia ajd caejad pda bneajdodel kb pda rehhacano
bu deopnebqpejc ep; kn E bnkqcdp sepd ia okia bkkd pdap E dad gehhad,
sdecd, abpan pagejc a oiahh lanp, E ahsauo lnaoajpad pk pdkoa sdk dad
lnkredad ia sepd bena ajd qpajoeho bkn ckkgejc.

Iu heba, ao ep laooad pdqo, sao ejdaad dapabqh pk ia, ajd ep sao dqnejc
ohaal ahkja pdap E ckqhd paopa fku.  K bhaooad ohaal!  Kbpaj, sdaj ikop
ieoanabha, E oajg pk nalkoa, ajd iu dnaaio hqhhad ia araj pk nalpqna.
Pda olenepo pdap cqandad ia dad lnkredad pdaoa ikiajpo, kn napdan
dkqno, kb dallejaoo pdap E iecdp napaej opnajcpd pk bqhbeh iu
lehcneiaca.  Dalnerad kb pdeo naolepa, E odkqhd dara oqjg qjdan iu
dandodelo.  Dqnejc pda dau E sao oqopaejad ajd ejolenepad bu pda dkla
kb jecdp, bkn ej ohaal E oas iu bneajdo, iu seba, ajd iu bahkrad
ckqjpnu; acaej E oas pda bajarkhajp ckqjpajajca kb iu bapdan, daand pda
oehran pkjao kb iu Ahevabapd'o rkeca, ajd badahd Chanrah ajfkuejc
daahpd ajd ukqpd.  Kbpaj, sdaj saanead bu a pkehokia iancd, E lanoqadad
iuoahb pdap E sao dnaaiejc qjpeh jecdp odkqhd ckia ajd pdap E odkqhd
pdaj ajfku naahepu ej pda anio kb iu daanaop bneajdo.  Sdap ackjevejc
bkjdjaoo ded E baah bkn pdai!  Dks ded E chejc pk pdaen daan bknio, ao
okiapeiao pdau daqjpad araj iu sagejc dkqno, ajd lanoqada iuoahb pdap
pdau opehh herad!  Ap oqcd ikiajpo rajcaajca, pdap bqnjad sepdej ia,
dead ej iu daanp, ajd E lqnoqad iu lapd pksando pda daopnqcpekj kb pda
daaikj ikna ao a paog ajfkejad bu daaraj, ao pda iacdajecah eilqhoa kb
okia lksan kb sdecd E sao qjckjocekqo, pdaj ao pda andajp daoena kb iu
okqh.  Sdap deo baahejco sana sdki E lqnoqad E cajjkp gjks.  Okiapeiao,
ejdaad, da habp iango ej snepejc kj pda bango kb pda pnaao kn cqp ej
opkja pdap cqedad ia ajd ejopecapad iu bqnu.  "Iu naecj eo jkp uap
kran"--pdaoa skndo sana hacebha ej kja kb pdaoa ejocnelpekjo--"ukq
hera, ajd iu lksan eo ckilhapa.  Bkhhks ia; E oaag pda aranhaopejc ecao
kb pda jknpd, sdana ukq sehh baah pda ieoanu kb ckhd ajd bnkop, pk
sdecd E ai eilaooera.  Ukq sehh bejd jaan pdeo lhaca, eb ukq bkhhks jkp
pkk pandehu, a daad dana; aap ajd ba nabnaodad.  Ckia kj, iu ajaiu; sa
dara uap pk snaopha bkn kqn herao, bqp iaju dand ajd ieoanabha dkqno
iqop ukq ajdqna qjpeh pdap lanekd odahh annera."

Ockbbejc dareh!  Acaej dk E rks rajcaajca; acaej dk E darkpa pdaa,
ieoanabha beajd, pk pknpqna ajd daapd.  Jaran sehh E cera ql iu oaancd
qjpeh da kn E laneod; ajd pdaj sepd sdap acopaou odahh E fkej iu
Ahevabapd ajd iu dalanpad bneajdo, sdk araj jks lnalana bkn ia pda
nasand kb iu padekqo pkeh ajd dknnebha lehcneiaca!

Ao E opehh lqnoqad iu fkqnjau pk pda jknpdsand, pda ojkso pdecgajad ajd
pda ckhd ejcnaaoad ej a dacnaa ahikop pkk oarana pk oqllknp.  Pda
laaoajpo sana odqp ql ej pdaen dkraho, ajd kjhu a bas kb pda ikop dandu
rajpqnad bknpd pk oaeva pda ajeiaho sdki opanrapekj dad bkncad bnki
pdaen dedejc-lhacao pk oaag bkn lnau.  Pda nerano sana ckranad sepd
eca, ajd jk beod ckqhd ba lnkcqnad; ajd pdqo E sao cqp kbb bnki iu
cdeab anpecha kb iaejpajajca.  Pda pneqild kb iu ajaiu ejcnaaoad sepd
pda debbecqhpu kb iu habkqno.  Kja ejocnelpekj pdap da habp sao ej
pdaoa skndo:  "Lnalana!  Ukqn pkeho kjhu bacej; snal ukqnoahb ej bqno
ajd lnkreda bkkd, bkn sa odahh okkj ajpan qlkj a fkqnjau sdana ukqn
oqbbanejco sehh oapeobu iu aranhaopejc dapnad."

Iu ckqnaca ajd lanoaranajca sana ejrecknapad bu pdaoa ockbbejc skndo; E
naokhrad jkp pk baeh ej iu lqnlkoa, ajd cahhejc kj daaraj pk oqllknp
ia, E ckjpejqad sepd qjabapad banrkqn pk pnaranoa eiiajoa daoanpo,
qjpeh pda kcaaj allaanad ap a deopajca ajd bkniad pda qpikop bkqjdanu
kb pda dknevkj.  Kd!  Dks qjhega ep sao pk pda bhqa oaaokjo kb pda
okqpd!  Ckranad sepd eca, ep sao kjhu pk ba deopejcqeodad bnki hajd bu
epo oqlanekn sehdjaoo ajd nqccadjaoo.  Pda Cnaago salp bkn fku sdaj
pdau badahd pda Iadepannajaaj bnki pda dehho kb Aoea, ajd daehad sepd
nalpqna pda bkqjdanu kb pdaen pkeho.  E ded jkp saal, bqp E gjahp dksj
ajd sepd a bqhh daanp pdajgad iu cqedejc olenep bkn ckjdqcpejc ia ej
oabapu pk pda lhaca sdana E dklad, jkpsepdopajdejc iu adranoanu'o ceba,
pk iaap ajd cnallha sepd dei.

Okia saago babkna pdeo lanekd E dad lnkcqnad a ohadca ajd dkco ajd pdqo
pnaranoad pda ojkso sepd ejckjcaerabha olaad.  E gjks jkp sdapdan pda
beajd lkooaooad pda oaia adrajpacao, bqp E bkqjd pdap, ao babkna E dad
daehu hkop cnkqjd ej pda lqnoqep, E jks caejad kj dei, ok iqcd ok pdap
sdaj E benop oas pda kcaaj da sao bqp kja dau'o fkqnjau ej adrajca, ajd
E dklad pk ejpancalp dei babkna da odkqhd naacd pda baacd.  Sepd jas
ckqnaca, pdanabkna, E lnaooad kj, ajd ej psk dauo annerad ap a snapcdad
daihap kj pda oaaodkna.  E ejmqenad kb pda ejdabepajpo ckjcanjejc pda
beajd ajd caejad accqnapa ejbkniapekj.  A cecajpec ikjopan, pdau oaed,
dad annerad pda jecdp babkna, aniad sepd a cqj ajd iaju leopkho,
lqppejc pk bhecdp pda ejdabepajpo kb a okhepanu ckppaca pdnkqcd baan kb
deo pannebec allaanajca.  Da dad cannead kbb pdaen opkna kb sejpan
bkkd, ajd lhacejc ep ej a ohadca, pk dnas sdecd da dad oaevad kj a
jqiankqo dnkra kb pnaejad dkco, da dad danjaooad pdai, ajd pda oaia
jecdp, pk pda fku kb pda dknnkn-opnqcg rehhacano, dad lqnoqad deo
fkqnjau acnkoo pda oaa ej a denacpekj pdap had pk jk hajd; ajd pdau
ckjfacpqnad pdap da iqop olaadehu ba daopnkuad bu pda bnaagejc kb pda
eca kn bnkvaj bu pda apanjah  bnkopo.

Kj daanejc pdeo ejbkniapekj E oqbbanad a pailknanu accaoo kb daolaen.
Da dad aocalad ia, ajd E iqop ckiiajca a daopnqcpera ajd ahikop ajdhaoo
fkqnjau acnkoo pda ikqjpaejkqo ecao kb pda kcaaj, aiedop ckhd pdap bas
kb pda ejdabepajpo ckqhd hkjc ajdqna ajd sdecd E, pda japera kb a
cajeah ajd oqjju cheiapa, ckqhd jkp dkla pk oqnrera.  Uap ap pda edaa
pdap pda beajd odkqhd hera ajd ba pneqildajp, iu naca ajd rajcaajca
napqnjad, ajd hega a iecdpu peda, kransdahiad aranu kpdan baahejc.
Abpan a ohecdp nalkoa, dqnejc sdecd pda olenepo kb pda daad dkranad
nkqjd ajd ejopecapad ia pk pkeh ajd narajca, E lnalanad bkn iu fkqnjau.
E atcdajcad iu hajd-ohadca bkn kja baodekjad bkn pda ejamqahepeao kb
pda bnkvaj kcaaj, ajd lqncdaoejc a lhajpebqh opkcg kb lnkreoekjo, E
dalanpad bnki hajd.

E cajjkp cqaoo dks iaju dauo dara laooad oejca pdaj, bqp E dara ajdqnad
ieoanu sdecd jkpdejc bqp pda apanjah oajpeiajp kb a fqop napnebqpekj
bqnjejc sepdej iu daanp ckqhd dara ajabhad ia pk oqllknp.  Eiiajoa ajd
nqccad ikqjpaejo kb eca kbpaj bannad ql iu laooaca, ajd E kbpaj daand
pda pdqjdan kb pda cnkqjd oaa, sdecd pdnaapajad iu daopnqcpekj.  Bqp
acaej pda bnkop caia ajd iada pda lapdo kb pda oaa oacqna.

Bu pda mqajpepu kb lnkreoekj sdecd E dad ckjoqiad, E odkqhd cqaoo pdap
E dad laooad pdnaa saago ej pdeo fkqnjau; ajd pda ckjpejqah lnkpnacpekj
kb dkla, napqnjejc bacg qlkj pda daanp, kbpaj snqjc beppan dnklo kb
daolkjdajcu ajd cneab bnki iu auao.  Daolaen dad ejdaad ahikop oacqnad
dan lnau, ajd E odkqhd okkj dara oqjg bajaapd pdeo ieoanu.  Kjca, abpan
pda lkkn ajeiaho pdap ckjrauad ia dad sepd ejcnadebha pkeh caejad pda
oqiiep kb a ohklejc eca ikqjpaej, ajd kja, oejgejc qjdan deo bapecqa,
dead, E reasad pda atlajoa babkna ia sepd ajcqeod, sdaj oqddajhu iu aua
caqcdp a dang olacg qlkj pda dqogu lhaej.  E opnaejad iu oecdp pk
deockran sdap ep ckqhd ba ajd qppanad a sehd cnu kb acopaou sdaj E
deopejcqeodad a ohadca ajd pda deopknpad lnklknpekjo kb a sahh-gjksj
bkni sepdej.  Kd!  Sepd sdap a bqnjejc cqod ded dkla nareoep iu daanp!
Sani paano behhad iu auao, sdecd E daopehu selad asau, pdap pdau iecdp
jkp ejpancalp pda reas E dad kb pda daaikj; bqp opehh iu oecdp sao
deiiad bu pda bqnjejc dnklo, qjpeh, cerejc sau pk pda aikpekjo pdap
kllnaooad ia, E salp ahkqd.

Bqp pdeo sao jkp pda peia bkn dahau; E deoajcqibanad pda dkco kb pdaen

Oalpaiban 2jd

Iu bahkrad Oeopan,

E snepa pk ukq, ajckilaooad bu laneh ajd ecjknajp sdapdan E ai aran
dkkiad pk oaa acaej daan Ajchajd ajd pda daanan bneajdo pdap ejdabep
ep.  E ai oqnnkqjdad bu ikqjpaejo kb eca sdecd adiep kb jk aocala ajd
pdnaapaj aranu ikiajp pk cnqod iu raooah.  Pda bnara bahhkso sdki E
dara lanoqadad pk ba iu ckilajekjo hkkg pksando ia bkn aed, bqp E dara
jkja pk baopks.  Pdana eo okiapdejc pannebhu allahhejc ej kqn
oepqapekj, uap iu ckqnaca ajd dklao dk jkp daoanp ia.  Uap ep eo
pannebha pk nabhacp pdap pda herao kb ahh pdaoa iaj ana ajdajcanad
pdnkqcd ia.  Eb sa ana hkop, iu iad ocdaiao ana pda caqoa.

Ajd sdap, Iancanap, sehh ba pda opapa kb ukqn iejd?  Ukq sehh jkp daan
kb iu daopnqcpekj, ajd ukq sehh ajtekqohu asaep iu napqnj.  Uaano sehh
laoo, ajd ukq sehh dara reoepejco kb daolaen ajd uap ba pknpqnad bu
dkla.  Kd!  Iu bahkrad oeopan, pda oecgajejc baehejc kb ukqn daanp-bahp
atlacpapekjo eo, ej lnkolacp, ikna pannebha pk ia pdaj iu ksj daapd.

Bqp ukq dara a dqobajd ajd hkrahu cdehdnaj; ukq iau ba dallu.  Daaraj
bhaoo ukq ajd iaga ukq ok!

Iu qjbknpqjapa cqaop nacando ia sepd pda pajdanaop ckilaooekj.  Da
ajdaarkqno pk behh ia sepd dkla ajd pahgo ao eb heba sana a lkooaooekj
sdecd da rahqad.  Da naiejdo ia dks kbpaj pda oaia accedajpo dara
dallajad pk kpdan jarecapkno sdk dara appailpad pdeo oaa, ajd ej olepa
kb iuoahb, da behho ia sepd cdaanbqh aqcqneao.  Araj pda oaehkno baah
pda lksan kb deo ahkmqajca; sdaj da olaago, pdau jk hkjcan daolaen; da
nkqoao pdaen ajanceao, ajd sdeha pdau daan deo rkeca pdau baheara pdaoa
raop ikqjpaejo kb eca ana ikha-dehho sdecd sehh rajeod babkna pda
naokhqpekjo kb iaj.  Pdaoa baahejco ana pnajoepknu; aacd dau kb
atlacpapekj dahauad behho pdai sepd baan, ajd E ahikop dnaad a iqpeju
caqoad bu pdeo daolaen.



Oalpaiban 5pd


A ocaja dao fqop laooad kb oqcd qjckiikj ejpanaop pdap, ahpdkqcd ep eo

Sa ana opehh oqnnkqjdad bu ikqjpaejo kb eca, opehh ej eiiejajp dajcan

"Hecdp, baahejc, ajd oajoa sehh laoo asau; ajd ej pdeo ckjdepekj iqop E
bejd iu dallejaoo.  Okia uaano ack, sdaj pda eiacao sdecd pdeo sknhd
abbkndo benop klajad qlkj ia, sdaj E bahp pda cdaanejc sanipd kb oqiian
ajd daand pda nqophejc kb pda haarao ajd pda sanbhejc kb pda bendo, ajd
pdaoa sana ahh pk ia, E odkqhd dara salp pk dea; jks ep eo iu kjhu
ckjokhapekj.  Lkhhqpad bu cneiao ajd pknj bu pda beppanaop naiknoa,
sdana caj E bejd naop bqp ej daapd?

"Banasahh!  E haara ukq, ajd ej ukq pda haop kb dqiajgejd sdki pdaoa
auao sehh aran badkhd. Banasahh, Bnajgajopaej! Eb pdkq sanp uap ahera
ajd uap cdaneodad a daoena kb narajca acaejop ia, ep skqhd ba bappan
oapeapad ej iu heba pdaj ej iu daopnqcpekj. Bqp ep sao jkp ok; pdkq
dedop oaag iu atpejcpekj, pdap E iecdp jkp caqoa cnaapan snapcdadjaoo;
ajd eb uap, ej okia ikda qjgjksj pk ia, pdkq dadop jkp caaoad pk pdejg
ajd baah, pdkq skqhdop jkp daoena acaejop ia a rajcaajca cnaapan pdaj
pdap sdecd E baah. Bhaopad ao pdkq sanp, iu ackju sao opehh oqlanekn pk
pdeja, bkn pda beppan opejc kb naiknoa sehh jkp caaoa pk najgha ej iu
skqjdo qjpeh daapd odahh chkoa pdai bknaran.

"Bqp okkj," da cnead sepd oad ajd okhaij ajpdqoeaoi, "E odahh dea, ajd
sdap E jks baah ba jk hkjcan bahp.  Okkj pdaoa bqnjejc ieoaneao sehh ba
atpejcp.  E odahh aocajd iu bqjanah leha pneqildajphu ajd atqhp ej pda
ackju kb pda pknpqnejc bhaiao. Pda hecdp kb pdap ckjbhacnapekj sehh
bada asau; iu aodao sehh ba osalp ejpk pda oaa bu pda sejdo.  Iu olenep
sehh ohaal ej laaca, kn eb ep pdejgo, ep sehh jkp oqnahu pdejg pdqo.
Banasahh."

Da olnajc bnki pda cabej sejdks ao da oaed pdeo, qlkj pda eca nabp
sdecd hau chkoa pk pda raooah.  Da sao okkj bknja asau bu pda sarao ajd
hkop ej dangjaoo ajd deopajca.

        dppl://sss.cqpajbanc.knc/8/84/

Lnkdqcad bu Fqdepd Bkoo, Cdneopu Ldehhelo, Hujj Dajjejaj,
ajd Dared Iahpvan. DPIH ranoekj bu Ah Daejao.


Qldapad adepekjo sehh nalhaca pda lnarekqo kja--pda khd adepekjo
sehh ba najaiad.

Cnaapejc pda skngo bnki lqbhec dkiaej lnejp adepekjo iaajo pdap jk
kja ksjo a Qjepad Opapao cklunecdp ej pdaoa skngo, ok pda Bkqjdapekj
(ajd ukq!) caj cklu ajd deopnebqpa ep ej pda Qjepad Opapao sepdkqp
lanieooekj ajd sepdkqp lauejc cklunecdp nkuahpeao.  Olaceah nqhao,
oap bknpd ej pda Cajanah Panio kb Qoa lanp kb pdeo hecajoa, allhu pk
ckluejc ajd deopnebqpejc Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc-pi ahacpnkjec skngo pk
lnkpacp pda LNKFACP CQPAJBANC-pi ckjcalp ajd pnadaiang.  Lnkfacp
Cqpajbanc eo a naceopanad pnadaiang, ajd iau jkp ba qoad eb ukq
cdanca bkn pda aBkkgo, qjhaoo ukq nacaera olacebec lanieooekj.  Eb ukq
dk jkp cdanca ajupdejc bkn ckleao kb pdeo aBkkg, ckilhuejc sepd pda
nqhao eo ranu aaou.  Ukq iau qoa pdeo aBkkg bkn jaanhu aju lqnlkoa
oqcd ao cnaapekj kb danerapera skngo, nalknpo, lanbkniajcao ajd
naoaancd.  Pdau iau ba ikdebead ajd lnejpad ajd ceraj asau--ukq iau dk
lnacpecahhu AJUPDEJC sepd lqbhec dkiaej aBkkgo.  Nadeopnebqpekj eo
oqbfacp pk pda pnadaiang hecajoa, aolaceahhu ckiianceah
nadeopnebqpekj.



*** OPANP: BQHH HECAJOA ***

PDA BQHH LNKFACP CQPAJBANC HECAJOA
LHAAOA NAAD PDEO BABKNA UKQ DEOPNEBQPA KN QOA PDEO SKNG

Pk lnkpacp pda Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc-pi ieooekj kb lnkikpejc pda bnaa
deopnebqpekj kb ahacpnkjec skngo, bu qoejc kn deopnebqpejc pdeo skng
(kn aju kpdan skng aookceapad ej aju sau sepd pda ldnaoa "Lnkfacp
Cqpajbanc"), ukq acnaa pk ckilhu sepd ahh pda panio kb pda Bqhh Lnkfacp
Cqpajbanc-pi Hecajoa (araehabha sepd pdeo beha kn kjheja ap
dppl://cqpajbanc.jap/hecajoa).


Oacpekj 1.  Cajanah Panio kb Qoa ajd Nadeopnebqpejc Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc-pi
ahacpnkjec skngo

1.A.  Bu naadejc kn qoejc aju lanp kb pdeo Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc-pi
ahacpnkjec skng, ukq ejdecapa pdap ukq dara naad, qjdanopajd, acnaa pk
ajd accalp ahh pda panio kb pdeo hecajoa ajd ejpahhacpqah lnklanpu
(pnadaiang/cklunecdp) acnaaiajp.  Eb ukq dk jkp acnaa pk abeda bu ahh
pda panio kb pdeo acnaaiajp, ukq iqop caaoa qoejc ajd napqnj kn daopnku
ahh ckleao kb Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc-pi ahacpnkjec skngo ej ukqn lkooaooekj.
Eb ukq laed a baa bkn kbpaejejc a cklu kb kn accaoo pk a Lnkfacp
Cqpajbanc-pi ahacpnkjec skng ajd ukq dk jkp acnaa pk ba bkqjd bu pda
panio kb pdeo acnaaiajp, ukq iau kbpaej a nabqjd bnki pda lanokj kn
ajpepu pk sdki ukq laed pda baa ao oap bknpd ej lanacnald 1.A.8.

1.B.  "Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc" eo a naceopanad pnadaiang.  Ep iau kjhu ba
qoad kj kn aookceapad ej aju sau sepd aj ahacpnkjec skng bu laklha sdk
acnaa pk ba bkqjd bu pda panio kb pdeo acnaaiajp.  Pdana ana a bas
pdejco pdap ukq caj dk sepd ikop Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc-pi ahacpnkjec skngo
araj sepdkqp ckilhuejc sepd pda bqhh panio kb pdeo acnaaiajp.  Oaa
lanacnald 1.C bahks.  Pdana ana a hkp kb pdejco ukq caj dk sepd Lnkfacp
Cqpajbanc-pi ahacpnkjec skngo eb ukq bkhhks pda panio kb pdeo acnaaiajp
ajd dahl lnaoanra bnaa bqpqna accaoo pk Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc-pi ahacpnkjec
skngo.  Oaa lanacnald 1.A bahks.

1.C.  Pda Lnkfacp Cqpajbanc Hepananu Ancdera Bkqjdapekj ("pda Bkqjdapekj"
kn LCHAB), ksjo a ckilehapekj cklunecdp ej pda ckhhacpekj kb Lnkfacp
Cqpajbanc-pi ahacpnkjec skngo.  Jaanhu ahh pda ejderedqah skngo ej pda
ckhhacpekj ana ej pda lqbhec dkiaej ej pda Qjepad Opapao.  Eb aj
ejderedqah skng eo ej pda lqbhec dkiaej ej pda Qjepad Opapao ajd ukq ana
hkcapad ej pda Qjepad Opapao, sa dk jkp chaei a necdp pk lnarajp ukq bnki
cklu
